00092 /* On VMware ESX there is a possibility that that netdev watchdog thread
00093  * runs before the reset task if the machine is loaded.  If this occurs
00094  * too many times, these premature watchdog triggers will cause a PSOD
00095  * on a VMware ESX beta build */ 
00096 #define TX_TIMEOUT  (20*HZ)
00097 #else
00098 #define TX_TIMEOUT  (5*HZ)

00354 #ifdef BNX2_BOOT_DISK
00355 u32 ether_crc_le(size_t len, unsigned char const *p)
00356 {
00357     u32 crc = ~0;
00358     int i;
00359 #define CRCPOLY_LE 0xedb88320
00360 
00361     while (len--) {
00362         crc ^= *p++;
00363         for (i = 0; i < 8; i++)
00364             crc = (crc >> 1) ^ ((crc & 1) ? CRCPOLY_LE : 0);
00365     }
00366     return crc;
00367 }
00368 #endif
00369 
00370 static inline u32 bnx2_tx_avail(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr)
00371 {
00372     u32 diff;
00373 
00374     smp_mb();
00375 
00376     /* The ring uses 256 indices for 255 entries, one of them
00377      * needs to be skipped.
00378      */
00379     diff = txr->tx_prod - txr->tx_cons;
00380     if (unlikely(diff >= TX_DESC_CNT)) {
00381         diff &= 0xffff;
00382         if (diff == TX_DESC_CNT)
00383             diff = MAX_TX_DESC_CNT;
00384     }
00385     return (bp->tx_ring_size - diff);
00386 }
00387 
00388 static u32
00389 bnx2_reg_rd_ind(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset)
00390 {
00391     u32 val;
00392 
00393     spin_lock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00394     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW_ADDRESS, offset);
00395     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW);
00396     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00397     return val;
00398 }
00399 
00400 static void
00401 bnx2_reg_wr_ind(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u32 val)
00402 {
00403     spin_lock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00404     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW_ADDRESS, offset);
00405     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW, val);
00406     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00407 }
00408 
00409 static void
00410 bnx2_shmem_wr(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u32 val)
00411 {
00412     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, bp->shmem_base + offset, val);
00413 }
00414 
00415 static u32
00416 bnx2_shmem_rd(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset)
00417 {
00418     return (bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, bp->shmem_base + offset));
00419 }
00420 
00421 static void
00422 bnx2_ctx_wr(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 cid_addr, u32 offset, u32 val)
00423 {
00424     offset += cid_addr;
00425     spin_lock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00426     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
00427         int i;
00428 
00429         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_DATA, val);
00430         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL,
00431                offset | BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL_WRITE_REQ);
00432         for (i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
00433             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL);
00434             if ((val & BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL_WRITE_REQ) == 0)
00435                 break;
00436             udelay(5);
00437         }
00438     } else {
00439         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_DATA_ADR, offset);
00440         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_DATA, val);
00441     }
00442     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->indirect_lock);
00443 }
00444 
00445 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
00446 static int
00447 bnx2_drv_ctl(struct net_device *dev, struct drv_ctl_info *info)
00448 {
00449     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
00450     struct drv_ctl_io *io = &info->data.io;
00451 
00452     switch (info->cmd) {
00453     case DRV_CTL_IO_WR_CMD:
00454         bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, io->offset, io->data);
00455         break;
00456     case DRV_CTL_IO_RD_CMD:
00457         io->data = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, io->offset);
00458         break;
00459     case DRV_CTL_CTX_WR_CMD:
00460         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, io->cid_addr, io->offset, io->data);
00461         break;
00462     default:
00463         return -EINVAL;
00464     }
00465     return 0;
00466 }
00467 
00468 static void bnx2_setup_cnic_irq_info(struct bnx2 *bp)
00469 {
00470     struct cnic_eth_dev *cp = &bp->cnic_eth_dev;
00471     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
00472     int sb_id;
00473 
00474     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX) {
00475         cp->drv_state |= CNIC_DRV_STATE_USING_MSIX;
00476         bnapi->cnic_present = 0;
00477         sb_id = bp->irq_nvecs;
00478         cp->irq_arr[0].irq_flags |= CNIC_IRQ_FL_MSIX;
00479     } else {
00480         cp->drv_state &= ~CNIC_DRV_STATE_USING_MSIX;
00481         bnapi->cnic_tag = bnapi->last_status_idx;
00482         bnapi->cnic_present = 1;
00483         sb_id = 0;
00484         cp->irq_arr[0].irq_flags &= ~CNIC_IRQ_FL_MSIX;
00485     }
00486 
00487     cp->irq_arr[0].vector = bp->irq_tbl[sb_id].vector;
00488     cp->irq_arr[0].status_blk = (void *)
00489         ((unsigned long) bnapi->status_blk.msi +
00490         (BNX2_SBLK_MSIX_ALIGN_SIZE * sb_id));
00491     cp->irq_arr[0].status_blk_num = sb_id;
00492     cp->num_irq = 1;
00493 }
00494 
00495 static int bnx2_register_cnic(struct net_device *dev, struct cnic_ops *ops,
00496                   void *data)
00497 {
00498     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
00499     struct cnic_eth_dev *cp = &bp->cnic_eth_dev;
00500 
00501     if (ops == NULL)
00502         return -EINVAL;
00503 
00504     if (cp->drv_state & CNIC_DRV_STATE_REGD)
00505         return -EBUSY;
00506 
00507     bp->cnic_data = data;
00508     rcu_assign_pointer(bp->cnic_ops, ops);
00509 
00510     cp->num_irq = 0;
00511     cp->drv_state = CNIC_DRV_STATE_REGD;
00512 
00513     bnx2_setup_cnic_irq_info(bp);
00514 
00515     return 0;
00516 }
00517 
00518 static int bnx2_unregister_cnic(struct net_device *dev)
00519 {
00520     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
00521     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
00522     struct cnic_eth_dev *cp = &bp->cnic_eth_dev;
00523 
00524     mutex_lock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00525     cp->drv_state = 0;
00526     bnapi->cnic_present = 0;
00527     rcu_assign_pointer(bp->cnic_ops, NULL);
00528     mutex_unlock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00529     synchronize_rcu();
00530     return 0;
00531 }
00532 
00533 struct cnic_eth_dev *bnx2_cnic_probe(struct net_device *dev)
00534 {
00535     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
00536     struct cnic_eth_dev *cp = &bp->cnic_eth_dev;
00537 
00538     cp->drv_owner = THIS_MODULE;
00539     cp->chip_id = bp->chip_id;
00540     cp->pdev = bp->pdev;
00541     cp->io_base = bp->regview;
00542     cp->drv_ctl = bnx2_drv_ctl;
00543     cp->drv_register_cnic = bnx2_register_cnic;
00544     cp->drv_unregister_cnic = bnx2_unregister_cnic;
00545 
00546     return cp;
00547 }
00548 EXPORT_SYMBOL(bnx2_cnic_probe);

00551 bnx2_cnic_stop(struct bnx2 *bp)
00552 {
00553     struct cnic_ops *c_ops;
00554     struct cnic_ctl_info info;
00555 
00556     mutex_lock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00557     c_ops = bp->cnic_ops;
00558     if (c_ops) {
00559         info.cmd = CNIC_CTL_STOP_CMD;
00560         c_ops->cnic_ctl(bp->cnic_data, &info);
00561     }
00562     mutex_unlock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00563 }

00565 static void
00566 bnx2_cnic_start(struct bnx2 *bp)
00567 {
00568     struct cnic_ops *c_ops;
00569     struct cnic_ctl_info info;
00570 
00571     mutex_lock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00572     c_ops = bp->cnic_ops;
00573     if (c_ops) {
00574         if (!(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)) {
00575             struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
00576

00578         }
00579         info.cmd = CNIC_CTL_START_CMD;
00580         c_ops->cnic_ctl(bp->cnic_data, &info);
00581     }
00582     mutex_unlock(&bp->cnic_lock);
00583 }

00598 
00599 static int
00600 bnx2_read_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 reg, u32 *val)
00601 {
00602     u32 val1;
00603     int i, ret;
00604 
00605     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_AUTO_POLLING) {
00606         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00607         val1 &= ~BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL;
00608 
00609         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, val1);
00610         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00611 
00612         udelay(40);
00613     }
00614 
00615     val1 = (bp->phy_addr << 21) | (reg << 16) |
00616         BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_READ | BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_DISEXT |
00617         BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY;
00618     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, val1);
00619 
00620     for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
00621         udelay(10);
00622 
00623         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
00624         if (!(val1 & BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
00625             udelay(5);
00626 
00627             val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
00628             val1 &= BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_DATA;
00629 
00630             break;
00631         }
00632     }
00633 
00634     if (val1 & BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY) {
00635         *val = 0x0;
00636         ret = -EBUSY;
00637     }
00638     else {
00639         *val = val1;
00640         ret = 0;
00641     }
00642 
00643     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_AUTO_POLLING) {
00644         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00645         val1 |= BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL;
00646 
00647         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, val1);
00648         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00649 
00650         udelay(40);
00651     }
00652 
00653     return ret;
00654 }
00655 
00656 static int
00657 bnx2_write_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 reg, u32 val)
00658 {
00659     u32 val1;
00660     int i, ret;
00661 
00662     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_AUTO_POLLING) {
00663         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00664         val1 &= ~BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL;
00665 
00666         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, val1);
00667         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00668 
00669         udelay(40);
00670     }
00671 
00672     val1 = (bp->phy_addr << 21) | (reg << 16) | val |
00673         BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_COMMAND_WRITE |
00674         BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY | BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_DISEXT;
00675     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM, val1);
00676 
00677     for (i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
00678         udelay(10);
00679 
00680         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM);
00681         if (!(val1 & BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)) {
00682             udelay(5);
00683             break;
00684         }
00685     }
00686 
00687     if (val1 & BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_COMM_START_BUSY)
00688             ret = -EBUSY;
00689     else
00690         ret = 0;
00691 
00692     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_AUTO_POLLING) {
00693         val1 = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00694         val1 |= BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE_AUTO_POLL;
00695 
00696         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE, val1);
00697         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MDIO_MODE);
00698 
00699         udelay(40);
00700     }
00701 
00702     return ret;
00703 }
00704 
00705 static void
00706 bnx2_disable_int(struct bnx2 *bp)
00707 {
00708     int i;
00709     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
00710 
00711     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
00712         bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00713         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD, bnapi->int_num |
00714                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT);
00715     }
00716     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD);
00717 }
00718 
00719 static void
00720 bnx2_enable_int(struct bnx2 *bp)
00721 {
00722     int i;
00723     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
00724 
00725     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
00726         bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00727 
00728         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD, bnapi->int_num |
00729                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
00730                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT |
00731                bnapi->last_status_idx);
00732 
00733         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD, bnapi->int_num |
00734                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
00735                bnapi->last_status_idx);
00736     }
00737     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND, bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW);
00738 }
00739 
00740 static void
00741 bnx2_disable_int_sync(struct bnx2 *bp)
00742 {
00743     int i;
00744 
00745     atomic_inc(&bp->intr_sem);
00746     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
00747         return;
00748 
00749     bnx2_disable_int(bp);
00750     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++)
00751 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x2051c)
00752         synchronize_irq(bp->irq_tbl[i].vector);
00753 #else
00754         synchronize_irq();
00755 #endif
00756 }
00757 
00758 static void
00759 bnx2_napi_disable(struct bnx2 *bp)
00760 {
00761 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
00762     int i;
00763 
00764     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++)
00765         napi_disable(&bp->bnx2_napi[i].napi);
00766 #else
00767     netif_poll_disable(bp->dev);
00768 #endif
00769 }
00770 
00771 static void
00772 bnx2_napi_enable(struct bnx2 *bp)
00773 {
00774 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
00775     int i;
00776 
00777     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++)
00778         napi_enable(&bp->bnx2_napi[i].napi);
00779 #else
00780     netif_poll_enable(bp->dev);
00781 #endif
00782 }
00783 
00784 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
00785 static void
00786 bnx2_netqueue_tx_flush_queue(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi,
00787                  struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr)
00788 {
00789     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;    
00790 
00791     rmb();
00792     if ((bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi) != txr->hw_tx_cons) ||
00793         (bnapi->tx_packets_sent != bnapi->tx_packets_processed)) {
00794         bnx2_tx_int(bp, bnapi, 100, 0);
00795         msleep(1);
00796 
00797         rmb();
00798     }
00799 }
00800 
00801 
00802 static void
00803 bnx2_netqueue_tx_flush(struct bnx2 *bp)
00804 {
00805     int i;
00806     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
00807         struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr;
00808 
00809     /*  Flush default ring */
00810     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
00811     txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
00812 
00813     bnx2_netqueue_tx_flush_queue(bnapi, txr);
00814     printk(KERN_ALERT PFX "%s: flushed default TX queue\n",
00815          bp->dev->name);
00816 
00817     /*  Flush NetQ rings */
00818     for_each_nondefault_tx_queue(bp, i) {
00819         bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00820         txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
00821 
00822         rmb();
00823 
00824         bnx2_netqueue_tx_flush_queue(bnapi, txr);
00825         printk(KERN_ALERT PFX "%s: flushed TX queue %d\n",
00826                bp->dev->name, i);
00827     }
00828 }
00829 
00830 static void
00831 bnx2_netif_stop(struct bnx2 *bp)
00832 {
00833     bnx2_cnic_stop(bp);
00834     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
00835         netif_tx_disable(bp->dev);
00836         bp->dev->trans_start = jiffies; /* prevent tx timeout */
00837     }
00838 
00839     bnx2_disable_int_sync(bp);
00840 
00841     /*  Give some settling time */
00842     msleep(250);
00843 
00844     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
00845         bnx2_napi_disable(bp);
00846     }
00847 
00848     rmb();
00849 
00850     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
00851         bnx2_netqueue_tx_flush(bp);
00852     }
00853 }
00854 
00855 #else
00856 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE <= 0x2061e)
00857 
00858 static void
00859 bnx2_netif_stop(struct bnx2 *bp)
00860 {
00861     bnx2_cnic_stop(bp);
00862     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
00863         bnx2_napi_disable(bp);
00864         netif_tx_disable(bp->dev);
00865         bp->dev->trans_start = jiffies; /* prevent tx timeout */
00866     }
00867     bnx2_disable_int_sync(bp);
00868 }
00869 
00870 #else
00871 
00872 static void
00873 bnx2_netif_stop(struct bnx2 *bp)
00874 {
00875     bnx2_cnic_stop(bp);
00876     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
00877         int i;
00878 
00879         bnx2_napi_disable(bp);
00880         netif_tx_disable(bp->dev);
00881         /* prevent tx timeout */
00882         for (i = 0; i < bp->dev->num_tx_queues; i++) {
00883             struct netdev_queue *txq;
00884 
00885             txq = netdev_get_tx_queue(bp->dev, i);
00886             txq->trans_start = jiffies;
00887         }
00888     }
00889     bnx2_disable_int_sync(bp);
00890 }
00891 #endif
00892 #endif
00893 
00894 static void
00895 bnx2_netif_start(struct bnx2 *bp)
00896 {
00897     if (atomic_dec_and_test(&bp->intr_sem)) {
00898         if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
00899             netif_tx_wake_all_queues(bp->dev);
00900             bnx2_napi_enable(bp);
00901             bnx2_enable_int(bp);
00902             bnx2_cnic_start(bp);
00903         }
00904     }
00905 }
00906 
00907 static void
00908 bnx2_free_tx_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
00909 {
00910     int i;
00911 
00912     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_tx_rings; i++) {
00913         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00914         struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
00915 
00916         if (txr->tx_desc_ring) {
00917             pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, TXBD_RING_SIZE,
00918                         txr->tx_desc_ring,
00919                         txr->tx_desc_mapping);
00920             txr->tx_desc_ring = NULL;
00921         }
00922         kfree(txr->tx_buf_ring);
00923         txr->tx_buf_ring = NULL;
00924     }
00925 }
00926 
00927 static void
00928 bnx2_free_rx_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
00929 {
00930     int i;
00931 
00932     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_rx_rings; i++) {
00933         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00934         struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
00935         int j;
00936 
00937         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_ring; j++) {
00938             if (rxr->rx_desc_ring[j])
00939                 pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, RXBD_RING_SIZE,
00940                             rxr->rx_desc_ring[j],
00941                             rxr->rx_desc_mapping[j]);
00942             rxr->rx_desc_ring[j] = NULL;
00943         }
00944         vfree(rxr->rx_buf_ring);
00945         rxr->rx_buf_ring = NULL;
00946 
00947         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_pg_ring; j++) {
00948             if (rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[j])
00949                 pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, RXBD_RING_SIZE,
00950                             rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[j],
00951                             rxr->rx_pg_desc_mapping[j]);
00952             rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[j] = NULL;
00953         }
00954         vfree(rxr->rx_pg_ring);
00955         rxr->rx_pg_ring = NULL;
00956     }
00957 }
00958 
00959 static int
00960 bnx2_alloc_tx_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
00961 {
00962     int i;
00963 
00964     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_tx_rings; i++) {
00965         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00966         struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
00967 
00968         txr->tx_buf_ring = kmalloc(SW_TXBD_RING_SIZE, GFP_KERNEL);
00969         if (txr->tx_buf_ring == NULL)
00970             return -ENOMEM;
00971 
00972         memset(txr->tx_buf_ring, 0, SW_TXBD_RING_SIZE);
00973         txr->tx_desc_ring =
00974             pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev, TXBD_RING_SIZE,
00975                          &txr->tx_desc_mapping);
00976         if (txr->tx_desc_ring == NULL)
00977             return -ENOMEM;
00978     }
00979     return 0;
00980 }
00981 
00982 static int
00983 bnx2_alloc_rx_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
00984 {
00985     int i;
00986 
00987     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_rx_rings; i++) {
00988         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
00989         struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
00990         int j;
00991 
00992         rxr->rx_buf_ring =
00993             vmalloc(SW_RXBD_RING_SIZE * bp->rx_max_ring);
00994         if (rxr->rx_buf_ring == NULL)
00995             return -ENOMEM;
00996 
00997         memset(rxr->rx_buf_ring, 0,
00998                SW_RXBD_RING_SIZE * bp->rx_max_ring);
00999 
01000         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_ring; j++) {
01001             rxr->rx_desc_ring[j] =
01002                 pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev, RXBD_RING_SIZE,
01003                              &rxr->rx_desc_mapping[j]);
01004             if (rxr->rx_desc_ring[j] == NULL)
01005                 return -ENOMEM;
01006 
01007         }
01008 
01009         if (bp->rx_pg_ring_size) {
01010             rxr->rx_pg_ring = vmalloc(SW_RXPG_RING_SIZE *
01011                           bp->rx_max_pg_ring);
01012             if (rxr->rx_pg_ring == NULL)
01013                 return -ENOMEM;
01014 
01015             memset(rxr->rx_pg_ring, 0, SW_RXPG_RING_SIZE *
01016                    bp->rx_max_pg_ring);
01017         }
01018 
01019         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_pg_ring; j++) {
01020             rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[j] =
01021                 pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev, RXBD_RING_SIZE,
01022                         &rxr->rx_pg_desc_mapping[j]);
01023             if (rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[j] == NULL)
01024                 return -ENOMEM;
01025 
01026         }
01027     }
01028     return 0;
01029 }
01030 
01031 static void
01032 bnx2_free_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
01033 {
01034     int i;
01035     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
01036 
01037     bnx2_free_tx_mem(bp);
01038     bnx2_free_rx_mem(bp);
01039 
01040     for (i = 0; i < bp->ctx_pages; i++) {
01041         if (bp->ctx_blk[i]) {
01042             pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, BCM_PAGE_SIZE,
01043                         bp->ctx_blk[i],
01044                         bp->ctx_blk_mapping[i]);
01045             bp->ctx_blk[i] = NULL;
01046         }
01047     }
01048     if (bnapi->status_blk.msi) {
01049         pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, bp->status_stats_size,
01050                     bnapi->status_blk.msi,
01051                     bp->status_blk_mapping);
01052         bnapi->status_blk.msi = NULL;
01053         bp->stats_blk = NULL;
01054     }
01055 }
01056 
01057 static int
01058 bnx2_alloc_mem(struct bnx2 *bp)
01059 {
01060     int i, status_blk_size, err;
01061     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
01062     void *status_blk;
01063 
01064     /* Combine status and statistics blocks into one allocation. */
01065     status_blk_size = L1_CACHE_ALIGN(sizeof(struct status_block));
01066 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
01067     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_MSIX_CAP)
01068         status_blk_size = L1_CACHE_ALIGN(BNX2_MAX_MSIX_HW_VEC *
01069                          BNX2_SBLK_MSIX_ALIGN_SIZE);
01070 #endif
01071     bp->status_stats_size = status_blk_size +
01072                 sizeof(struct statistics_block);
01073 
01074     status_blk = pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev, bp->status_stats_size,
01075                       &bp->status_blk_mapping);
01076     if (status_blk == NULL)
01077         goto alloc_mem_err;
01078 
01079     memset(status_blk, 0, bp->status_stats_size);
01080 
01081     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
01082     bnapi->status_blk.msi = status_blk;
01083     bnapi->hw_tx_cons_ptr =
01084         &bnapi->status_blk.msi->status_tx_quick_consumer_index0;
01085     bnapi->hw_rx_cons_ptr =
01086         &bnapi->status_blk.msi->status_rx_quick_consumer_index0;
01087     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_MSIX_CAP) {
01088         for (i = 1; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++) {
01089             struct status_block_msix *sblk;
01090 
01091             bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
01092 
01093             sblk = (void *) (status_blk +
01094                      BNX2_SBLK_MSIX_ALIGN_SIZE * i);
01095             bnapi->status_blk.msix = sblk;
01096             bnapi->hw_tx_cons_ptr =
01097                 &sblk->status_tx_quick_consumer_index;
01098             bnapi->hw_rx_cons_ptr =
01099                 &sblk->status_rx_quick_consumer_index;
01100             bnapi->int_num = i << 24;
01101         }
01102     }
01103 
01104     bp->stats_blk = status_blk + status_blk_size;
01105 
01106     bp->stats_blk_mapping = bp->status_blk_mapping + status_blk_size;
01107 
01108     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
01109         /* NetQ uses CID 100, so we need 16K of context memory */
01110 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
01111         bp->ctx_pages = 0x4000 / BCM_PAGE_SIZE;
01112 #else  /* !defined(__VMKLNX__) */
01113         bp->ctx_pages = 0x2000 / BCM_PAGE_SIZE;
01114 #endif /* defined(__VMKLNX__) */
01115         if (bp->ctx_pages == 0)
01116             bp->ctx_pages = 1;
01117         for (i = 0; i < bp->ctx_pages; i++) {
01118             bp->ctx_blk[i] = pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev,
01119                         BCM_PAGE_SIZE,
01120                         &bp->ctx_blk_mapping[i]);
01121             if (bp->ctx_blk[i] == NULL)
01122                 goto alloc_mem_err;
01123         }
01124     }
01125 
01126     err = bnx2_alloc_rx_mem(bp);
01127     if (err)
01128         goto alloc_mem_err;
01129 
01130     err = bnx2_alloc_tx_mem(bp);
01131     if (err)
01132         goto alloc_mem_err;
01133 
01134     return 0;
01135 
01136 alloc_mem_err:
01137     bnx2_free_mem(bp);
01138     return -ENOMEM;
01139 }
01140 
01141 static void
01142 bnx2_report_fw_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
01143 {
01144     u32 fw_link_status = 0;
01145 
01146     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
01147         return;
01148 
01149     if (bp->link_up) {
01150         u32 bmsr;
01151 
01152         switch (bp->line_speed) {
01153         case SPEED_10:
01154             if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
01155                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_10HALF;
01156             else
01157                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_10FULL;
01158             break;
01159         case SPEED_100:
01160             if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
01161                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_100HALF;
01162             else
01163                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_100FULL;
01164             break;
01165         case SPEED_1000:
01166             if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
01167                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_1000HALF;
01168             else
01169                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_1000FULL;
01170             break;
01171         case SPEED_2500:
01172             if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
01173                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_2500HALF;
01174             else
01175                 fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_2500FULL;
01176             break;
01177         }
01178 
01179         fw_link_status |= BNX2_LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP;
01180 
01181         if (bp->autoneg) {
01182             fw_link_status |= BNX2_LINK_STATUS_AN_ENABLED;
01183 
01184             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
01185             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
01186 
01187             if (!(bmsr & BMSR_ANEGCOMPLETE) ||
01188                 bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT)
01189                 fw_link_status |= BNX2_LINK_STATUS_PARALLEL_DET;
01190             else
01191                 fw_link_status |= BNX2_LINK_STATUS_AN_COMPLETE;
01192         }
01193     }
01194     else
01195         fw_link_status = BNX2_LINK_STATUS_LINK_DOWN;
01196 
01197     bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_LINK_STATUS, fw_link_status);
01198 }
01199 
01200 static char *
01201 bnx2_xceiver_str(struct bnx2 *bp)
01202 {
01203     return ((bp->phy_port == PORT_FIBRE) ? "SerDes" :
01204         ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) ? "Remote Copper" :
01205          "Copper"));
01206 }
01207 
01208 static void
01209 bnx2_report_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
01210 {
01211     if (bp->link_up) {
01212         netif_carrier_on(bp->dev);
01213         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s NIC %s Link is Up, ", bp->dev->name,
01214                bnx2_xceiver_str(bp));
01215 
01216         printk("%d Mbps ", bp->line_speed);
01217 
01218         if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01219             printk("full duplex");
01220         else
01221             printk("half duplex");
01222 
01223         if (bp->flow_ctrl) {
01224             if (bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_RX) {
01225                 printk(", receive ");
01226                 if (bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_TX)
01227                     printk("& transmit ");
01228             }
01229             else {
01230                 printk(", transmit ");
01231             }
01232             printk("flow control ON");
01233         }
01234         printk("\n");
01235     }
01236     else {
01237         netif_carrier_off(bp->dev);
01238         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s NIC %s Link is Down\n", bp->dev->name,
01239                bnx2_xceiver_str(bp));
01240     }
01241 
01242     bnx2_report_fw_link(bp);
01243 }
01244 
01245 static void
01246 bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(struct bnx2 *bp)
01247 {
01248     u32 local_adv, remote_adv;
01249 
01250     bp->flow_ctrl = 0;
01251     if ((bp->autoneg & (AUTONEG_SPEED | AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL)) !=
01252         (AUTONEG_SPEED | AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL)) {
01253 
01254         if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL) {
01255             bp->flow_ctrl = bp->req_flow_ctrl;
01256         }
01257         return;
01258     }
01259 
01260     if (bp->duplex != DUPLEX_FULL) {
01261         return;
01262     }
01263 
01264     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
01265         (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708)) {
01266         u32 val;
01267 
01268         bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1, &val);
01269         if (val & BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_TX_PAUSE)
01270             bp->flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_TX;
01271         if (val & BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_RX_PAUSE)
01272             bp->flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_RX;
01273         return;
01274     }
01275 
01276     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &local_adv);
01277     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_lpa, &remote_adv);
01278 
01279     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
01280         u32 new_local_adv = 0;
01281         u32 new_remote_adv = 0;
01282 
01283         if (local_adv & ADVERTISE_1000XPAUSE)
01284             new_local_adv |= ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP;
01285         if (local_adv & ADVERTISE_1000XPSE_ASYM)
01286             new_local_adv |= ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM;
01287         if (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_1000XPAUSE)
01288             new_remote_adv |= ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP;
01289         if (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_1000XPSE_ASYM)
01290             new_remote_adv |= ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM;
01291 
01292         local_adv = new_local_adv;
01293         remote_adv = new_remote_adv;
01294     }
01295 
01296     /* See Table 28B-3 of 802.3ab-1999 spec. */
01297     if (local_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP) {
01298         if(local_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM) {
01299                     if (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP) {
01300                 bp->flow_ctrl = FLOW_CTRL_TX | FLOW_CTRL_RX;
01301             }
01302             else if (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM) {
01303                 bp->flow_ctrl = FLOW_CTRL_RX;
01304             }
01305         }
01306         else {
01307             if (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP) {
01308                 bp->flow_ctrl = FLOW_CTRL_TX | FLOW_CTRL_RX;
01309             }
01310         }
01311     }
01312     else if (local_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM) {
01313         if ((remote_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP) &&
01314             (remote_adv & ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM)) {
01315 
01316             bp->flow_ctrl = FLOW_CTRL_TX;
01317         }
01318     }
01319 }
01320 
01321 static int
01322 bnx2_5709s_linkup(struct bnx2 *bp)
01323 {
01324     u32 val, speed;
01325 
01326     bp->link_up = 1;
01327 
01328     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_GP_STATUS);
01329     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_STATUS1, &val);
01330     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01331 
01332     if ((bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) == 0) {
01333         bp->line_speed = bp->req_line_speed;
01334         bp->duplex = bp->req_duplex;
01335         return 0;
01336     }
01337     speed = val & MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_MSK;
01338     switch (speed) {
01339         case MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_10:
01340             bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
01341             break;
01342         case MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_100:
01343             bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
01344             break;
01345         case MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_1G:
01346         case MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_1GKV:
01347             bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
01348             break;
01349         case MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_SPEED_2_5G:
01350             bp->line_speed = SPEED_2500;
01351             break;
01352     }
01353     if (val & MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_FD)
01354         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01355     else
01356         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01357     return 0;
01358 }
01359 
01360 static int
01361 bnx2_5708s_linkup(struct bnx2 *bp)
01362 {
01363     u32 val;
01364 
01365     bp->link_up = 1;
01366     bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1, &val);
01367     switch (val & BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_SPEED_MASK) {
01368         case BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_SPEED_10:
01369             bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
01370             break;
01371         case BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_SPEED_100:
01372             bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
01373             break;
01374         case BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_SPEED_1G:
01375             bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
01376             break;
01377         case BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_SPEED_2G5:
01378             bp->line_speed = SPEED_2500;
01379             break;
01380     }
01381     if (val & BCM5708S_1000X_STAT1_FD)
01382         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01383     else
01384         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01385 
01386     return 0;
01387 }
01388 
01389 static int
01390 bnx2_5706s_linkup(struct bnx2 *bp)
01391 {
01392     u32 bmcr, local_adv, remote_adv, common;
01393 
01394     bp->link_up = 1;
01395     bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
01396 
01397     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01398     if (bmcr & BMCR_FULLDPLX) {
01399         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01400     }
01401     else {
01402         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01403     }
01404 
01405     if (!(bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE)) {
01406         return 0;
01407     }
01408 
01409     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &local_adv);
01410     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_lpa, &remote_adv);
01411 
01412     common = local_adv & remote_adv;
01413     if (common & (ADVERTISE_1000XHALF | ADVERTISE_1000XFULL)) {
01414 
01415         if (common & ADVERTISE_1000XFULL) {
01416             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01417         }
01418         else {
01419             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01420         }
01421     }
01422 
01423     return 0;
01424 }
01425 
01426 static int
01427 bnx2_copper_linkup(struct bnx2 *bp)
01428 {
01429     u32 bmcr;
01430 
01431     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01432     if (bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE) {
01433         u32 local_adv, remote_adv, common;
01434 
01435         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_CTRL1000, &local_adv);
01436         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_STAT1000, &remote_adv);
01437 
01438         common = local_adv & (remote_adv >> 2);
01439         if (common & ADVERTISE_1000FULL) {
01440             bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
01441             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01442         }
01443         else if (common & ADVERTISE_1000HALF) {
01444             bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
01445             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01446         }
01447         else {
01448             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &local_adv);
01449             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_lpa, &remote_adv);
01450 
01451             common = local_adv & remote_adv;
01452             if (common & ADVERTISE_100FULL) {
01453                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
01454                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01455             }
01456             else if (common & ADVERTISE_100HALF) {
01457                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
01458                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01459             }
01460             else if (common & ADVERTISE_10FULL) {
01461                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
01462                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01463             }
01464             else if (common & ADVERTISE_10HALF) {
01465                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
01466                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01467             }
01468             else {
01469                 bp->line_speed = 0;
01470                 bp->link_up = 0;
01471             }
01472         }
01473     }
01474     else {
01475         if (bmcr & BMCR_SPEED100) {
01476             bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
01477         }
01478         else {
01479             bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
01480         }
01481         if (bmcr & BMCR_FULLDPLX) {
01482             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
01483         }
01484         else {
01485             bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
01486         }
01487     }
01488 
01489     return 0;
01490 }
01491 
01492 static void
01493 bnx2_init_rx_context(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 cid)
01494 {
01495     u32 val, rx_cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(cid);
01496 
01497     val = BNX2_L2CTX_CTX_TYPE_CTX_BD_CHN_TYPE_VALUE;
01498     val |= BNX2_L2CTX_CTX_TYPE_SIZE_L2;
01499     val |= 0x02 << 8;
01500 
01501     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
01502         u32 lo_water, hi_water;
01503 
01504         if (bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_TX)
01505             lo_water = BNX2_L2CTX_LO_WATER_MARK_DEFAULT;
01506         else
01507             lo_water = BNX2_L2CTX_LO_WATER_MARK_DIS;
01508         if (lo_water >= bp->rx_ring_size)
01509             lo_water = 0;
01510 
01511         hi_water = min(bp->rx_ring_size / 4, (int) lo_water + 16);
01512 
01513         if (hi_water <= lo_water)
01514             lo_water = 0;
01515 
01516         hi_water /= BNX2_L2CTX_HI_WATER_MARK_SCALE;
01517         lo_water /= BNX2_L2CTX_LO_WATER_MARK_SCALE;
01518 
01519         if (hi_water > 0xf)
01520             hi_water = 0xf;
01521         else if (hi_water == 0)
01522             lo_water = 0;
01523         val |= lo_water | (hi_water << BNX2_L2CTX_HI_WATER_MARK_SHIFT);
01524     }
01525     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_CTX_TYPE, val);
01526 }
01527 
01528 static void
01529 bnx2_init_all_rx_contexts(struct bnx2 *bp)
01530 {
01531     int i;
01532     u32 cid;
01533 
01534     for (i = 0, cid = RX_CID; i < bp->num_rx_rings; i++, cid++) {
01535         if (i == 1)
01536             cid = RX_RSS_CID;
01537         bnx2_init_rx_context(bp, cid);
01538     }
01539 }
01540 
01541 static void
01542 bnx2_set_mac_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
01543 {
01544     u32 val;
01545 
01546     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_TX_LENGTHS, 0x2620);
01547     if (bp->link_up && (bp->line_speed == SPEED_1000) &&
01548         (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)) {
01549         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_TX_LENGTHS, 0x26ff);
01550     }
01551 
01552     /* Configure the EMAC mode register. */
01553     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE);
01554 
01555     val &= ~(BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_HALF_DUPLEX |
01556         BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MAC_LOOP | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_FORCE_LINK |
01557         BNX2_EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE);
01558 
01559     if (bp->link_up) {
01560         switch (bp->line_speed) {
01561             case SPEED_10:
01562                 if (CHIP_NUM(bp) != CHIP_NUM_5706) {
01563                     val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII_10M;
01564                     break;
01565                 }
01566                 /* fall through */
01567             case SPEED_100:
01568                 val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII;
01569                 break;
01570             case SPEED_2500:
01571                 val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE;
01572                 /* fall through */
01573             case SPEED_1000:
01574                 val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII;
01575                 break;
01576         }
01577     }
01578     else {
01579         val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII;
01580     }
01581 
01582     /* Set the MAC to operate in the appropriate duplex mode. */
01583     if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_HALF)
01584         val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_HALF_DUPLEX;
01585     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE, val);
01586 
01587     /* Enable/disable rx PAUSE. */
01588     bp->rx_mode &= ~BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_FLOW_EN;
01589 
01590     if (bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_RX)
01591         bp->rx_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_FLOW_EN;
01592     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE, bp->rx_mode);
01593 
01594     /* Enable/disable tx PAUSE. */
01595     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_TX_MODE);
01596     val &= ~BNX2_EMAC_TX_MODE_FLOW_EN;
01597 
01598     if (bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_TX)
01599         val |= BNX2_EMAC_TX_MODE_FLOW_EN;
01600     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_TX_MODE, val);
01601 
01602     /* Acknowledge the interrupt. */
01603     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_STATUS, BNX2_EMAC_STATUS_LINK_CHANGE);
01604 
01605     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01606         bnx2_init_all_rx_contexts(bp);
01607 }
01608 
01609 static void
01610 bnx2_enable_bmsr1(struct bnx2 *bp)
01611 {
01612     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
01613         (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709))
01614         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01615                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_GP_STATUS);
01616 }
01617 
01618 static void
01619 bnx2_disable_bmsr1(struct bnx2 *bp)
01620 {
01621     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
01622         (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709))
01623         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01624                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01625 }
01626 
01627 static int
01628 bnx2_test_and_enable_2g5(struct bnx2 *bp)
01629 {
01630     u32 up1;
01631     int ret = 1;
01632 
01633     if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE))
01634         return 0;
01635 
01636     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)
01637         bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_2500baseX_Full;
01638 
01639     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01640         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_OVER1G);
01641 
01642     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_up1, &up1);
01643     if (!(up1 & BCM5708S_UP1_2G5)) {
01644         up1 |= BCM5708S_UP1_2G5;
01645         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_up1, up1);
01646         ret = 0;
01647     }
01648 
01649     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01650         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01651                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01652 
01653     return ret;
01654 }
01655 
01656 static int
01657 bnx2_test_and_disable_2g5(struct bnx2 *bp)
01658 {
01659     u32 up1;
01660     int ret = 0;
01661 
01662     if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE))
01663         return 0;
01664 
01665     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01666         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_OVER1G);
01667 
01668     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_up1, &up1);
01669     if (up1 & BCM5708S_UP1_2G5) {
01670         up1 &= ~BCM5708S_UP1_2G5;
01671         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_up1, up1);
01672         ret = 1;
01673     }
01674 
01675     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01676         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01677                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01678 
01679     return ret;
01680 }
01681 
01682 static void
01683 bnx2_enable_forced_2g5(struct bnx2 *bp)
01684 {
01685     u32 bmcr;
01686 
01687     if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE))
01688         return;
01689 
01690     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
01691         u32 val;
01692 
01693         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01694                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_SERDES_DIG);
01695         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_MISC1, &val);
01696         val &= ~MII_BNX2_SD_MISC1_FORCE_MSK;
01697         val |= MII_BNX2_SD_MISC1_FORCE | MII_BNX2_SD_MISC1_FORCE_2_5G;
01698         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_MISC1, val);
01699 
01700         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01701                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01702         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01703 
01704     } else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708) {
01705         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01706         bmcr |= BCM5708S_BMCR_FORCE_2500;
01707     } else {
01708         return;
01709     }
01710 
01711     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) {
01712         bmcr &= ~BMCR_ANENABLE;
01713         if (bp->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01714             bmcr |= BMCR_FULLDPLX;
01715     }
01716     bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr);
01717 }
01718 
01719 static void
01720 bnx2_disable_forced_2g5(struct bnx2 *bp)
01721 {
01722     u32 bmcr;
01723 
01724     if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE))
01725         return;
01726 
01727     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
01728         u32 val;
01729 
01730         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01731                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_SERDES_DIG);
01732         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_MISC1, &val);
01733         val &= ~MII_BNX2_SD_MISC1_FORCE;
01734         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_MISC1, val);
01735 
01736         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR,
01737                    MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
01738         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01739 
01740     } else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708) {
01741         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01742         bmcr &= ~BCM5708S_BMCR_FORCE_2500;
01743     } else {
01744         return;
01745     }
01746 
01747     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)
01748         bmcr |= BMCR_SPEED1000 | BMCR_ANENABLE | BMCR_ANRESTART;
01749     bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr);
01750 }
01751 
01752 static void
01753 bnx2_5706s_force_link_dn(struct bnx2 *bp, int start)
01754 {
01755     u32 val;
01756 
01757     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_ADDRESS, MII_EXPAND_SERDES_CTL);
01758     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, &val);
01759     if (start)
01760         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, val & 0xff0f);
01761     else
01762         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, val | 0xc0);
01763 }
01764 
01765 static int
01766 bnx2_set_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
01767 {
01768     u32 bmsr;
01769     u8 link_up;
01770 
01771     if (bp->loopback == MAC_LOOPBACK || bp->loopback == PHY_LOOPBACK) {
01772         bp->link_up = 1;
01773         return 0;
01774     }
01775 
01776     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
01777         return 0;
01778 
01779     link_up = bp->link_up;
01780 
01781     bnx2_enable_bmsr1(bp);
01782     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr1, &bmsr);
01783     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr1, &bmsr);
01784     bnx2_disable_bmsr1(bp);
01785 
01786     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
01787         (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706)) {
01788         u32 val, an_dbg;
01789 
01790         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_FORCED_DOWN) {
01791             bnx2_5706s_force_link_dn(bp, 0);
01792             bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_FORCED_DOWN;
01793         }
01794         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_STATUS);
01795 
01796         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG);
01797         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &an_dbg);
01798         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &an_dbg);
01799 
01800         if ((val & BNX2_EMAC_STATUS_LINK) &&
01801             !(an_dbg & MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG_NOSYNC))
01802             bmsr |= BMSR_LSTATUS;
01803         else
01804             bmsr &= ~BMSR_LSTATUS;
01805     }
01806 
01807     if (bmsr & BMSR_LSTATUS) {
01808         bp->link_up = 1;
01809 
01810         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
01811             if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706)
01812                 bnx2_5706s_linkup(bp);
01813             else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708)
01814                 bnx2_5708s_linkup(bp);
01815             else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
01816                 bnx2_5709s_linkup(bp);
01817         }
01818         else {
01819             bnx2_copper_linkup(bp);
01820         }
01821         bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
01822     }
01823     else {
01824         if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
01825             (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED))
01826             bnx2_disable_forced_2g5(bp);
01827 
01828         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT) {
01829             u32 bmcr;
01830 
01831             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01832             bmcr |= BMCR_ANENABLE;
01833             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr);
01834 
01835             bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT;
01836         }
01837         bp->link_up = 0;
01838     }
01839 
01840     if (bp->link_up != link_up) {
01841         bnx2_report_link(bp);
01842     }
01843 
01844     bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
01845 
01846     return 0;
01847 }
01848 
01849 static int
01850 bnx2_reset_phy(struct bnx2 *bp)
01851 {
01852     int i;
01853     u32 reg;
01854 
01855         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_RESET);
01856 
01857 #define PHY_RESET_MAX_WAIT 100
01858     for (i = 0; i < PHY_RESET_MAX_WAIT; i++) {
01859         udelay(10);
01860 
01861         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &reg);
01862         if (!(reg & BMCR_RESET)) {
01863             udelay(20);
01864             break;
01865         }
01866     }
01867     if (i == PHY_RESET_MAX_WAIT) {
01868         return -EBUSY;
01869     }
01870     return 0;
01871 }
01872 
01873 static u32
01874 bnx2_phy_get_pause_adv(struct bnx2 *bp)
01875 {
01876     u32 adv = 0;
01877 
01878     if ((bp->req_flow_ctrl & (FLOW_CTRL_RX | FLOW_CTRL_TX)) ==
01879         (FLOW_CTRL_RX | FLOW_CTRL_TX)) {
01880 
01881         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
01882             adv = ADVERTISE_1000XPAUSE;
01883         }
01884         else {
01885             adv = ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP;
01886         }
01887     }
01888     else if (bp->req_flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_TX) {
01889         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
01890             adv = ADVERTISE_1000XPSE_ASYM;
01891         }
01892         else {
01893             adv = ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM;
01894         }
01895     }
01896     else if (bp->req_flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_RX) {
01897         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
01898             adv = ADVERTISE_1000XPAUSE | ADVERTISE_1000XPSE_ASYM;
01899         }
01900         else {
01901             adv = ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP | ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM;
01902         }
01903     }
01904     return adv;
01905 }
01906 
01907 static int bnx2_fw_sync(struct bnx2 *, u32, int, int);
01908 
01909 static int
01910 bnx2_setup_remote_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, u8 port)
01911 __releases(&bp->phy_lock)
01912 __acquires(&bp->phy_lock)
01913 {
01914     u32 speed_arg = 0, pause_adv;
01915 
01916     pause_adv = bnx2_phy_get_pause_adv(bp);
01917 
01918     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) {
01919         speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_ENABLE_AUTONEG;
01920         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half)
01921             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10HALF;
01922         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full)
01923             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10FULL;
01924         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half)
01925             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100HALF;
01926         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full)
01927             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100FULL;
01928         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
01929             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_1GFULL;
01930         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_2500baseX_Full)
01931             speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_2G5FULL;
01932     } else {
01933         if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_2500)
01934             speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_2G5FULL;
01935         else if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_1000)
01936             speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_1GFULL;
01937         else if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_100) {
01938             if (bp->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01939                 speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100FULL;
01940             else
01941                 speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100HALF;
01942         } else if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_10) {
01943             if (bp->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
01944                 speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10FULL;
01945             else
01946                 speed_arg = BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10HALF;
01947         }
01948     }
01949 
01950     if (pause_adv & (ADVERTISE_1000XPAUSE | ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP))
01951         speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_FC_SYM_PAUSE;
01952     if (pause_adv & (ADVERTISE_1000XPSE_ASYM | ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM))
01953         speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_FC_ASYM_PAUSE;
01954 
01955     if (port == PORT_TP)
01956         speed_arg |= BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_PHY_APP_REMOTE |
01957                  BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_ETH_AT_WIRESPEED;
01958 
01959     bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_DRV_MB_ARG0, speed_arg);
01960 
01961     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
01962     bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_CMD_SET_LINK, 1, 0);
01963     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
01964 
01965     return 0;
01966 }
01967 
01968 static int
01969 bnx2_setup_serdes_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, u8 port)
01970 __releases(&bp->phy_lock)
01971 __acquires(&bp->phy_lock)
01972 {
01973     u32 adv, bmcr;
01974     u32 new_adv = 0;
01975 
01976     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
01977         return (bnx2_setup_remote_phy(bp, port));
01978 
01979     if (!(bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)) {
01980         u32 new_bmcr;
01981         int force_link_down = 0;
01982 
01983         if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_2500) {
01984             if (!bnx2_test_and_enable_2g5(bp))
01985                 force_link_down = 1;
01986         } else if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_1000) {
01987             if (bnx2_test_and_disable_2g5(bp))
01988                 force_link_down = 1;
01989         }
01990         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &adv);
01991         adv &= ~(ADVERTISE_1000XFULL | ADVERTISE_1000XHALF);
01992 
01993         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
01994         new_bmcr = bmcr & ~BMCR_ANENABLE;
01995         new_bmcr |= BMCR_SPEED1000;
01996 
01997         if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
01998             if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_2500)
01999                 bnx2_enable_forced_2g5(bp);
02000             else if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_1000) {
02001                 bnx2_disable_forced_2g5(bp);
02002                 new_bmcr &= ~0x2000;
02003             }
02004 
02005         } else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708) {
02006             if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_2500)
02007                 new_bmcr |= BCM5708S_BMCR_FORCE_2500;
02008             else
02009                 new_bmcr = bmcr & ~BCM5708S_BMCR_FORCE_2500;
02010         }
02011 
02012         if (bp->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL) {
02013             adv |= ADVERTISE_1000XFULL;
02014             new_bmcr |= BMCR_FULLDPLX;
02015         }
02016         else {
02017             adv |= ADVERTISE_1000XHALF;
02018             new_bmcr &= ~BMCR_FULLDPLX;
02019         }
02020         if ((new_bmcr != bmcr) || (force_link_down)) {
02021             /* Force a link down visible on the other side */
02022             if (bp->link_up) {
02023                 bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, adv &
02024                            ~(ADVERTISE_1000XFULL |
02025                          ADVERTISE_1000XHALF));
02026                 bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr |
02027                     BMCR_ANRESTART | BMCR_ANENABLE);
02028 
02029                 bp->link_up = 0;
02030                 netif_carrier_off(bp->dev);
02031                 bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, new_bmcr);
02032                 bnx2_report_link(bp);
02033             }
02034             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, adv);
02035             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, new_bmcr);
02036         } else {
02037             bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
02038             bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02039         }
02040         return 0;
02041     }
02042 
02043     bnx2_test_and_enable_2g5(bp);
02044 
02045     if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
02046         new_adv |= ADVERTISE_1000XFULL;
02047 
02048     new_adv |= bnx2_phy_get_pause_adv(bp);
02049 
02050     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &adv);
02051     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
02052 
02053     bp->serdes_an_pending = 0;
02054     if ((adv != new_adv) || ((bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE) == 0)) {
02055         /* Force a link down visible on the other side */
02056         if (bp->link_up) {
02057             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_LOOPBACK);
02058             spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02059             bnx2_msleep(20);
02060             spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02061         }
02062 
02063         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, new_adv);
02064         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr | BMCR_ANRESTART |
02065             BMCR_ANENABLE);
02066         /* Speed up link-up time when the link partner
02067          * does not autonegotiate which is very common
02068          * in blade servers. Some blade servers use
02069          * IPMI for kerboard input and it's important
02070          * to minimize link disruptions. Autoneg. involves
02071          * exchanging base pages plus 3 next pages and
02072          * normally completes in about 120 msec.
02073          */
02074         bp->current_interval = BNX2_SERDES_AN_TIMEOUT;
02075         bp->serdes_an_pending = 1;
02076         mod_timer(&bp->timer, jiffies + bp->current_interval);
02077     } else {
02078         bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
02079         bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02080     }
02081 
02082     return 0;
02083 }
02084 
02085 #define ETHTOOL_ALL_FIBRE_SPEED                     \
02086     (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE) ?          \
02087         (ADVERTISED_2500baseX_Full | ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full) :\
02088         (ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
02089 
02090 #define ETHTOOL_ALL_COPPER_SPEED                    \
02091     (ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half | ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full |        \
02092     ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half | ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full |       \
02093     ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
02094 
02095 #define PHY_ALL_10_100_SPEED (ADVERTISE_10HALF | ADVERTISE_10FULL | \
02096     ADVERTISE_100HALF | ADVERTISE_100FULL | ADVERTISE_CSMA)
02097 
02098 #define PHY_ALL_1000_SPEED (ADVERTISE_1000HALF | ADVERTISE_1000FULL)
02099 
02100 static void
02101 bnx2_set_default_remote_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
02102 {
02103     u32 link;
02104 
02105     if (bp->phy_port == PORT_TP)
02106         link = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_RPHY_COPPER_LINK);
02107     else
02108         link = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_RPHY_SERDES_LINK);
02109 
02110     if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_ENABLE_AUTONEG) {
02111         bp->req_line_speed = 0;
02112         bp->autoneg |= AUTONEG_SPEED;
02113         bp->advertising = ADVERTISED_Autoneg;
02114         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10HALF)
02115             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half;
02116         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10FULL)
02117             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full;
02118         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100HALF)
02119             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half;
02120         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100FULL)
02121             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full;
02122         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_1GFULL)
02123             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full;
02124         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_2G5FULL)
02125             bp->advertising |= ADVERTISED_2500baseX_Full;
02126     } else {
02127         bp->autoneg = 0;
02128         bp->advertising = 0;
02129         bp->req_duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
02130         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10) {
02131             bp->req_line_speed = SPEED_10;
02132             if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_10HALF)
02133                 bp->req_duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02134         }
02135         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100) {
02136             bp->req_line_speed = SPEED_100;
02137             if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_100HALF)
02138                 bp->req_duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02139         }
02140         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_1GFULL)
02141             bp->req_line_speed = SPEED_1000;
02142         if (link & BNX2_NETLINK_SET_LINK_SPEED_2G5FULL)
02143             bp->req_line_speed = SPEED_2500;
02144     }
02145 }
02146 
02147 static void
02148 bnx2_set_default_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
02149 {
02150     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP) {
02151         bnx2_set_default_remote_link(bp);
02152         return;
02153     }
02154 
02155     bp->autoneg = AUTONEG_SPEED | AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL;
02156     bp->req_line_speed = 0;
02157     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
02158         u32 reg;
02159 
02160         bp->advertising = ETHTOOL_ALL_FIBRE_SPEED | ADVERTISED_Autoneg;
02161 
02162         reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_CONFIG);
02163         reg &= BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_CFG_DFLT_LINK_MASK;
02164         if (reg == BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_CFG_DFLT_LINK_1G) {
02165             bp->autoneg = 0;
02166             bp->req_line_speed = bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
02167             bp->req_duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
02168         }
02169     } else
02170         bp->advertising = ETHTOOL_ALL_COPPER_SPEED | ADVERTISED_Autoneg;
02171 }
02172 
02173 static void
02174 bnx2_send_heart_beat(struct bnx2 *bp)
02175 {
02176     u32 msg;
02177     u32 addr;
02178 
02179     spin_lock(&bp->indirect_lock);
02180     msg = (u32) (++bp->fw_drv_pulse_wr_seq & BNX2_DRV_PULSE_SEQ_MASK);
02181     addr = bp->shmem_base + BNX2_DRV_PULSE_MB;
02182     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW_ADDRESS, addr);
02183     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW, msg);
02184     spin_unlock(&bp->indirect_lock);
02185 }
02186 
02187 static void
02188 bnx2_remote_phy_event(struct bnx2 *bp)
02189 {
02190     u32 msg;
02191     u8 link_up = bp->link_up;
02192     u8 old_port;
02193 
02194     msg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_LINK_STATUS);
02195 
02196     if (msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_HEART_BEAT_EXPIRED)
02197         bnx2_send_heart_beat(bp);
02198 
02199     msg &= ~BNX2_LINK_STATUS_HEART_BEAT_EXPIRED;
02200 
02201     if ((msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_LINK_UP) == BNX2_LINK_STATUS_LINK_DOWN)
02202         bp->link_up = 0;
02203     else {
02204         u32 speed;
02205 
02206         bp->link_up = 1;
02207         speed = msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_SPEED_MASK;
02208         bp->duplex = DUPLEX_FULL;
02209         switch (speed) {
02210             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_10HALF:
02211                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02212             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_10FULL:
02213                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_10;
02214                 break;
02215             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_100HALF:
02216                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02217             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_100BASE_T4:
02218             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_100FULL:
02219                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_100;
02220                 break;
02221             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_1000HALF:
02222                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02223             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_1000FULL:
02224                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_1000;
02225                 break;
02226             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_2500HALF:
02227                 bp->duplex = DUPLEX_HALF;
02228             case BNX2_LINK_STATUS_2500FULL:
02229                 bp->line_speed = SPEED_2500;
02230                 break;
02231             default:
02232                 bp->line_speed = 0;
02233                 break;
02234         }
02235 
02236         bp->flow_ctrl = 0;
02237         if ((bp->autoneg & (AUTONEG_SPEED | AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL)) !=
02238             (AUTONEG_SPEED | AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL)) {
02239             if (bp->duplex == DUPLEX_FULL)
02240                 bp->flow_ctrl = bp->req_flow_ctrl;
02241         } else {
02242             if (msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_TX_FC_ENABLED)
02243                 bp->flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_TX;
02244             if (msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_RX_FC_ENABLED)
02245                 bp->flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_RX;
02246         }
02247 
02248         old_port = bp->phy_port;
02249         if (msg & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_SERDES_LINK)
02250             bp->phy_port = PORT_FIBRE;
02251         else
02252             bp->phy_port = PORT_TP;
02253 
02254         if (old_port != bp->phy_port)
02255             bnx2_set_default_link(bp);
02256 
02257     }
02258     if (bp->link_up != link_up)
02259         bnx2_report_link(bp);
02260 
02261     bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02262 }
02263 
02264 static int
02265 bnx2_set_remote_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
02266 {
02267     u32 evt_code;
02268 
02269     spin_lock(&bp->indirect_lock);
02270     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW_ADDRESS,
02271            bp->shmem_base + BNX2_FW_EVT_CODE_MB);
02272     evt_code = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_REG_WINDOW);
02273     spin_unlock(&bp->indirect_lock);
02274     switch (evt_code) {
02275         case BNX2_FW_EVT_CODE_LINK_EVENT:
02276             bnx2_remote_phy_event(bp);
02277             break;
02278         case BNX2_FW_EVT_CODE_SW_TIMER_EXPIRATION_EVENT:
02279         default:
02280             bnx2_send_heart_beat(bp);
02281             break;
02282     }
02283     return 0;
02284 }
02285 
02286 static int
02287 bnx2_setup_copper_phy(struct bnx2 *bp)
02288 __releases(&bp->phy_lock)
02289 __acquires(&bp->phy_lock)
02290 {
02291     u32 bmcr;
02292     u32 new_bmcr;
02293 
02294     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
02295 
02296     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) {
02297         u32 adv_reg, adv1000_reg;
02298         u32 new_adv_reg = 0;
02299         u32 new_adv1000_reg = 0;
02300 
02301         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, &adv_reg);
02302         adv_reg &= (PHY_ALL_10_100_SPEED | ADVERTISE_PAUSE_CAP |
02303             ADVERTISE_PAUSE_ASYM);
02304 
02305         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_CTRL1000, &adv1000_reg);
02306         adv1000_reg &= PHY_ALL_1000_SPEED;
02307 
02308         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half)
02309             new_adv_reg |= ADVERTISE_10HALF;
02310         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full)
02311             new_adv_reg |= ADVERTISE_10FULL;
02312         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half)
02313             new_adv_reg |= ADVERTISE_100HALF;
02314         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full)
02315             new_adv_reg |= ADVERTISE_100FULL;
02316         if (bp->advertising & ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
02317             new_adv1000_reg |= ADVERTISE_1000FULL;
02318 
02319         new_adv_reg |= ADVERTISE_CSMA;
02320 
02321         new_adv_reg |= bnx2_phy_get_pause_adv(bp);
02322 
02323         if ((adv1000_reg != new_adv1000_reg) ||
02324             (adv_reg != new_adv_reg) ||
02325             ((bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE) == 0)) {
02326 
02327             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_adv, new_adv_reg);
02328             bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_CTRL1000, new_adv1000_reg);
02329             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_ANRESTART |
02330                 BMCR_ANENABLE);
02331         }
02332         else if (bp->link_up) {
02333             /* Flow ctrl may have changed from auto to forced */
02334             /* or vice-versa. */
02335 
02336             bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
02337             bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02338         }
02339         return 0;
02340     }
02341 
02342     new_bmcr = 0;
02343     if (bp->req_line_speed == SPEED_100) {
02344         new_bmcr |= BMCR_SPEED100;
02345     }
02346     if (bp->req_duplex == DUPLEX_FULL) {
02347         new_bmcr |= BMCR_FULLDPLX;
02348     }
02349     if (new_bmcr != bmcr) {
02350         u32 bmsr;
02351 
02352         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
02353         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
02354 
02355         if (bmsr & BMSR_LSTATUS) {
02356             /* Force link down */
02357             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_LOOPBACK);
02358             spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02359             bnx2_msleep(50);
02360             spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02361 
02362             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
02363             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr, &bmsr);
02364         }
02365 
02366         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, new_bmcr);
02367 
02368         /* Normally, the new speed is setup after the link has
02369          * gone down and up again. In some cases, link will not go
02370          * down so we need to set up the new speed here.
02371          */
02372         if (bmsr & BMSR_LSTATUS) {
02373             bp->line_speed = bp->req_line_speed;
02374             bp->duplex = bp->req_duplex;
02375             bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
02376             bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02377         }
02378     } else {
02379         bnx2_resolve_flow_ctrl(bp);
02380         bnx2_set_mac_link(bp);
02381     }
02382     return 0;
02383 }
02384 
02385 static int
02386 bnx2_setup_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, u8 port)
02387 __releases(&bp->phy_lock)
02388 __acquires(&bp->phy_lock)
02389 {
02390     if (bp->loopback == MAC_LOOPBACK)
02391         return 0;
02392 
02393     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
02394         return (bnx2_setup_serdes_phy(bp, port));
02395     }
02396     else {
02397         return (bnx2_setup_copper_phy(bp));
02398     }
02399 }
02400 
02401 static int
02402 bnx2_init_5709s_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
02403 {
02404     u32 val;
02405 
02406     bp->mii_bmcr = MII_BMCR + 0x10;
02407     bp->mii_bmsr = MII_BMSR + 0x10;
02408     bp->mii_bmsr1 = MII_BNX2_GP_TOP_AN_STATUS1;
02409     bp->mii_adv = MII_ADVERTISE + 0x10;
02410     bp->mii_lpa = MII_LPA + 0x10;
02411     bp->mii_up1 = MII_BNX2_OVER1G_UP1;
02412 
02413     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_AER);
02414     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_AER_AER, MII_BNX2_AER_AER_AN_MMD);
02415 
02416     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
02417     if (reset_phy)
02418         bnx2_reset_phy(bp);
02419 
02420     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_SERDES_DIG);
02421 
02422     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_1000XCTL1, &val);
02423     val &= ~MII_BNX2_SD_1000XCTL1_AUTODET;
02424     val |= MII_BNX2_SD_1000XCTL1_FIBER;
02425     /* NEMO temp. FIX */
02426     if (bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_CONFIG) & 0x80000000)
02427         val |= (1 << 3);
02428     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_SERDES_DIG_1000XCTL1, val);
02429 
02430     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_OVER1G);
02431     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_OVER1G_UP1, &val);
02432     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE)
02433         val |= BCM5708S_UP1_2G5;
02434     else
02435         val &= ~BCM5708S_UP1_2G5;
02436     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_OVER1G_UP1, val);
02437 
02438     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_BAM_NXTPG);
02439     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BAM_NXTPG_CTL, &val);
02440     val |= MII_BNX2_NXTPG_CTL_T2 | MII_BNX2_NXTPG_CTL_BAM;
02441     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BAM_NXTPG_CTL, val);
02442 
02443     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_CL73_USERB0);
02444 
02445     val = MII_BNX2_CL73_BAM_EN | MII_BNX2_CL73_BAM_STA_MGR_EN |
02446           MII_BNX2_CL73_BAM_NP_AFT_BP_EN;
02447     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_CL73_BAM_CTL1, val);
02448 
02449     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR, MII_BNX2_BLK_ADDR_COMBO_IEEEB0);
02450 
02451     return 0;
02452 }
02453 
02454 static int
02455 bnx2_init_5708s_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
02456 {
02457     u32 val;
02458 
02459     if (reset_phy)
02460         bnx2_reset_phy(bp);
02461 
02462     bp->mii_up1 = BCM5708S_UP1;
02463 
02464     bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_DIG3);
02465     bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_DIG_3_0, BCM5708S_DIG_3_0_USE_IEEE);
02466     bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_DIG);
02467 
02468     bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_CTL1, &val);
02469     val |= BCM5708S_1000X_CTL1_FIBER_MODE | BCM5708S_1000X_CTL1_AUTODET_EN;
02470     bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_CTL1, val);
02471 
02472     bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_CTL2, &val);
02473     val |= BCM5708S_1000X_CTL2_PLLEL_DET_EN;
02474     bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_1000X_CTL2, val);
02475 
02476     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE) {
02477         bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_UP1, &val);
02478         val |= BCM5708S_UP1_2G5;
02479         bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_UP1, val);
02480     }
02481 
02482     if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_A0) ||
02483         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_B0) ||
02484         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_B1)) {
02485         /* increase tx signal amplitude */
02486         bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR,
02487                    BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_TX_MISC);
02488         bnx2_read_phy(bp, BCM5708S_TX_ACTL1, &val);
02489         val &= ~BCM5708S_TX_ACTL1_DRIVER_VCM;
02490         bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_TX_ACTL1, val);
02491         bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_DIG);
02492     }
02493 
02494     val = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_CONFIG) &
02495           BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_CFG_TXCTL3_MASK;
02496 
02497     if (val) {
02498         u32 is_backplane;
02499 
02500         is_backplane = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_CONFIG);
02501         if (is_backplane & BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_PHY_BACKPLANE) {
02502             bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR,
02503                        BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_TX_MISC);
02504             bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_TX_ACTL3, val);
02505             bnx2_write_phy(bp, BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR,
02506                        BCM5708S_BLK_ADDR_DIG);
02507         }
02508     }
02509     return 0;
02510 }
02511 
02512 static int
02513 bnx2_init_5706s_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
02514 {
02515     if (reset_phy)
02516         bnx2_reset_phy(bp);
02517 
02518     bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT;
02519 
02520     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706)
02521             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_GP_HW_CTL0, 0x300);
02522 
02523     if (bp->dev->mtu > 1500) {
02524         u32 val;
02525 
02526         /* Set extended packet length bit */
02527         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x7);
02528         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x18, &val);
02529         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, (val & 0xfff8) | 0x4000);
02530 
02531         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x1c, 0x6c00);
02532         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x1c, &val);
02533         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x1c, (val & 0x3ff) | 0xec02);
02534     }
02535     else {
02536         u32 val;
02537 
02538         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x7);
02539         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x18, &val);
02540         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, val & ~0x4007);
02541 
02542         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x1c, 0x6c00);
02543         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x1c, &val);
02544         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x1c, (val & 0x3fd) | 0xec00);
02545     }
02546 
02547     return 0;
02548 }
02549 
02550 static int
02551 bnx2_init_copper_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
02552 {
02553     u32 val;
02554 
02555     if (reset_phy)
02556         bnx2_reset_phy(bp);
02557 
02558     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_CRC_FIX) {
02559         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x0c00);
02560         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x17, 0x000a);
02561         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x15, 0x310b);
02562         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x17, 0x201f);
02563         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x15, 0x9506);
02564         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x17, 0x401f);
02565         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x15, 0x14e2);
02566         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x0400);
02567     }
02568 
02569     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_DIS_EARLY_DAC) {
02570         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_ADDRESS,
02571                    MII_BNX2_DSP_EXPAND_REG | 0x8);
02572         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, &val);
02573         val &= ~(1 << 8);
02574         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, val);
02575     }
02576 
02577     if (bp->dev->mtu > 1500) {
02578         /* Set extended packet length bit */
02579         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x7);
02580         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x18, &val);
02581         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, val | 0x4000);
02582 
02583         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x10, &val);
02584         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x10, val | 0x1);
02585     }
02586     else {
02587         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x7);
02588         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x18, &val);
02589         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, val & ~0x4007);
02590 
02591         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x10, &val);
02592         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x10, val & ~0x1);
02593     }
02594 
02595     /* ethernet@wirespeed */
02596     bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, 0x7007);
02597     bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x18, &val);
02598     bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x18, val | (1 << 15) | (1 << 4));
02599     return 0;
02600 }
02601 
02602 
02603 static int
02604 bnx2_init_phy(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
02605 __releases(&bp->phy_lock)
02606 __acquires(&bp->phy_lock)
02607 {
02608     u32 val;
02609     int rc = 0;
02610 
02611     bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_MASK;
02612     bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_INT_MODE_LINK_READY;
02613 
02614     bp->mii_bmcr = MII_BMCR;
02615     bp->mii_bmsr = MII_BMSR;
02616     bp->mii_bmsr1 = MII_BMSR;
02617     bp->mii_adv = MII_ADVERTISE;
02618     bp->mii_lpa = MII_LPA;
02619 
02620         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_ATTENTION_ENA, BNX2_EMAC_ATTENTION_ENA_LINK);
02621 
02622     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
02623         goto setup_phy;
02624 
02625     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_PHYSID1, &val);
02626     bp->phy_id = val << 16;
02627     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_PHYSID2, &val);
02628     bp->phy_id |= val & 0xffff;
02629 
02630     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
02631         if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706)
02632             rc = bnx2_init_5706s_phy(bp, reset_phy);
02633         else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708)
02634             rc = bnx2_init_5708s_phy(bp, reset_phy);
02635         else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
02636             rc = bnx2_init_5709s_phy(bp, reset_phy);
02637     }
02638     else {
02639         rc = bnx2_init_copper_phy(bp, reset_phy);
02640     }
02641 
02642 setup_phy:
02643     if (!rc)
02644         rc = bnx2_setup_phy(bp, bp->phy_port);
02645 
02646     return rc;
02647 }
02648 
02649 static int
02650 bnx2_set_mac_loopback(struct bnx2 *bp)
02651 {
02652     u32 mac_mode;
02653 
02654     mac_mode = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE);
02655     mac_mode &= ~BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT;
02656     mac_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MAC_LOOP | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_FORCE_LINK;
02657     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE, mac_mode);
02658     bp->link_up = 1;
02659     return 0;
02660 }
02661 
02662 static int bnx2_test_link(struct bnx2 *);
02663 
02664 static int
02665 bnx2_set_phy_loopback(struct bnx2 *bp)
02666 {
02667     u32 mac_mode;
02668     int rc, i;
02669 
02670     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02671     rc = bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_LOOPBACK | BMCR_FULLDPLX |
02672                 BMCR_SPEED1000);
02673     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
02674     if (rc)
02675         return rc;
02676 
02677     for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
02678         if (bnx2_test_link(bp) == 0)
02679             break;
02680         bnx2_msleep(100);
02681     }
02682 
02683     mac_mode = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE);
02684     mac_mode &= ~(BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_HALF_DUPLEX |
02685               BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MAC_LOOP | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_FORCE_LINK |
02686               BNX2_EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE);
02687 
02688     mac_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII;
02689     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE, mac_mode);
02690     bp->link_up = 1;
02691     return 0;
02692 }
02693 
02694 static int
02695 bnx2_fw_sync(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 msg_data, int ack, int silent)
02696 {
02697     int i;
02698     u32 val;
02699 
02700     bp->fw_wr_seq++;
02701     msg_data |= bp->fw_wr_seq;
02702 
02703     bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_DRV_MB, msg_data);
02704 
02705     if (!ack)
02706         return 0;
02707 
02708     /* wait for an acknowledgement. */
02709     for (i = 0; i < (BNX2_FW_ACK_TIME_OUT_MS / 10); i++) {
02710         bnx2_msleep(10);
02711 
02712         val = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_FW_MB);
02713 
02714         if ((val & BNX2_FW_MSG_ACK) == (msg_data & BNX2_DRV_MSG_SEQ))
02715             break;
02716     }
02717     if ((msg_data & BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA) == BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA_WAIT0)
02718         return 0;
02719 
02720     /* If we timed out, inform the firmware that this is the case. */
02721     if ((val & BNX2_FW_MSG_ACK) != (msg_data & BNX2_DRV_MSG_SEQ)) {
02722         if (!silent)
02723             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "fw sync timeout, reset code = "
02724                         "%x\n", msg_data);
02725 
02726         msg_data &= ~BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE;
