02727         msg_data |= BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_FW_TIMEOUT;
02728 
02729         bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_DRV_MB, msg_data);
02730 
02731         return -EBUSY;
02732     }
02733 
02734     if ((val & BNX2_FW_MSG_STATUS_MASK) != BNX2_FW_MSG_STATUS_OK)
02735         return -EIO;
02736 
02737     return 0;
02738 }
02739 
02740 static int
02741 bnx2_init_5709_context(struct bnx2 *bp)
02742 {
02743     int i, ret = 0;
02744     u32 val;
02745 
02746     val = BNX2_CTX_COMMAND_ENABLED | BNX2_CTX_COMMAND_MEM_INIT | (1 << 12);
02747     val |= (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8) << 16;
02748     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_COMMAND, val);
02749     for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
02750         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_COMMAND);
02751         if (!(val & BNX2_CTX_COMMAND_MEM_INIT))
02752             break;
02753         udelay(2);
02754     }
02755     if (val & BNX2_CTX_COMMAND_MEM_INIT)
02756         return -EBUSY;
02757 
02758     for (i = 0; i < bp->ctx_pages; i++) {
02759         int j;
02760 
02761         if (bp->ctx_blk[i])
02762             memset(bp->ctx_blk[i], 0, BCM_PAGE_SIZE);
02763         else
02764             return -ENOMEM;
02765 
02766         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_DATA0,
02767                (bp->ctx_blk_mapping[i] & 0xffffffff) |
02768                BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_DATA0_VALID);
02769         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_DATA1,
02770                (u64) bp->ctx_blk_mapping[i] >> 32);
02771         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_CTRL, i |
02772                BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_CTRL_WRITE_REQ);
02773         for (j = 0; j < 10; j++) {
02774 
02775             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_CTRL);
02776             if (!(val & BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_CTRL_WRITE_REQ))
02777                 break;
02778             udelay(5);
02779         }
02780         if (val & BNX2_CTX_HOST_PAGE_TBL_CTRL_WRITE_REQ) {
02781             ret = -EBUSY;
02782             break;
02783         }
02784     }
02785     return ret;
02786 }
02787 
02788 static void
02789 bnx2_init_context(struct bnx2 *bp)
02790 {
02791     u32 vcid;
02792 
02793     vcid = 96;
02794     while (vcid) {
02795         u32 vcid_addr, pcid_addr, offset;
02796         int i;
02797 
02798         vcid--;
02799 
02800         if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) {
02801             u32 new_vcid;
02802 
02803             vcid_addr = GET_PCID_ADDR(vcid);
02804             if (vcid & 0x8) {
02805                 new_vcid = 0x60 + (vcid & 0xf0) + (vcid & 0x7);
02806             }
02807             else {
02808                 new_vcid = vcid;
02809             }
02810             pcid_addr = GET_PCID_ADDR(new_vcid);
02811         }
02812         else {
02813                 vcid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(vcid);
02814             pcid_addr = vcid_addr;
02815         }
02816 
02817         for (i = 0; i < (CTX_SIZE / PHY_CTX_SIZE); i++) {
02818             vcid_addr += (i << PHY_CTX_SHIFT);
02819             pcid_addr += (i << PHY_CTX_SHIFT);
02820 
02821             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_VIRT_ADDR, vcid_addr);
02822             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_PAGE_TBL, pcid_addr);
02823 
02824             /* Zero out the context. */
02825             for (offset = 0; offset < PHY_CTX_SIZE; offset += 4)
02826                 bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, vcid_addr, offset, 0);
02827         }
02828     }
02829 }
02830 
02831 static int
02832 bnx2_alloc_bad_rbuf(struct bnx2 *bp)
02833 {
02834     u16 *good_mbuf;
02835     u32 good_mbuf_cnt;
02836     u32 val;
02837 
02838     good_mbuf = kmalloc(512 * sizeof(u16), GFP_KERNEL);
02839     if (good_mbuf == NULL) {
02840         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "Failed to allocate memory in "
02841                     "bnx2_alloc_bad_rbuf\n");
02842         return -ENOMEM;
02843     }
02844 
02845     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS,
02846         BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS_RX_MBUF_ENABLE);
02847 
02848     good_mbuf_cnt = 0;
02849 
02850     /* Allocate a bunch of mbufs and save the good ones in an array. */
02851     val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_STATUS1);
02852     while (val & BNX2_RBUF_STATUS1_FREE_COUNT) {
02853         bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_COMMAND,
02854                 BNX2_RBUF_COMMAND_ALLOC_REQ);
02855 
02856         val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_FW_BUF_ALLOC);
02857 
02858         val &= BNX2_RBUF_FW_BUF_ALLOC_VALUE;
02859 
02860         /* The addresses with Bit 9 set are bad memory blocks. */
02861         if (!(val & (1 << 9))) {
02862             good_mbuf[good_mbuf_cnt] = (u16) val;
02863             good_mbuf_cnt++;
02864         }
02865 
02866         val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_STATUS1);
02867     }
02868 
02869     /* Free the good ones back to the mbuf pool thus discarding
02870      * all the bad ones. */
02871     while (good_mbuf_cnt) {
02872         good_mbuf_cnt--;
02873 
02874         val = good_mbuf[good_mbuf_cnt];
02875         val = (val << 9) | val | 1;
02876 
02877         bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_FW_BUF_FREE, val);
02878     }
02879     kfree(good_mbuf);
02880     return 0;
02881 }
02882 
02883 static void
02884 bnx2_set_mac_addr(struct bnx2 *bp, u8 *mac_addr, u32 pos)
02885 {
02886     u32 val;
02887 
02888     val = (mac_addr[0] << 8) | mac_addr[1];
02889 
02890     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MAC_MATCH0 + (pos * 8), val);
02891 
02892     val = (mac_addr[2] << 24) | (mac_addr[3] << 16) |
02893         (mac_addr[4] << 8) | mac_addr[5];
02894 
02895     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MAC_MATCH1 + (pos * 8), val);
02896 }
02897 
02898 static inline int
02899 bnx2_alloc_rx_page(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr, u16 index)
02900 {
02901     dma_addr_t mapping;
02902     struct sw_pg *rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[index];
02903     struct rx_bd *rxbd =
02904         &rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[RX_RING(index)][RX_IDX(index)];
02905     struct page *page = alloc_page(GFP_ATOMIC);
02906 
02907     if (!page)
02908         return -ENOMEM;
02909     mapping = pci_map_page(bp->pdev, page, 0, PAGE_SIZE,
02910                    PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
02911 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x02061b)
02912     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(bp->pdev, mapping)) {
02913 #else
02914     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(mapping)) {
02915 #endif
02916         __free_page(page);
02917         return -EIO;
02918     }
02919 
02920     rx_pg->page = page;
02921     pci_unmap_addr_set(rx_pg, mapping, mapping);
02922     rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) mapping >> 32;
02923     rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) mapping & 0xffffffff;
02924     return 0;
02925 }
02926 
02927 static void
02928 bnx2_free_rx_page(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr, u16 index)
02929 {
02930     struct sw_pg *rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[index];
02931     struct page *page = rx_pg->page;
02932 
02933     if (!page)
02934         return;
02935 
02936     pci_unmap_page(bp->pdev, pci_unmap_addr(rx_pg, mapping), PAGE_SIZE,
02937                PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
02938 
02939     __free_page(page);
02940     rx_pg->page = NULL;
02941 }
02942 
02943 static inline int
02944 bnx2_alloc_rx_skb(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr, u16 index)
02945 {
02946     struct sk_buff *skb;
02947     struct sw_bd *rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[index];
02948     dma_addr_t mapping;
02949     struct rx_bd *rxbd = &rxr->rx_desc_ring[RX_RING(index)][RX_IDX(index)];
02950     unsigned long align;
02951 
02952     skb = netdev_alloc_skb(bp->dev, bp->rx_buf_size);
02953     if (skb == NULL) {
02954         return -ENOMEM;
02955     }
02956 
02957     if (unlikely((align = (unsigned long) skb->data & (BNX2_RX_ALIGN - 1))))
02958         skb_reserve(skb, BNX2_RX_ALIGN - align);
02959 
02960     mapping = pci_map_single(bp->pdev, skb->data, bp->rx_buf_use_size,
02961         PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
02962 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x02061b)
02963     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(bp->pdev, mapping)) {
02964 #else
02965     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(mapping)) {
02966 #endif
02967         dev_kfree_skb(skb);
02968         return -EIO;
02969     }
02970 
02971     rx_buf->skb = skb;
02972     pci_unmap_addr_set(rx_buf, mapping, mapping);
02973 
02974     rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) mapping >> 32;
02975     rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) mapping & 0xffffffff;
02976 
02977     rxr->rx_prod_bseq += bp->rx_buf_use_size;
02978 
02979     return 0;
02980 }
02981 
02982 static int
02983 bnx2_phy_event_is_set(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi, u32 event)
02984 {
02985     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
02986     u32 new_link_state, old_link_state;
02987     int is_set = 1;
02988 
02989     new_link_state = sblk->status_attn_bits & event;
02990     old_link_state = sblk->status_attn_bits_ack & event;
02991     if (new_link_state != old_link_state) {
02992         if (new_link_state)
02993             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_STATUS_BIT_SET_CMD, event);
02994         else
02995             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_STATUS_BIT_CLEAR_CMD, event);
02996     } else
02997         is_set = 0;
02998 
02999     return is_set;
03000 }
03001 
03002 static void
03003 bnx2_phy_int(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03004 {
03005     spin_lock(&bp->phy_lock);
03006 
03007     if (bnx2_phy_event_is_set(bp, bnapi, STATUS_ATTN_BITS_LINK_STATE))
03008         bnx2_set_link(bp);
03009     if (bnx2_phy_event_is_set(bp, bnapi, STATUS_ATTN_BITS_TIMER_ABORT))
03010         bnx2_set_remote_link(bp);
03011 
03012     spin_unlock(&bp->phy_lock);
03013 
03014 }
03015 
03016 static inline u16
03017 bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03018 {
03019     u16 cons;
03020 
03021     /* Tell compiler that status block fields can change. */
03022     barrier();
03023     cons = *bnapi->hw_tx_cons_ptr;
03024     barrier();
03025     if (unlikely((cons & MAX_TX_DESC_CNT) == MAX_TX_DESC_CNT))
03026         cons++;
03027     return cons;
03028 }
03029 
03030 static int
03031 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
03032 bnx2_tx_int(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi, int budget,
03033         int check_queue)
03034 #else       
03035 bnx2_tx_int(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi, int budget)
03036 #endif
03037 {
03038     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
03039     u16 hw_cons, sw_cons, sw_ring_cons;
03040 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
03041     int tx_pkt = 0;
03042 #else
03043     int tx_pkt = 0, index;
03044     struct netdev_queue *txq;
03045 
03046     index = (bnapi - bp->bnx2_napi);
03047     txq = netdev_get_tx_queue(bp->dev, index);
03048 #endif
03049 
03050     hw_cons = bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi);
03051     sw_cons = txr->tx_cons;
03052 
03053     while (sw_cons != hw_cons) {
03054         struct sw_tx_bd *tx_buf;
03055         struct sk_buff *skb;
03056         int i, last;
03057 
03058         sw_ring_cons = TX_RING_IDX(sw_cons);
03059 
03060         tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[sw_ring_cons];
03061         skb = tx_buf->skb;
03062 
03063         /* prefetch skb_end_pointer() to speedup skb_shinfo(skb) */
03064         prefetch(&skb->end);
03065 
03066 #ifdef BCM_TSO 
03067         /* partial BD completions possible with TSO packets */
03068         if (tx_buf->is_gso) {
03069             u16 last_idx, last_ring_idx;
03070 
03071             last_idx = sw_cons + tx_buf->nr_frags + 1;
03072             last_ring_idx = sw_ring_cons + tx_buf->nr_frags + 1;
03073             if (unlikely(last_ring_idx >= MAX_TX_DESC_CNT)) {
03074                 last_idx++;
03075             }
03076             if (((s16) ((s16) last_idx - (s16) hw_cons)) > 0) {
03077                 break;
03078             }
03079         }
03080 #endif
03081         pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev, pci_unmap_addr(tx_buf, mapping),
03082             skb_headlen(skb), PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
03083 
03084         tx_buf->skb = NULL;
03085         last = tx_buf->nr_frags;
03086 
03087         for (i = 0; i < last; i++) {
03088             sw_cons = NEXT_TX_BD(sw_cons);
03089 
03090             pci_unmap_page(bp->pdev,
03091                 pci_unmap_addr(
03092                     &txr->tx_buf_ring[TX_RING_IDX(sw_cons)],
03093                     mapping),
03094                 skb_shinfo(skb)->frags[i].size,
03095                 PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
03096         }
03097 
03098         sw_cons = NEXT_TX_BD(sw_cons);
03099 
03100         dev_kfree_skb(skb);
03101 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03102         bnapi->stats.tx_packets++;
03103         bnapi->stats.tx_bytes += skb->len;
03104         bnapi->tx_packets_processed++;
03105         wmb();
03106 #endif
03107         tx_pkt++;
03108         if (tx_pkt == budget)
03109             break;
03110 
03111         if (hw_cons == sw_cons)
03112             hw_cons = bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi);
03113     }
03114 
03115     txr->hw_tx_cons = hw_cons;
03116     txr->tx_cons = sw_cons;
03117 
03118     /* Need to make the tx_cons update visible to bnx2_start_xmit()
03119      * before checking for netif_tx_queue_stopped().  Without the
03120      * memory barrier, there is a small possibility that bnx2_start_xmit()
03121      * will miss it and cause the queue to be stopped forever.
03122      */
03123     smp_mb();
03124 
03125 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03126     if ((!check_queue) || (bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_SUSPENDED))
03127         return tx_pkt;
03128 #endif      
03129 
03130 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
03131     if (unlikely(netif_queue_stopped(bp->dev)) &&
03132              (bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) > bp->tx_wake_thresh)) {
03133         netif_tx_lock(bp->dev);
03134         if ((netif_queue_stopped(bp->dev)) &&
03135             (bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) > bp->tx_wake_thresh))
03136             netif_wake_queue(bp->dev);
03137         netif_tx_unlock(bp->dev);
03138     }
03139 #else
03140     if (unlikely(netif_tx_queue_stopped(txq)) &&
03141              (bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) > bp->tx_wake_thresh)) {
03142         __netif_tx_lock(txq, smp_processor_id());
03143         if ((netif_tx_queue_stopped(txq)) &&
03144             (bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) > bp->tx_wake_thresh))
03145             netif_tx_wake_queue(txq);
03146         __netif_tx_unlock(txq);
03147     }
03148 #endif
03149     return tx_pkt;
03150 }
03151 
03152 static void
03153 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb_pages(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr,
03154             struct sk_buff *skb, int count)
03155 {
03156     struct sw_pg *cons_rx_pg, *prod_rx_pg;
03157     struct rx_bd *cons_bd, *prod_bd;
03158     int i;
03159     u16 hw_prod, prod;
03160     u16 cons = rxr->rx_pg_cons;
03161 
03162     cons_rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[cons];
03163 
03164     /* The caller was unable to allocate a new page to replace the
03165      * last one in the frags array, so we need to recycle that page
03166      * and then free the skb.
03167      */
03168     if (skb) {
03169         struct page *page;
03170         struct skb_shared_info *shinfo;
03171 
03172         shinfo = skb_shinfo(skb);
03173         shinfo->nr_frags--;
03174         page = shinfo->frags[shinfo->nr_frags].page;
03175         shinfo->frags[shinfo->nr_frags].page = NULL;
03176 
03177         cons_rx_pg->page = page;
03178         dev_kfree_skb(skb);
03179     }
03180 
03181     hw_prod = rxr->rx_pg_prod;
03182 
03183     for (i = 0; i < count; i++) {
03184         prod = RX_PG_RING_IDX(hw_prod);
03185 
03186         prod_rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[prod];
03187         cons_rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[cons];
03188         cons_bd = &rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[RX_RING(cons)][RX_IDX(cons)];
03189         prod_bd = &rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring[RX_RING(prod)][RX_IDX(prod)];
03190 
03191         if (prod != cons) {
03192             prod_rx_pg->page = cons_rx_pg->page;
03193             cons_rx_pg->page = NULL;
03194             pci_unmap_addr_set(prod_rx_pg, mapping,
03195                 pci_unmap_addr(cons_rx_pg, mapping));
03196 
03197             prod_bd->rx_bd_haddr_hi = cons_bd->rx_bd_haddr_hi;
03198             prod_bd->rx_bd_haddr_lo = cons_bd->rx_bd_haddr_lo;
03199 
03200         }
03201         cons = RX_PG_RING_IDX(NEXT_RX_BD(cons));
03202         hw_prod = NEXT_RX_BD(hw_prod);
03203     }
03204     rxr->rx_pg_prod = hw_prod;
03205     rxr->rx_pg_cons = cons;
03206 }
03207 
03208 static inline void
03209 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr,
03210           struct sk_buff *skb, u16 cons, u16 prod)
03211 {
03212     struct sw_bd *cons_rx_buf, *prod_rx_buf;
03213     struct rx_bd *cons_bd, *prod_bd;
03214 
03215     cons_rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[cons];
03216     prod_rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[prod];
03217 
03218     pci_dma_sync_single_for_device(bp->pdev,
03219         pci_unmap_addr(cons_rx_buf, mapping),
03220         BNX2_RX_OFFSET + BNX2_RX_COPY_THRESH, PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
03221 
03222     rxr->rx_prod_bseq += bp->rx_buf_use_size;
03223 
03224     prod_rx_buf->skb = skb;
03225 
03226     if (cons == prod)
03227         return;
03228 
03229     pci_unmap_addr_set(prod_rx_buf, mapping,
03230             pci_unmap_addr(cons_rx_buf, mapping));
03231 
03232     cons_bd = &rxr->rx_desc_ring[RX_RING(cons)][RX_IDX(cons)];
03233     prod_bd = &rxr->rx_desc_ring[RX_RING(prod)][RX_IDX(prod)];
03234     prod_bd->rx_bd_haddr_hi = cons_bd->rx_bd_haddr_hi;
03235     prod_bd->rx_bd_haddr_lo = cons_bd->rx_bd_haddr_lo;
03236 }
03237 
03238 static int
03239 bnx2_rx_skb(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr, struct sk_buff *skb,
03240         unsigned int len, unsigned int hdr_len, dma_addr_t dma_addr,
03241         u32 ring_idx)
03242 {
03243     int err;
03244     u16 prod = ring_idx & 0xffff;
03245 
03246     err = bnx2_alloc_rx_skb(bp, rxr, prod);
03247     if (unlikely(err)) {
03248         bnx2_reuse_rx_skb(bp, rxr, skb, (u16) (ring_idx >> 16), prod);
03249         if (hdr_len) {
03250             unsigned int raw_len = len + 4;
03251             int pages = PAGE_ALIGN(raw_len - hdr_len) >> PAGE_SHIFT;
03252 
03253             bnx2_reuse_rx_skb_pages(bp, rxr, NULL, pages);
03254         }
03255         return err;
03256     }
03257 
03258     skb_reserve(skb, BNX2_RX_OFFSET);
03259     pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev, dma_addr, bp->rx_buf_use_size,
03260              PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
03261 
03262     if (hdr_len == 0) {
03263         skb_put(skb, len);
03264         return 0;
03265     } else {
03266         unsigned int i, frag_len, frag_size, pages;
03267         struct sw_pg *rx_pg;
03268         u16 pg_cons = rxr->rx_pg_cons;
03269         u16 pg_prod = rxr->rx_pg_prod;
03270 
03271         frag_size = len + 4 - hdr_len;
03272         pages = PAGE_ALIGN(frag_size) >> PAGE_SHIFT;
03273         skb_put(skb, hdr_len);
03274 
03275         for (i = 0; i < pages; i++) {
03276             dma_addr_t mapping_old;
03277 
03278             frag_len = min(frag_size, (unsigned int) PAGE_SIZE);
03279             if (unlikely(frag_len <= 4)) {
03280                 unsigned int tail = 4 - frag_len;
03281 
03282                 rxr->rx_pg_cons = pg_cons;
03283                 rxr->rx_pg_prod = pg_prod;
03284                 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb_pages(bp, rxr, NULL,
03285                             pages - i);
03286                 skb->len -= tail;
03287                 if (i == 0) {
03288                     skb->tail -= tail;
03289                 } else {
03290                     skb_frag_t *frag =
03291                         &skb_shinfo(skb)->frags[i - 1];
03292                     frag->size -= tail;
03293                     skb->data_len -= tail;
03294                     skb->truesize -= tail;
03295                 }
03296                 return 0;
03297             }
03298             rx_pg = &rxr->rx_pg_ring[pg_cons];
03299 
03300             /* Don't unmap yet.  If we're unable to allocate a new
03301              * page, we need to recycle the page and the DMA addr.
03302              */
03303             mapping_old = pci_unmap_addr(rx_pg, mapping);
03304             if (i == pages - 1)
03305                 frag_len -= 4;
03306 
03307             bnx2_skb_fill_page_desc(skb, i, rx_pg->page, 0,
03308                         frag_len);
03309             rx_pg->page = NULL;
03310 
03311             err = bnx2_alloc_rx_page(bp, rxr,
03312                          RX_PG_RING_IDX(pg_prod));
03313             if (unlikely(err)) {
03314                 rxr->rx_pg_cons = pg_cons;
03315                 rxr->rx_pg_prod = pg_prod;
03316                 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb_pages(bp, rxr, skb,
03317                             pages - i);
03318                 return err;
03319             }
03320 
03321             pci_unmap_page(bp->pdev, mapping_old,
03322                        PAGE_SIZE, PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
03323 
03324             frag_size -= frag_len;
03325             skb->data_len += frag_len;
03326             skb->truesize += frag_len;
03327             skb->len += frag_len;
03328 
03329             pg_prod = NEXT_RX_BD(pg_prod);
03330             pg_cons = RX_PG_RING_IDX(NEXT_RX_BD(pg_cons));
03331         }
03332         rxr->rx_pg_prod = pg_prod;
03333         rxr->rx_pg_cons = pg_cons;
03334     }
03335     return 0;
03336 }
03337 
03338 static inline u16
03339 bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03340 {
03341     u16 cons;
03342 
03343     /* Tell compiler that status block fields can change. */
03344     barrier();
03345     cons = *bnapi->hw_rx_cons_ptr;
03346     barrier();
03347     if (unlikely((cons & MAX_RX_DESC_CNT) == MAX_RX_DESC_CNT))
03348         cons++;
03349     return cons;
03350 }
03351 
03352 static int
03353 bnx2_rx_int(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi, int budget)
03354 {
03355     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
03356     u16 hw_cons, sw_cons, sw_ring_cons, sw_prod, sw_ring_prod;
03357     struct l2_fhdr *rx_hdr;
03358     int rx_pkt = 0, pg_ring_used = 0;
03359 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03360     int index = (bnapi - bp->bnx2_napi);
03361 #endif
03362 
03363     hw_cons = bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi);
03364     sw_cons = rxr->rx_cons;
03365     sw_prod = rxr->rx_prod;
03366 
03367     /* Memory barrier necessary as speculative reads of the rx
03368      * buffer can be ahead of the index in the status block
03369      */
03370     rmb();
03371     while (sw_cons != hw_cons) {
03372         unsigned int len, hdr_len;
03373         u32 status;
03374         struct sw_bd *rx_buf;
03375         struct sk_buff *skb;
03376         dma_addr_t dma_addr;
03377         u16 vtag = 0;
03378         int hw_vlan __maybe_unused = 0;
03379 
03380         sw_ring_cons = RX_RING_IDX(sw_cons);
03381         sw_ring_prod = RX_RING_IDX(sw_prod);
03382 
03383         rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[sw_ring_cons];
03384         skb = rx_buf->skb;
03385 
03386         rx_buf->skb = NULL;
03387 
03388         dma_addr = pci_unmap_addr(rx_buf, mapping);
03389 
03390         pci_dma_sync_single_for_cpu(bp->pdev, dma_addr,
03391             BNX2_RX_OFFSET + BNX2_RX_COPY_THRESH,
03392             PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
03393 
03394         rx_hdr = (struct l2_fhdr *) skb->data;
03395         len = rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_pkt_len;
03396         status = rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_status;
03397 
03398         hdr_len = 0;
03399         if (status & L2_FHDR_STATUS_SPLIT) {
03400             hdr_len = rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_ip_xsum;
03401             pg_ring_used = 1;
03402         } else if (len > bp->rx_jumbo_thresh) {
03403             hdr_len = bp->rx_jumbo_thresh;
03404             pg_ring_used = 1;
03405         }
03406 
03407         if (unlikely(status & (L2_FHDR_ERRORS_BAD_CRC |
03408                        L2_FHDR_ERRORS_PHY_DECODE |
03409                        L2_FHDR_ERRORS_ALIGNMENT |
03410                        L2_FHDR_ERRORS_TOO_SHORT |
03411                        L2_FHDR_ERRORS_GIANT_FRAME))) {
03412 
03413 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03414             bnapi->stats.rx_errors++;
03415 
03416             if (status & L2_FHDR_ERRORS_BAD_CRC)
03417                 bnapi->stats.rx_crc_errors++;
03418 
03419             if (status &
03420                  (L2_FHDR_ERRORS_TOO_SHORT |
03421                   L2_FHDR_ERRORS_GIANT_FRAME))
03422                 bnapi->stats.rx_frame_errors++;
03423 #endif
03424 
03425             bnx2_reuse_rx_skb(bp, rxr, skb, sw_ring_cons,
03426                       sw_ring_prod);
03427             if (pg_ring_used) {
03428                 int pages;
03429 
03430                 pages = PAGE_ALIGN(len - hdr_len) >> PAGE_SHIFT;
03431 
03432                 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb_pages(bp, rxr, NULL, pages);
03433             }
03434             goto next_rx;
03435         }
03436 
03437         len -= 4;
03438 
03439         if (len <= bp->rx_copy_thresh) {
03440             struct sk_buff *new_skb;
03441 
03442             new_skb = netdev_alloc_skb(bp->dev, len + 6);
03443             if (new_skb == NULL) {
03444                 bnx2_reuse_rx_skb(bp, rxr, skb, sw_ring_cons,
03445                           sw_ring_prod);
03446                 goto next_rx;
03447             }
03448 
03449             /* aligned copy */
03450 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20616)
03451             skb_copy_from_linear_data_offset(skb,
03452                              BNX2_RX_OFFSET - 6,
03453                       new_skb->data, len + 6);
03454 #else
03455             memcpy(new_skb->data, skb->data + BNX2_RX_OFFSET - 6,
03456                    len + 6);
03457 #endif
03458 
03459             skb_reserve(new_skb, 6);
03460             skb_put(new_skb, len);
03461 
03462             bnx2_reuse_rx_skb(bp, rxr, skb,
03463                 sw_ring_cons, sw_ring_prod);
03464 
03465             skb = new_skb;
03466         } else if (unlikely(bnx2_rx_skb(bp, rxr, skb, len, hdr_len,
03467                dma_addr, (sw_ring_cons << 16) | sw_ring_prod)))
03468             goto next_rx;
03469 
03470         if ((status & L2_FHDR_STATUS_L2_VLAN_TAG) &&
03471             !(bp->rx_mode & BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_KEEP_VLAN_TAG)) {
03472             vtag = rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_vlan_tag;
03473 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
03474             if (bp->vlgrp)
03475                 hw_vlan = 1;
03476             else
03477 #endif
03478             {
03479                 struct vlan_ethhdr *ve = (struct vlan_ethhdr *)
03480                     __skb_push(skb, 4);
03481 
03482                 bcm_memmove(ve, skb->data + 4, ETH_ALEN * 2);
03483                 ve->h_vlan_proto = htons(ETH_P_8021Q);
03484                 ve->h_vlan_TCI = htons(vtag);
03485                 len += 4;
03486             }
03487         }
03488 
03489         skb->protocol = eth_type_trans(skb, bp->dev);
03490 
03491         if ((len > (bp->dev->mtu + ETH_HLEN)) &&
03492             (ntohs(skb->protocol) != 0x8100)) {
03493 
03494             dev_kfree_skb(skb);
03495             goto next_rx;
03496 
03497         }
03498 
03499         skb->ip_summed = CHECKSUM_NONE;
03500         if (bp->rx_csum &&
03501             (status & (L2_FHDR_STATUS_TCP_SEGMENT |
03502             L2_FHDR_STATUS_UDP_DATAGRAM))) {
03503 
03504             if (likely((status & (L2_FHDR_ERRORS_TCP_XSUM |
03505                           L2_FHDR_ERRORS_UDP_XSUM)) == 0))
03506                 skb->ip_summed = CHECKSUM_UNNECESSARY;
03507         }
03508 
03509         skb_record_rx_queue(skb, bnapi - &bp->bnx2_napi[0]);
03510 
03511 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03512         vmknetddi_queueops_set_skb_queueid(skb,
03513                 VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_RX_QUEUEID(index));
03514 #endif
03515 
03516 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
03517         if (hw_vlan)
03518             vlan_hwaccel_receive_skb(skb, bp->vlgrp, vtag);
03519         else
03520 #endif
03521             netif_receive_skb(skb);
03522 
03523 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x02061b) || defined(__VMKLNX__)
03524         bp->dev->last_rx = jiffies;
03525 #endif
03526         rx_pkt++;
03527 
03528 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03529         /*  Update queue specific stats */
03530         bnapi->stats.rx_packets++;
03531         bnapi->stats.rx_bytes += len;
03532 #endif
03533 
03534 next_rx:
03535         sw_cons = NEXT_RX_BD(sw_cons);
03536         sw_prod = NEXT_RX_BD(sw_prod);
03537 
03538         if ((rx_pkt == budget))
03539             break;
03540 
03541         /* Refresh hw_cons to see if there is new work */
03542         if (sw_cons == hw_cons) {
03543             hw_cons = bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi);
03544             rmb();
03545         }
03546     }
03547     rxr->rx_cons = sw_cons;
03548     rxr->rx_prod = sw_prod;
03549 
03550     if (pg_ring_used)
03551         REG_WR16(bp, rxr->rx_pg_bidx_addr, rxr->rx_pg_prod);
03552 
03553     REG_WR16(bp, rxr->rx_bidx_addr, sw_prod);
03554 
03555     REG_WR(bp, rxr->rx_bseq_addr, rxr->rx_prod_bseq);
03556 
03557     mmiowb();
03558 
03559     return rx_pkt;
03560 
03561 }
03562 
03563 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
03564 /* MSI ISR - The only difference between this and the INTx ISR
03565  * is that the MSI interrupt is always serviced.
03566  */
03567 static irqreturn_t
03568 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20613)
03569 bnx2_msi(int irq, void *dev_instance)
03570 #else
03571 bnx2_msi(int irq, void *dev_instance, struct pt_regs *regs)
03572 #endif
03573 {
03574     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = dev_instance;
03575     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
03576 
03577     prefetch(bnapi->status_blk.msi);
03578     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03579         BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_USE_INT_HC_PARAM |
03580         BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT);
03581 
03582     /* Return here if interrupt is disabled. */
03583     if (unlikely(atomic_read(&bp->intr_sem) != 0))
03584         return IRQ_HANDLED;
03585 
03586 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
03587     napi_schedule(&bnapi->napi);
03588 #else
03589     netif_rx_schedule(bp->dev);
03590 #endif
03591 
03592     return IRQ_HANDLED;
03593 }
03594 
03595 static irqreturn_t
03596 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20613)
03597 bnx2_msi_1shot(int irq, void *dev_instance)
03598 #else
03599 bnx2_msi_1shot(int irq, void *dev_instance, struct pt_regs *regs)
03600 #endif
03601 {
03602     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = dev_instance;
03603     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
03604 
03605     prefetch(bnapi->status_blk.msi);
03606 
03607     /* Return here if interrupt is disabled. */
03608     if (unlikely(atomic_read(&bp->intr_sem) != 0))
03609         return IRQ_HANDLED;
03610 
03611 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
03612     napi_schedule(&bnapi->napi);
03613 #else
03614     netif_rx_schedule(bp->dev);
03615 #endif
03616 
03617     return IRQ_HANDLED;
03618 }
03619 #endif
03620 
03621 static irqreturn_t
03622 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20613)
03623 bnx2_interrupt(int irq, void *dev_instance)
03624 #else
03625 bnx2_interrupt(int irq, void *dev_instance, struct pt_regs *regs)
03626 #endif
03627 {
03628     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = dev_instance;
03629     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
03630     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
03631 
03632     /* When using INTx, it is possible for the interrupt to arrive
03633      * at the CPU before the status block posted prior to the
03634      * interrupt. Reading a register will flush the status block.
03635      * When using MSI, the MSI message will always complete after
03636      * the status block write.
03637      */
03638     if ((sblk->status_idx == bnapi->last_status_idx) &&
03639         (REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS) &
03640          BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS_INTA_VALUE))
03641         return IRQ_NONE;
03642 
03643     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03644         BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_USE_INT_HC_PARAM |
03645         BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT);
03646 
03647     /* Read back to deassert IRQ immediately to avoid too many
03648      * spurious interrupts.
03649      */
03650     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD);
03651 
03652     /* Return here if interrupt is shared and is disabled. */
03653     if (unlikely(atomic_read(&bp->intr_sem) != 0))
03654         return IRQ_HANDLED;
03655 
03656 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
03657     if (napi_schedule_prep(&bnapi->napi)) {
03658         bnapi->last_status_idx = sblk->status_idx;
03659         __napi_schedule(&bnapi->napi);
03660     }
03661 #else
03662     if (netif_rx_schedule_prep(bp->dev)) {
03663         bnapi->last_status_idx = sblk->status_idx;
03664         __netif_rx_schedule(bp->dev);
03665     }
03666 #endif
03667 
03668     return IRQ_HANDLED;
03669 }
03670 
03671 static inline int
03672 bnx2_has_fast_work(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03673 {
03674     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
03675     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
03676 
03677     if ((bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi) != rxr->rx_cons) ||
03678         (bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi) != txr->hw_tx_cons))
03679         return 1;
03680     return 0;
03681 }
03682 
03683 #define STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS  (STATUS_ATTN_BITS_LINK_STATE | \
03684                  STATUS_ATTN_BITS_TIMER_ABORT)
03685 
03686 static inline int
03687 bnx2_has_work(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03688 {
03689     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
03690 
03691     if (bnx2_has_fast_work(bnapi))
03692         return 1;
03693 
03694 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
03695     if (bnapi->cnic_present && (bnapi->cnic_tag != sblk->status_idx))
03696         return 1;
03697 #endif
03698 
03699     if ((sblk->status_attn_bits & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS) !=
03700         (sblk->status_attn_bits_ack & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS))
03701         return 1;
03702 
03703     return 0;
03704 }
03705 
03706 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
03707 static void
03708 bnx2_chk_missed_msi(struct bnx2 *bp)
03709 {
03710     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
03711     u32 msi_ctrl;
03712 
03713     if (bnx2_has_work(bnapi)) {
03714         msi_ctrl = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MSI_CONTROL);
03715         if (!(msi_ctrl & BNX2_PCICFG_MSI_CONTROL_ENABLE))
03716             return;
03717 
03718         if (bnapi->last_status_idx == bp->idle_chk_status_idx) {
03719             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MSI_CONTROL, msi_ctrl &
03720                    ~BNX2_PCICFG_MSI_CONTROL_ENABLE);
03721             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MSI_CONTROL, msi_ctrl);
03722 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20613)
03723             bnx2_msi(bp->irq_tbl[0].vector, bnapi);
03724 #else
03725             bnx2_msi(bp->irq_tbl[0].vector, bnapi, NULL);
03726 #endif
03727         }
03728     }
03729 
03730     bp->idle_chk_status_idx = bnapi->last_status_idx;
03731 }
03732 #endif
03733 
03734 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
03735 static void bnx2_poll_cnic(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03736 {
03737     struct cnic_ops *c_ops;
03738 
03739     if (!bnapi->cnic_present)
03740         return;
03741 
03742     rcu_read_lock();
03743     c_ops = rcu_dereference(bp->cnic_ops);
03744     if (c_ops)
03745         bnapi->cnic_tag = c_ops->cnic_handler(bp->cnic_data,
03746                               bnapi->status_blk.msi);
03747     rcu_read_unlock();
03748 }
03749 #endif
03750 
03751 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
03752 static void bnx2_poll_link(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
03753 {
03754     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
03755     u32 status_attn_bits = sblk->status_attn_bits;
03756     u32 status_attn_bits_ack = sblk->status_attn_bits_ack;
03757 
03758     if ((status_attn_bits & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS) !=
03759         (status_attn_bits_ack & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS)) {
03760 
03761         bnx2_phy_int(bp, bnapi);
03762 
03763         /* This is needed to take care of transient status
03764          * during link changes.
03765          */
03766         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND,
03767                bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW_WO_INT);
03768         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
03769     }
03770 }
03771 
03772 static int bnx2_poll_work(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi,
03773               int work_done, int budget)
03774 {
03775     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
03776     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
03777 
03778     if (bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi) != txr->hw_tx_cons)
03779 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
03780         bnx2_tx_int(bp, bnapi, 0, 1);
03781 #else
03782         bnx2_tx_int(bp, bnapi, 0);
03783 #endif
03784 
03785     if (bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi) != rxr->rx_cons)
03786         work_done += bnx2_rx_int(bp, bnapi, budget - work_done);
03787 
03788     wmb();
03789     return work_done;
03790 }
03791 
03792 static int bnx2_poll_msix(struct napi_struct *napi, int budget)
03793 {
03794     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = container_of(napi, struct bnx2_napi, napi);
03795     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
03796     int work_done = 0;
03797     struct status_block_msix *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msix;
03798 
03799     while (1) {
03800         work_done = bnx2_poll_work(bp, bnapi, work_done, budget);
03801         if (unlikely(work_done >= budget))
03802             break;
03803 
03804         bnapi->last_status_idx = sblk->status_idx;
03805         /* status idx must be read before checking for more work. */
03806         rmb();
03807         if (likely(!bnx2_has_fast_work(bnapi))) {
03808 
03809             napi_complete(napi);
03810             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD, bnapi->int_num |
03811                    BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03812                    bnapi->last_status_idx);
03813             break;
03814         }
03815     }
03816     return work_done;
03817 }
03818 
03819 static int bnx2_poll(struct napi_struct *napi, int budget)
03820 {
03821     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = container_of(napi, struct bnx2_napi, napi);
03822     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
03823     int work_done = 0;
03824     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
03825 
03826     while (1) {
03827         bnx2_poll_link(bp, bnapi);
03828 
03829         work_done = bnx2_poll_work(bp, bnapi, work_done, budget);
03830 
03831 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
03832         if (bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp) &&
03833             (bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED))
03834             bnx2_netqueue_service_bnx2_msix(bnapi);
03835 #endif
03836 
03837 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
03838         bnx2_poll_cnic(bp, bnapi);
03839 #endif
03840 
03841         /* bnapi->last_status_idx is used below to tell the hw how
03842          * much work has been processed, so we must read it before
03843          * checking for more work.
03844          */
03845         bnapi->last_status_idx = sblk->status_idx;
03846 
03847         if (unlikely(work_done >= budget))
03848             break;
03849 
03850         rmb();
03851         if (likely(!bnx2_has_work(bnapi))) {
03852             napi_complete(napi);
03853             if (likely(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI_OR_MSIX)) {
03854                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03855                        BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03856                        bnapi->last_status_idx);
03857                 break;
03858             }
03859             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03860                    BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03861                    BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT |
03862                    bnapi->last_status_idx);
03863 
03864             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03865                    BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03866                    bnapi->last_status_idx);
03867             break;
03868         }
03869     }
03870 
03871     return work_done;
03872 }
03873 
03874 #else
03875 
03876 static int
03877 bnx2_poll(struct net_device *dev, int *budget)
03878 {
03879     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
03880     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
03881     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
03882     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
03883     struct status_block *sblk = bnapi->status_blk.msi;
03884     u32 status_attn_bits = sblk->status_attn_bits;
03885     u32 status_attn_bits_ack = sblk->status_attn_bits_ack;
03886 
03887     if ((status_attn_bits & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS) !=
03888         (status_attn_bits_ack & STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS)) {
03889 
03890         bnx2_phy_int(bp, bnapi);
03891 
03892         /* This is needed to take care of transient status
03893          * during link changes.
03894          */
03895         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND,
03896                bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW_WO_INT);
03897         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
03898     }
03899 
03900     if (bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(bnapi) != txr->hw_tx_cons)
03901 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
03902         bnx2_tx_int(bp, bnapi, 0, 1);
03903 #else
03904         bnx2_tx_int(bp, bnapi, 0);
03905 #endif
03906 
03907     if (bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi) != rxr->rx_cons) {
03908         int orig_budget = *budget;
03909         int work_done;
03910 
03911         if (orig_budget > dev->quota)
03912             orig_budget = dev->quota;
03913 
03914         work_done = bnx2_rx_int(bp, bnapi, orig_budget);
03915         *budget -= work_done;
03916         dev->quota -= work_done;
03917     }
03918 
03919 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
03920     bnx2_poll_cnic(bp, bnapi);
03921 #endif
03922 
03923     bnapi->last_status_idx = sblk->status_idx;
03924     rmb();
03925 
03926     if (!bnx2_has_work(bnapi)) {
03927         netif_rx_complete(dev);
03928         if (likely(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI_OR_MSIX)) {
03929             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03930                    BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03931                    bnapi->last_status_idx);
03932             return 0;
03933         }
03934         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03935                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03936                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT |
03937                bnapi->last_status_idx);
03938 
03939         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD,
03940                BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_INDEX_VALID |
03941                bnapi->last_status_idx);
03942         return 0;
03943     }
03944 
03945     return 1;
03946 }
03947 #endif
03948 
03949 /* Called with rtnl_lock from vlan functions and also netif_tx_lock
03950  * from set_multicast.
03951  */
03952 static void
03953 bnx2_set_rx_mode(struct net_device *dev)
03954 {
03955     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
03956     u32 rx_mode, sort_mode;
03957 #ifdef HAVE_SET_RX_MODE
03958 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x2061f)
03959     struct netdev_hw_addr *ha;
03960 #else
03961     struct dev_addr_list *uc_ptr;
03962 #endif
03963 #endif
03964     int i;
03965 
03966     if (!netif_running(dev))
03967         return;
03968 
03969     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
03970 
03971     rx_mode = bp->rx_mode & ~(BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_PROMISCUOUS |
03972                   BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_KEEP_VLAN_TAG);
03973     sort_mode = 1 | BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_BC_EN;
03974 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
03975     if (!bp->vlgrp && (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN))
03976         rx_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_KEEP_VLAN_TAG;
03977 #else
03978     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN)
03979         rx_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_KEEP_VLAN_TAG;
03980 #endif
03981     if (dev->flags & IFF_PROMISC) {
03982         /* Promiscuous mode. */
03983         rx_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_PROMISCUOUS;
03984         sort_mode |= BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_PROM_EN |
03985                  BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_PROM_VLAN;
03986     }
03987     else if (dev->flags & IFF_ALLMULTI) {
03988         for (i = 0; i < NUM_MC_HASH_REGISTERS; i++) {
03989             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MULTICAST_HASH0 + (i * 4),
03990                    0xffffffff);
03991             }
03992         sort_mode |= BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_MC_EN;
03993     }
03994     else {
03995         /* Accept one or more multicast(s). */
03996         struct dev_mc_list *mclist;
03997         u32 mc_filter[NUM_MC_HASH_REGISTERS];
03998         u32 regidx;
03999         u32 bit;
04000         u32 crc;
04001 
04002         memset(mc_filter, 0, 4 * NUM_MC_HASH_REGISTERS);
04003 
04004         for (i = 0, mclist = dev->mc_list; mclist && i < dev->mc_count;
04005              i++, mclist = mclist->next) {
04006 
04007             crc = ether_crc_le(ETH_ALEN, mclist->dmi_addr);
04008             bit = crc & 0xff;
04009             regidx = (bit & 0xe0) >> 5;
04010             bit &= 0x1f;
04011             mc_filter[regidx] |= (1 << bit);
04012         }
04013 
04014         for (i = 0; i < NUM_MC_HASH_REGISTERS; i++) {
04015             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MULTICAST_HASH0 + (i * 4),
04016                    mc_filter[i]);
04017         }
04018 
04019         sort_mode |= BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_MC_HSH_EN;
04020     }
04021 
04022 #ifdef HAVE_SET_RX_MODE
04023 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x2061f)
04024     if (dev->uc_count > BNX2_MAX_UNICAST_ADDRESSES) {
04025 #else
04026     if (dev->uc.count > BNX2_MAX_UNICAST_ADDRESSES) {
04027 #endif
04028         rx_mode |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_PROMISCUOUS;
04029         sort_mode |= BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_PROM_EN |
04030                  BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_PROM_VLAN;
04031     } else if (!(dev->flags & IFF_PROMISC)) {
04032 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x2061f)
04033         uc_ptr = dev->uc_list;
04034 
04035         /* Add all entries into to the match filter list */
04036         for (i = 0; i < dev->uc_count; i++) {
04037             bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, uc_ptr->da_addr,
04038                       i + BNX2_START_UNICAST_ADDRESS_INDEX);
04039             sort_mode |= (1 <<
04040                       (i + BNX2_START_UNICAST_ADDRESS_INDEX));
04041             uc_ptr = uc_ptr->next;
04042         }
04043 #else
04044         i = 0;
04045         list_for_each_entry(ha, &dev->uc.list, list) {
04046             bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, ha->addr,
04047                       i + BNX2_START_UNICAST_ADDRESS_INDEX);
04048             sort_mode |= (1 <<
04049                       (i + BNX2_START_UNICAST_ADDRESS_INDEX));
04050             i++;
04051         }
04052 #endif
04053     }
04054 #endif
04055 
04056     if (rx_mode != bp->rx_mode) {
04057         bp->rx_mode = rx_mode;
04058         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE, rx_mode);
04059     }
04060 
04061     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, 0x0);
04062     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, sort_mode);
04063     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, sort_mode | BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_ENA);
04064 
04065     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
04066 }
04067 
04068 #define FW_BUF_SIZE 0x10000
04069 
04070 static int
04071 bnx2_gunzip_init(struct bnx2 *bp)
04072 {
04073     if ((bp->gunzip_buf = vmalloc(FW_BUF_SIZE)) == NULL)
04074         goto gunzip_nomem1;
04075 
04076     if ((bp->strm = kmalloc(sizeof(*bp->strm), GFP_KERNEL)) == NULL)
04077         goto gunzip_nomem2;
04078 
04079     bp->strm->workspace = kmalloc(zlib_inflate_workspacesize(), GFP_KERNEL);
04080     if (bp->strm->workspace == NULL)
04081         goto gunzip_nomem3;
04082 
04083     return 0;
04084 
04085 gunzip_nomem3:
04086     kfree(bp->strm);
04087     bp->strm = NULL;
04088 
04089 gunzip_nomem2:
04090     vfree(bp->gunzip_buf);
04091     bp->gunzip_buf = NULL;
04092 
04093 gunzip_nomem1:
04094     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: Cannot allocate firmware buffer for "
04095                 "uncompression.\n", bp->dev->name);
04096     return -ENOMEM;
04097 }
04098 
04099 static void
04100 bnx2_gunzip_end(struct bnx2 *bp)
04101 {
04102     kfree(bp->strm->workspace);
04103 
04104     kfree(bp->strm);
04105     bp->strm = NULL;
04106 
04107     if (bp->gunzip_buf) {
04108         vfree(bp->gunzip_buf);
04109         bp->gunzip_buf = NULL;
04110     }
04111 }
04112 
04113 static int
04114 bnx2_gunzip(struct bnx2 *bp, const u8 *zbuf,
04115         int len, void **outbuf, int *outlen)
04116 {
04117     int rc;
04118 
04119     bp->strm->next_in = zbuf;
04120     bp->strm->avail_in = len;
04121     bp->strm->next_out = bp->gunzip_buf;
04122     bp->strm->avail_out = FW_BUF_SIZE;
04123 
04124     rc = zlib_inflateInit2(bp->strm, -MAX_WBITS);
04125     if (rc != Z_OK)
04126         return rc;
04127 
04128     rc = zlib_inflate(bp->strm, Z_FINISH);
04129 
04130     *outlen = FW_BUF_SIZE - bp->strm->avail_out;
04131     *outbuf = bp->gunzip_buf;
04132 
04133     if ((rc != Z_OK) && (rc != Z_STREAM_END))
04134         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: Firmware decompression error: %s\n",
04135                bp->dev->name, bp->strm->msg);
04136 
04137     zlib_inflateEnd(bp->strm);
04138 
04139     if (rc == Z_STREAM_END)
04140         return 0;
04141 
04142     return rc;
04143 }
04144 
04145 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
04146 struct bnx2_cpus_scratch_debug {
04147     u32 offset;     /*  Scratch pad offset to firmware version */
04148     char    *name;      /*  Name of the CPU */
04149 };
04150 
04151 #define BNX2_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET      0x10
04152 #define BNX2_TPAT_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET 0x410
04153 
04154 static void
04155 bnx2_print_fw_versions(struct bnx2 *bp)
04156 {
04157     /*  Array of the firmware offset's + CPU strings */
04158     const struct bnx2_cpus_scratch_debug cpus_scratch[] = {
04159         { .offset = BNX2_TXP_SCRATCH + BNX2_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET,
04160           .name   = "TXP" },
04161         { .offset = BNX2_TPAT_SCRATCH +
04162                 BNX2_TPAT_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET,
04163           .name   = "TPAT" },
04164         { .offset = BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH + BNX2_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET,
04165           .name   = "RXP" },
04166         { .offset = BNX2_COM_SCRATCH + BNX2_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET,
04167           .name   = "COM" },
04168         { .offset = BNX2_CP_SCRATCH + BNX2_SCRATCH_FW_VERSION_OFFSET,
04169           .name   = "CP" },
04170         /* There is no versioning for MCP firmware */
04171     };
04172     int i;
04173 
04174     printk(KERN_INFO "bnx2 %s: CPU fw versions: ",
04175            bp->dev->name);
04176     for (i = 0; i < ARRAY_SIZE(cpus_scratch); i++) {
04177         /*  The FW versions are 11 bytes long + 1 extra byte for
04178          *  the NULL termination */
04179         char version[12];
04180         int j;
04181 
04182         /*  Copy 4 bytes at a time */
04183         for (j = 0; j < sizeof(version); j += 4) {
04184             u32 val;
04185 
04186             val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, cpus_scratch[i].offset + j);
04187             val = be32_to_cpu(val);
04188             memcpy(&version[j], &val, sizeof(val));
04189         }
04190 
04191         /*  Force a NULL terminiated string */
04192         version[11] = '\0';
04193 
04194         printk("%s: '%s' ", cpus_scratch[i].name, version);
04195     }
04196     printk("\n");
04197 }
04198 #endif
04199 
04200 static u32
04201 rv2p_fw_fixup(u32 rv2p_proc, int idx, u32 loc, u32 rv2p_code)
04202 {
04203     switch (idx) {
04204     case RV2P_P1_FIXUP_PAGE_SIZE_IDX:
04205         rv2p_code &= ~RV2P_BD_PAGE_SIZE_MSK;
04206         rv2p_code |= RV2P_BD_PAGE_SIZE;
04207         break;
04208     }
04209     return rv2p_code;
04210 }
04211 
04212 static void
04213 load_rv2p_fw(struct bnx2 *bp, __le32 *rv2p_code, u32 rv2p_code_len,
04214     u32 rv2p_proc, u32 fixup_loc)
04215 {
04216     __le32 *rv2p_code_start = rv2p_code;
04217     int i;
04218     u32 val, cmd, addr;
04219 
04220     if (rv2p_proc == RV2P_PROC1) {
04221         cmd = BNX2_RV2P_PROC1_ADDR_CMD_RDWR;
04222         addr = BNX2_RV2P_PROC1_ADDR_CMD;
04223     } else {
04224         cmd = BNX2_RV2P_PROC2_ADDR_CMD_RDWR;
04225         addr = BNX2_RV2P_PROC2_ADDR_CMD;
04226     }
04227 
04228     for (i = 0; i < rv2p_code_len; i += 8) {
04229         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_INSTR_HIGH, le32_to_cpu(*rv2p_code));
04230         rv2p_code++;
04231         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_INSTR_LOW, le32_to_cpu(*rv2p_code));
04232         rv2p_code++;
04233 
04234         val = (i / 8) | cmd;
04235         REG_WR(bp, addr, val);
04236     }
04237 
04238     rv2p_code = rv2p_code_start;
04239     if (fixup_loc && ((fixup_loc * 4) < rv2p_code_len)) {
04240         u32 code;
04241 
04242         code = le32_to_cpu(*(rv2p_code + fixup_loc - 1));
04243         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_INSTR_HIGH, code);
04244         code = le32_to_cpu(*(rv2p_code + fixup_loc));
04245         code = rv2p_fw_fixup(rv2p_proc, 0, fixup_loc, code);
04246         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_INSTR_LOW, code);
04247 
04248         val = (fixup_loc / 2) | cmd;
04249         REG_WR(bp, addr, val);
04250     }
04251 
04252     /* Reset the processor, un-stall is done later. */
04253     if (rv2p_proc == RV2P_PROC1) {
04254         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_COMMAND, BNX2_RV2P_COMMAND_PROC1_RESET);
04255     }
04256     else {
04257         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_COMMAND, BNX2_RV2P_COMMAND_PROC2_RESET);
04258     }
04259 }
04260 
04261 static int
04262 load_cpu_fw(struct bnx2 *bp, const struct cpu_reg *cpu_reg, struct fw_info *fw)
04263 {
04264     u32 offset;
04265     u32 val;
04266     int rc;
04267 
04268     /* Halt the CPU. */
04269     val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, cpu_reg->mode);
04270     val |= cpu_reg->mode_value_halt;
04271     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->mode, val);
04272     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->state, cpu_reg->state_value_clear);
04273 
04274     /* Load the Text area. */
04275     offset = cpu_reg->spad_base + (fw->text_addr - cpu_reg->mips_view_base);
04276 
04277     if (fw->gz_text) {
04278         u32 text_len;
04279         void *text;
04280 
04281         rc = bnx2_gunzip(bp, fw->gz_text, fw->gz_text_len, &text,
04282                  &text_len);
04283         if (rc)
04284             return rc;
04285 
04286         fw->text = text;
04287     }
04288     if (fw->text) {
04289         int j;
04290         for (j = 0; j < (fw->text_len / 4); j++, offset += 4) {
04291             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, offset, le32_to_cpu(fw->text[j]));
04292             }
04293     }
04294 
04295     /* Load the Data area. */
04296     offset = cpu_reg->spad_base + (fw->data_addr - cpu_reg->mips_view_base);
04297     if (fw->data) {
04298         int j;
04299 
04300         for (j = 0; j < (fw->data_len / 4); j++, offset += 4) {
04301             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, offset, fw->data[j]);
04302         }
04303     }
04304 
04305     /* Load the SBSS area. */
04306     offset = cpu_reg->spad_base + (fw->sbss_addr - cpu_reg->mips_view_base);
04307     if (fw->sbss_len) {
04308         int j;
04309 
04310         for (j = 0; j < (fw->sbss_len / 4); j++, offset += 4) {
04311             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, offset, 0);
04312         }
04313     }
04314 
04315     /* Load the BSS area. */
04316     offset = cpu_reg->spad_base + (fw->bss_addr - cpu_reg->mips_view_base);
04317     if (fw->bss_len) {
04318         int j;
04319 
04320         for (j = 0; j < (fw->bss_len/4); j++, offset += 4) {
04321             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, offset, 0);
04322         }
04323     }
04324 
04325     /* Load the Read-Only area. */
04326     offset = cpu_reg->spad_base +
04327         (fw->rodata_addr - cpu_reg->mips_view_base);
04328     if (fw->rodata) {
04329         int j;
04330 
04331         for (j = 0; j < (fw->rodata_len / 4); j++, offset += 4) {
04332             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, offset, fw->rodata[j]);
04333         }
04334     }
04335 
04336     /* Clear the pre-fetch instruction. */
04337     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->inst, 0);
04338     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->pc, fw->start_addr);
04339 
04340     /* Start the CPU. */
04341     val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, cpu_reg->mode);
04342     val &= ~cpu_reg->mode_value_halt;
04343     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->state, cpu_reg->state_value_clear);
04344     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, cpu_reg->mode, val);
04345 
04346     return 0;
04347 }
04348 
04349 static int
04350 bnx2_init_cpus(struct bnx2 *bp)
04351 {
04352     struct fw_info *fw;
04353     int rc = 0, rv2p_len;
04354     void *text;
04355     const void *rv2p;
04356     u32 text_len, fixup_loc;
04357 
04358     if ((rc = bnx2_gunzip_init(bp)) != 0)
04359         return rc;
04360 
04361     /* Initialize the RV2P processor. */
04362     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
04363         if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5709_A0) ||
04364             (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5709_A1)) {
04365             rv2p = bnx2_xi90_rv2p_proc1;
04366             rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_xi90_rv2p_proc1);
04367             fixup_loc = XI90_RV2P_PROC1_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04368         } else {
04369             rv2p = bnx2_xi_rv2p_proc1;
04370             rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_xi_rv2p_proc1);
04371             fixup_loc = XI_RV2P_PROC1_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04372         }
04373     } else {
04374         rv2p = bnx2_rv2p_proc1;
04375         rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_rv2p_proc1);
04376         fixup_loc = RV2P_PROC1_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04377     }
04378     rc = bnx2_gunzip(bp, rv2p, rv2p_len, &text, &text_len);
04379     if (rc)
04380         goto init_cpu_err;
04381 
04382     load_rv2p_fw(bp, text, text_len, RV2P_PROC1, fixup_loc);
04383 
04384     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
04385         if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5709_A0) ||
04386             (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5709_A1)) {
04387             rv2p = bnx2_xi90_rv2p_proc2;
04388             rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_xi90_rv2p_proc2);
04389             fixup_loc = XI90_RV2P_PROC2_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04390         } else {
04391             rv2p = bnx2_xi_rv2p_proc2;
04392             rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_xi_rv2p_proc2);
04393             fixup_loc = XI_RV2P_PROC2_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04394         }
04395     } else {
04396         rv2p = bnx2_rv2p_proc2;
04397         rv2p_len = sizeof(bnx2_rv2p_proc2);
04398         fixup_loc = RV2P_PROC2_MAX_BD_PAGE_LOC;
04399     }
04400     rc = bnx2_gunzip(bp, rv2p, rv2p_len, &text, &text_len);
04401     if (rc)
04402         goto init_cpu_err;
04403 
04404     load_rv2p_fw(bp, text, text_len, RV2P_PROC2, fixup_loc);
04405 
04406     /* Initialize the RX Processor. */
04407     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
04408         fw = &bnx2_rxp_fw_09;
04409     else
04410         fw = &bnx2_rxp_fw_06;
04411 
04412     rc = load_cpu_fw(bp, &cpu_reg_rxp, fw);
04413     if (rc)
04414         goto init_cpu_err;
04415 
04416     /* Initialize the TX Processor. */
04417     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
04418         fw = &bnx2_txp_fw_09;
04419     else
04420         fw = &bnx2_txp_fw_06;
04421 
04422     rc = load_cpu_fw(bp, &cpu_reg_txp, fw);
04423     if (rc)
04424         goto init_cpu_err;
04425 
04426     /* Initialize the TX Patch-up Processor. */
04427     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
04428         fw = &bnx2_tpat_fw_09;
04429     else
04430         fw = &bnx2_tpat_fw_06;
04431 
04432     rc = load_cpu_fw(bp, &cpu_reg_tpat, fw);
04433     if (rc)
04434         goto init_cpu_err;
04435 
04436     /* Initialize the Completion Processor. */
04437     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
04438         fw = &bnx2_com_fw_09;
04439     else
04440         fw = &bnx2_com_fw_06;
04441 
04442     rc = load_cpu_fw(bp, &cpu_reg_com, fw);
04443     if (rc)
04444         goto init_cpu_err;
04445 
04446     /* Initialize the Command Processor. */
04447     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
04448         fw = &bnx2_cp_fw_09;
04449     else
04450         fw = &bnx2_cp_fw_06;
04451 
04452     rc = load_cpu_fw(bp, &cpu_reg_cp, fw);
04453     if (rc)
04454         goto init_cpu_err;
04455 
04456 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
04457     bnx2_print_fw_versions(bp);
04458 #endif
04459 
04460 init_cpu_err:
04461     bnx2_gunzip_end(bp);
04462     return rc;
04463 }
04464 
04465 static int
04466 bnx2_set_power_state(struct bnx2 *bp, pci_power_t state)
04467 {
04468     u16 pmcsr;
04469 
04470     pci_read_config_word(bp->pdev, bp->pm_cap + PCI_PM_CTRL, &pmcsr);
04471 
04472     switch (state) {
04473     case PCI_D0: {
04474         u32 val;
04475 
04476         pci_write_config_word(bp->pdev, bp->pm_cap + PCI_PM_CTRL,
04477             (pmcsr & ~PCI_PM_CTRL_STATE_MASK) |
04478             PCI_PM_CTRL_PME_STATUS);
04479 
04480         if (pmcsr & PCI_PM_CTRL_STATE_MASK)
04481             /* delay required during transition out of D3hot */
04482             bnx2_msleep(20);
04483 
04484         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE);
04485         val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MPKT_RCVD | BNX2_EMAC_MODE_ACPI_RCVD;
04486         val &= ~BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MPKT;
04487         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE, val);
04488 
04489         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RPM_CONFIG);
04490         val &= ~BNX2_RPM_CONFIG_ACPI_ENA;
04491         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_CONFIG, val);
04492         break;
04493     }
04494     case PCI_D3hot: {
04495         int i;
04496         u32 val, wol_msg;
04497 
04498         if (bp->wol) {
04499             u32 advertising;
04500             u8 autoneg;
04501 
04502             autoneg = bp->autoneg;
04503             advertising = bp->advertising;
04504 
04505             if (bp->phy_port == PORT_TP) {
04506                 bp->autoneg = AUTONEG_SPEED;
04507                 bp->advertising = ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half |
04508                     ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full |
04509                     ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half |
04510                     ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full |
04511                     ADVERTISED_Autoneg;
04512             }
04513 
04514             spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
04515             bnx2_setup_phy(bp, bp->phy_port);
04516             spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
04517 
04518             bp->autoneg = autoneg;
04519             bp->advertising = advertising;
04520 
04521             bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, bp->dev->dev_addr, 0);
04522 
04523             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE);
04524 
04525             /* Enable port mode. */
04526             val &= ~BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT;
04527             val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MPKT_RCVD |
04528                    BNX2_EMAC_MODE_ACPI_RCVD |
04529                    BNX2_EMAC_MODE_MPKT;
04530             if (bp->phy_port == PORT_TP)
04531                 val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_MII;
04532             else {
04533                 val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_PORT_GMII;
04534                 if (bp->line_speed == SPEED_2500)
04535                     val |= BNX2_EMAC_MODE_25G_MODE;
04536             }
04537 
04538             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MODE, val);
04539 
04540             /* receive all multicast */
04541             for (i = 0; i < NUM_MC_HASH_REGISTERS; i++) {
04542                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_MULTICAST_HASH0 + (i * 4),
04543                        0xffffffff);
04544             }
04545             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE,
04546                    BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_SORT_MODE);
04547 
04548             val = 1 | BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_BC_EN |
04549                   BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_MC_EN;
04550             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, 0x0);
04551             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, val);
04552             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0, val |
04553                    BNX2_RPM_SORT_USER0_ENA);
04554 
04555             /* Need to enable EMAC and RPM for WOL. */
04556             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS,
04557                    BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS_RX_PARSER_MAC_ENABLE |
04558                    BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS_TX_HEADER_Q_ENABLE |
04559                    BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS_EMAC_ENABLE);
04560 
04561             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RPM_CONFIG);
04562             val &= ~BNX2_RPM_CONFIG_ACPI_ENA;
04563             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RPM_CONFIG, val);
04564 
04565             wol_msg = BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_SUSPEND_WOL;
04566         }
04567         else {
04568             wol_msg = BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_SUSPEND_NO_WOL;
04569         }
04570 
04571         if (!(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL))
04572             bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA_WAIT3 | wol_msg,
04573                      1, 0);
04574 
04575         pmcsr &= ~PCI_PM_CTRL_STATE_MASK;
04576         if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) ||
04577             (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A1)) {
04578 
04579             if (bp->wol)
04580                 pmcsr |= 3;
04581         }
04582         else {
04583             pmcsr |= 3;
04584         }
04585         if (bp->wol) {
04586             pmcsr |= PCI_PM_CTRL_PME_ENABLE;
04587         }
04588         pci_write_config_word(bp->pdev, bp->pm_cap + PCI_PM_CTRL,
04589                       pmcsr);
04590 
04591         /* No more memory access after this point until
04592          * device is brought back to D0.
04593          */
04594         udelay(50);
04595         break;
04596     }
04597     default:
04598         return -EINVAL;
04599     }
04600     return 0;
04601 }
04602 
04603 static int
04604 bnx2_acquire_nvram_lock(struct bnx2 *bp)
04605 {
04606     u32 val;
04607     int j;
04608 
04609     /* Request access to the flash interface. */
04610     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB_ARB_REQ_SET2);
04611     for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04612         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB);
04613         if (val & BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB_ARB_ARB2)
04614             break;
04615 
04616         udelay(5);
04617     }
04618 
04619     if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04620         return -EBUSY;
04621 
04622     return 0;
04623 }
04624 
04625 static int
04626 bnx2_release_nvram_lock(struct bnx2 *bp)
04627 {
04628     int j;
04629     u32 val;
04630 
04631     /* Relinquish nvram interface. */
04632     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB_ARB_REQ_CLR2);
04633 
04634     for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04635         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB);
04636         if (!(val & BNX2_NVM_SW_ARB_ARB_ARB2))
04637             break;
04638 
04639         udelay(5);
04640     }
04641 
04642     if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04643         return -EBUSY;
04644 
04645     return 0;
04646 }
04647 
04648 
04649 static int
04650 bnx2_enable_nvram_write(struct bnx2 *bp)
04651 {
04652     u32 val;
04653 
04654     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG);
04655     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG, val | BNX2_MISC_CFG_NVM_WR_EN_PCI);
04656 
04657     if (bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_WREN) {
04658         int j;
04659 
04660         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE);
04661         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND,
04662                BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_WREN | BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DOIT);
04663 
04664         for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04665             udelay(5);
04666 
04667             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND);
04668             if (val & BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE)
04669                 break;
04670         }
04671 
04672         if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04673             return -EBUSY;
04674     }
04675     return 0;
04676 }
04677 
04678 static void
04679 bnx2_disable_nvram_write(struct bnx2 *bp)
04680 {
04681     u32 val;
04682 
04683     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG);
04684     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG, val & ~BNX2_MISC_CFG_NVM_WR_EN);
04685 }
04686 
04687 
04688 static void
04689 bnx2_enable_nvram_access(struct bnx2 *bp)
04690 {
04691     u32 val;
04692 
04693     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE);
04694     /* Enable both bits, even on read. */
04695     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE,
04696            val | BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE_EN | BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE_WR_EN);
04697 }
04698 
04699 static void
04700 bnx2_disable_nvram_access(struct bnx2 *bp)
04701 {
04702     u32 val;
04703 
04704     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE);
04705     /* Disable both bits, even after read. */
04706     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE,
04707         val & ~(BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE_EN |
04708             BNX2_NVM_ACCESS_ENABLE_WR_EN));
04709 }
04710 
04711 static int
04712 bnx2_nvram_erase_page(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset)
04713 {
04714     u32 cmd;
04715     int j;
04716 
04717     if (bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED)
04718         /* Buffered flash, no erase needed */
04719         return 0;
04720 
04721     /* Build an erase command */
04722     cmd = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_ERASE | BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_WR |
04723           BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DOIT;
04724 
04725     /* Need to clear DONE bit separately. */
04726     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE);
04727 
04728     /* Address of the NVRAM to read from. */
04729     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_ADDR, offset & BNX2_NVM_ADDR_NVM_ADDR_VALUE);
04730 
04731     /* Issue an erase command. */
04732     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, cmd);
04733 
04734     /* Wait for completion. */
04735     for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04736         u32 val;
04737 
04738         udelay(5);
04739 
04740         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND);
04741         if (val & BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE)
04742             break;
04743     }
04744 
04745     if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04746         return -EBUSY;
04747 
04748     return 0;
04749 }
04750 
04751 static int
04752 bnx2_nvram_read_dword(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u8 *ret_val, u32 cmd_flags)
04753 {
04754     u32 cmd;
04755     int j;
04756 
04757     /* Build the command word. */
04758     cmd = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DOIT | cmd_flags;
04759 
04760     /* Calculate an offset of a buffered flash, not needed for 5709. */
04761     if (bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_TRANSLATE) {
04762         offset = ((offset / bp->flash_info->page_size) <<
04763                bp->flash_info->page_bits) +
04764               (offset % bp->flash_info->page_size);
04765     }
04766 
04767     /* Need to clear DONE bit separately. */
04768     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE);
04769 
04770     /* Address of the NVRAM to read from. */
04771     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_ADDR, offset & BNX2_NVM_ADDR_NVM_ADDR_VALUE);
04772 
04773     /* Issue a read command. */
04774     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, cmd);
04775 
04776     /* Wait for completion. */
04777     for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04778         u32 val;
04779 
04780         udelay(5);
04781 
04782         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND);
04783         if (val & BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE) {
04784             __be32 v = cpu_to_be32(REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_READ));
04785             memcpy(ret_val, &v, 4);
04786             break;
04787         }
04788     }
04789     if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04790         return -EBUSY;
04791 
04792     return 0;
04793 }
04794 
04795 
04796 static int
04797 bnx2_nvram_write_dword(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u8 *val, u32 cmd_flags)
04798 {
04799     u32 cmd;
04800     __be32 val32;
04801     int j;
04802 
04803     /* Build the command word. */
04804     cmd = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DOIT | BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_WR | cmd_flags;
04805 
04806     /* Calculate an offset of a buffered flash, not needed for 5709. */
04807     if (bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_TRANSLATE) {
04808         offset = ((offset / bp->flash_info->page_size) <<
04809               bp->flash_info->page_bits) +
04810              (offset % bp->flash_info->page_size);
04811     }
04812 
04813     /* Need to clear DONE bit separately. */
04814     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE);
04815 
04816     memcpy(&val32, val, 4);
04817 
04818     /* Write the data. */
04819     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_WRITE, be32_to_cpu(val32));
04820 
04821     /* Address of the NVRAM to write to. */
04822     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_ADDR, offset & BNX2_NVM_ADDR_NVM_ADDR_VALUE);
04823 
04824     /* Issue the write command. */
04825     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND, cmd);
04826 
04827     /* Wait for completion. */
04828     for (j = 0; j < NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT; j++) {
04829         udelay(5);
04830 
04831         if (REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_COMMAND) & BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_DONE)
04832             break;
04833     }
04834     if (j >= NVRAM_TIMEOUT_COUNT)
04835         return -EBUSY;
04836 
04837     return 0;
04838 }
04839 
04840 static int
04841 bnx2_init_nvram(struct bnx2 *bp)
04842 {
04843     u32 val;
04844     int j, entry_count, rc = 0;
04845     const struct flash_spec *flash;
04846 
04847     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
04848         bp->flash_info = &flash_5709;
04849         goto get_flash_size;
04850     }
04851 
04852     /* Determine the selected interface. */
04853     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_NVM_CFG1);
04854 
04855     entry_count = ARRAY_SIZE(flash_table);
04856 
04857     if (val & 0x40000000) {
04858 
04859         /* Flash interface has been reconfigured */
04860         for (j = 0, flash = &flash_table[0]; j < entry_count;
04861              j++, flash++) {
04862             if ((val & FLASH_BACKUP_STRAP_MASK) ==
04863                 (flash->config1 & FLASH_BACKUP_STRAP_MASK)) {
04864                 bp->flash_info = flash;
04865                 break;
04866             }
04867         }
04868     }
04869     else {
04870         u32 mask;
04871         /* Not yet been reconfigured */
04872 
04873         if (val & (1 << 23))
04874             mask = FLASH_BACKUP_STRAP_MASK;
04875         else
04876             mask = FLASH_STRAP_MASK;
04877 
04878         for (j = 0, flash = &flash_table[0]; j < entry_count;
04879             j++, flash++) {
04880 
04881             if ((val & mask) == (flash->strapping & mask)) {
04882                 bp->flash_info = flash;
04883 
04884                 /* Request access to the flash interface. */
04885                 if ((rc = bnx2_acquire_nvram_lock(bp)) != 0)
04886                     return rc;
04887 
04888                 /* Enable access to flash interface */
04889                 bnx2_enable_nvram_access(bp);
04890 
04891                 /* Reconfigure the flash interface */
04892                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_CFG1, flash->config1);
04893                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_CFG2, flash->config2);
04894                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_CFG3, flash->config3);
04895                 REG_WR(bp, BNX2_NVM_WRITE1, flash->write1);
04896 
04897                 /* Disable access to flash interface */
04898                 bnx2_disable_nvram_access(bp);
04899                 bnx2_release_nvram_lock(bp);
04900 
04901                 break;
04902             }
04903         }
04904     } /* if (val & 0x40000000) */
04905 
04906     if (j == entry_count) {
04907         bp->flash_info = NULL;
04908         printk(KERN_ALERT PFX "Unknown flash/EEPROM type.\n");
04909         return -ENODEV;
04910     }
04911 
04912 get_flash_size:
04913     val = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_CONFIG2);
04914     val &= BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG2_NVM_SIZE_MASK;
04915     if (val)
04916         bp->flash_size = val;
04917     else
04918         bp->flash_size = bp->flash_info->total_size;
04919 
04920     return rc;
04921 }
04922 
04923 static int
04924 bnx2_nvram_read(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u8 *ret_buf,
04925         int buf_size)
04926 {
04927     int rc = 0;
04928     u32 cmd_flags, offset32, len32, extra;
04929 
04930     if (buf_size == 0)
04931         return 0;
04932 
04933     /* Request access to the flash interface. */
04934     if ((rc = bnx2_acquire_nvram_lock(bp)) != 0)
04935         return rc;
04936 
04937     /* Enable access to flash interface */
04938     bnx2_enable_nvram_access(bp);
04939 
04940     len32 = buf_size;
04941     offset32 = offset;
04942     extra = 0;
04943 
04944     cmd_flags = 0;
04945 
04946     if (offset32 & 3) {
04947         u8 buf[4];
04948         u32 pre_len;
04949 
04950         offset32 &= ~3;
04951         pre_len = 4 - (offset & 3);
04952 
04953         if (pre_len >= len32) {
04954             pre_len = len32;
04955             cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_FIRST |
04956                     BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
04957         }
04958         else {
04959             cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_FIRST;
04960         }
04961 
04962         rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp, offset32, buf, cmd_flags);
04963 
04964         if (rc)
04965             return rc;
04966 
04967         memcpy(ret_buf, buf + (offset & 3), pre_len);
04968 
04969         offset32 += 4;
04970         ret_buf += pre_len;
04971         len32 -= pre_len;
04972     }
04973     if (len32 & 3) {
04974         extra = 4 - (len32 & 3);
04975         len32 = (len32 + 4) & ~3;
04976     }
04977 
04978     if (len32 == 4) {
04979         u8 buf[4];
04980 
04981         if (cmd_flags)
04982             cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
04983         else
04984             cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_FIRST |
04985                     BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
04986 
04987         rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp, offset32, buf, cmd_flags);
04988 
04989         memcpy(ret_buf, buf, 4 - extra);
04990     }
04991     else if (len32 > 0) {
04992         u8 buf[4];
04993 
04994         /* Read the first word. */
04995         if (cmd_flags)
04996             cmd_flags = 0;
04997         else
04998             cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_FIRST;
04999 
05000         rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp, offset32, ret_buf, cmd_flags);
05001 
05002         /* Advance to the next dword. */
05003         offset32 += 4;
05004         ret_buf += 4;
05005         len32 -= 4;
05006 
05007         while (len32 > 4 && rc == 0) {
05008             rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp, offset32, ret_buf, 0);
05009 
05010             /* Advance to the next dword. */
05011             offset32 += 4;
05012             ret_buf += 4;
05013             len32 -= 4;
05014         }
05015 
05016         if (rc)
05017             return rc;
05018 
05019         cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
05020         rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp, offset32, buf, cmd_flags);
05021 
05022         memcpy(ret_buf, buf, 4 - extra);
05023     }
05024 
05025     /* Disable access to flash interface */
05026     bnx2_disable_nvram_access(bp);
05027 
05028     bnx2_release_nvram_lock(bp);
05029 
05030     return rc;
05031 }
05032 
05033 static int
05034 bnx2_nvram_write(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset, u8 *data_buf,
05035         int buf_size)
05036 {
05037     u32 written, offset32, len32;
05038     u8 *buf, start[4], end[4], *align_buf = NULL, *flash_buffer = NULL;
05039     int rc = 0;
05040     int align_start, align_end;
05041 
05042     buf = data_buf;
05043     offset32 = offset;
05044     len32 = buf_size;
05045     align_start = align_end = 0;
05046 
05047     if ((align_start = (offset32 & 3))) {
05048         offset32 &= ~3;
05049         len32 += align_start;
05050         if (len32 < 4)
05051             len32 = 4;
05052         if ((rc = bnx2_nvram_read(bp, offset32, start, 4)))
05053             return rc;
05054     }
05055 
05056     if (len32 & 3) {
05057         align_end = 4 - (len32 & 3);
05058         len32 += align_end;
05059         if ((rc = bnx2_nvram_read(bp, offset32 + len32 - 4, end, 4)))
05060             return rc;
05061     }
05062 
05063     if (align_start || align_end) {
05064         align_buf = kmalloc(len32, GFP_KERNEL);
05065         if (align_buf == NULL)
05066             return -ENOMEM;
05067         if (align_start) {
05068             memcpy(align_buf, start, 4);
05069         }
05070         if (align_end) {
05071             memcpy(align_buf + len32 - 4, end, 4);
05072         }
05073         memcpy(align_buf + align_start, data_buf, buf_size);
05074         buf = align_buf;
05075     }
05076 
05077     if (!(bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED)) {
05078         flash_buffer = kmalloc(264, GFP_KERNEL);
05079         if (flash_buffer == NULL) {
05080             rc = -ENOMEM;
05081             goto nvram_write_end;
05082         }
05083     }
05084 
05085     written = 0;
05086     while ((written < len32) && (rc == 0)) {
05087         u32 page_start, page_end, data_start, data_end;
05088         u32 addr, cmd_flags;
05089         int i;
05090 
05091             /* Find the page_start addr */
05092         page_start = offset32 + written;
05093         page_start -= (page_start % bp->flash_info->page_size);
05094         /* Find the page_end addr */
05095         page_end = page_start + bp->flash_info->page_size;
05096         /* Find the data_start addr */
05097         data_start = (written == 0) ? offset32 : page_start;
05098         /* Find the data_end addr */
05099         data_end = (page_end > offset32 + len32) ?
05100             (offset32 + len32) : page_end;
05101 
05102         /* Request access to the flash interface. */
05103         if ((rc = bnx2_acquire_nvram_lock(bp)) != 0)
05104             goto nvram_write_end;
05105 
05106         /* Enable access to flash interface */
05107         bnx2_enable_nvram_access(bp);
05108 
05109         cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_FIRST;
05110         if (!(bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED)) {
05111             int j;
05112 
05113             /* Read the whole page into the buffer
05114              * (non-buffer flash only) */
