05115             for (j = 0; j < bp->flash_info->page_size; j += 4) {
05116                 if (j == (bp->flash_info->page_size - 4)) {
05117                     cmd_flags |= BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
05118                 }
05119                 rc = bnx2_nvram_read_dword(bp,
05120                     page_start + j,
05121                     &flash_buffer[j],
05122                     cmd_flags);
05123 
05124                 if (rc)
05125                     goto nvram_write_end;
05126 
05127                 cmd_flags = 0;
05128             }
05129         }
05130 
05131         /* Enable writes to flash interface (unlock write-protect) */
05132         if ((rc = bnx2_enable_nvram_write(bp)) != 0)
05133             goto nvram_write_end;
05134 
05135         /* Loop to write back the buffer data from page_start to
05136          * data_start */
05137         i = 0;
05138         if (!(bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED)) {
05139             /* Erase the page */
05140             if ((rc = bnx2_nvram_erase_page(bp, page_start)) != 0)
05141                 goto nvram_write_end;
05142 
05143             /* Re-enable the write again for the actual write */
05144             bnx2_enable_nvram_write(bp);
05145 
05146             for (addr = page_start; addr < data_start;
05147                 addr += 4, i += 4) {
05148 
05149                 rc = bnx2_nvram_write_dword(bp, addr,
05150                     &flash_buffer[i], cmd_flags);
05151 
05152                 if (rc != 0)
05153                     goto nvram_write_end;
05154 
05155                 cmd_flags = 0;
05156             }
05157         }
05158 
05159         /* Loop to write the new data from data_start to data_end */
05160         for (addr = data_start; addr < data_end; addr += 4, i += 4) {
05161             if ((addr == page_end - 4) ||
05162                 ((bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED) &&
05163                  (addr == data_end - 4))) {
05164 
05165                 cmd_flags |= BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
05166             }
05167             rc = bnx2_nvram_write_dword(bp, addr, buf,
05168                 cmd_flags);
05169 
05170             if (rc != 0)
05171                 goto nvram_write_end;
05172 
05173             cmd_flags = 0;
05174             buf += 4;
05175         }
05176 
05177         /* Loop to write back the buffer data from data_end
05178          * to page_end */
05179         if (!(bp->flash_info->flags & BNX2_NV_BUFFERED)) {
05180             for (addr = data_end; addr < page_end;
05181                 addr += 4, i += 4) {
05182 
05183                 if (addr == page_end-4) {
05184                     cmd_flags = BNX2_NVM_COMMAND_LAST;
05185                         }
05186                 rc = bnx2_nvram_write_dword(bp, addr,
05187                     &flash_buffer[i], cmd_flags);
05188 
05189                 if (rc != 0)
05190                     goto nvram_write_end;
05191 
05192                 cmd_flags = 0;
05193             }
05194         }
05195 
05196         /* Disable writes to flash interface (lock write-protect) */
05197         bnx2_disable_nvram_write(bp);
05198 
05199         /* Disable access to flash interface */
05200         bnx2_disable_nvram_access(bp);
05201         bnx2_release_nvram_lock(bp);
05202 
05203         /* Increment written */
05204         written += data_end - data_start;
05205     }
05206 
05207 nvram_write_end:
05208     kfree(flash_buffer);
05209     kfree(align_buf);
05210     return rc;
05211 }
05212 
05213 static void
05214 bnx2_init_fw_cap(struct bnx2 *bp)
05215 {
05216     u32 val, sig = 0;
05217 
05218     bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP;
05219     bp->flags &= ~BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN;
05220 
05221     if (!(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_ASF_ENABLE))
05222         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN;
05223 
05224     val = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_FW_CAP_MB);
05225     if ((val & BNX2_FW_CAP_SIGNATURE_MASK) != BNX2_FW_CAP_SIGNATURE)
05226         return;
05227 
05228     if ((val & BNX2_FW_CAP_CAN_KEEP_VLAN) == BNX2_FW_CAP_CAN_KEEP_VLAN) {
05229         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN;
05230         sig |= BNX2_DRV_ACK_CAP_SIGNATURE | BNX2_FW_CAP_CAN_KEEP_VLAN;
05231     }
05232 
05233     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) &&
05234         (val & BNX2_FW_CAP_REMOTE_PHY_CAPABLE)) {
05235         u32 link;
05236 
05237         bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP;
05238 
05239         link = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_LINK_STATUS);
05240         if (link & BNX2_LINK_STATUS_SERDES_LINK)
05241             bp->phy_port = PORT_FIBRE;
05242         else
05243             bp->phy_port = PORT_TP;
05244 
05245         sig |= BNX2_DRV_ACK_CAP_SIGNATURE |
05246                BNX2_FW_CAP_REMOTE_PHY_CAPABLE;
05247     }
05248 
05249     if (netif_running(bp->dev) && sig)
05250         bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_DRV_ACK_CAP_MB, sig);
05251 }
05252 
05253 static void
05254 bnx2_setup_msix_tbl(struct bnx2 *bp)
05255 {
05256     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW_ADDR, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW_ADDR_SEP_WIN);
05257 
05258     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW2_ADDR, BNX2_MSIX_TABLE_ADDR);
05259     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW3_ADDR, BNX2_MSIX_PBA_ADDR);
05260 }
05261 
05262 static int
05263 bnx2_reset_chip(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 reset_code)
05264 {
05265     u32 val;
05266     int i, rc = 0;
05267     u8 old_port;
05268 
05269     /* Wait for the current PCI transaction to complete before
05270      * issuing a reset. */
05271     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS,
05272            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS_TX_DMA_ENABLE |
05273            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS_DMA_ENGINE_ENABLE |
05274            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS_RX_DMA_ENABLE |
05275            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS_HOST_COALESCE_ENABLE);
05276     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_CLR_BITS);
05277     udelay(5);
05278 
05279     /* Wait for the firmware to tell us it is ok to issue a reset. */
05280     bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA_WAIT0 | reset_code, 1, 1);
05281 
05282     /* Deposit a driver reset signature so the firmware knows that
05283      * this is a soft reset. */
05284     bnx2_shmem_wr(bp, BNX2_DRV_RESET_SIGNATURE,
05285               BNX2_DRV_RESET_SIGNATURE_MAGIC);
05286 
05287     /* Do a dummy read to force the chip to complete all current transaction
05288      * before we issue a reset. */
05289     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_ID);
05290 
05291     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05292         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_COMMAND, BNX2_MISC_COMMAND_SW_RESET);
05293         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_COMMAND);
05294         udelay(5);
05295 
05296         val = BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_REG_WINDOW_ENA |
05297               BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_TARGET_MB_WORD_SWAP;
05298 
05299         pci_write_config_dword(bp->pdev, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG, val);
05300 
05301     } else {
05302         val = BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_CORE_RST_REQ |
05303               BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_REG_WINDOW_ENA |
05304               BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_TARGET_MB_WORD_SWAP;
05305 
05306         /* Chip reset. */
05307         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG, val);
05308 
05309         /* Reading back any register after chip reset will hang the
05310          * bus on 5706 A0 and A1.  The msleep below provides plenty
05311          * of margin for write posting.
05312          */
05313         if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) ||
05314             (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A1))
05315             bnx2_msleep(20);
05316 
05317         /* Reset takes approximate 30 usec */
05318         for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
05319             val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG);
05320             if ((val & (BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_CORE_RST_REQ |
05321                     BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_CORE_RST_BSY)) == 0)
05322                 break;
05323             udelay(10);
05324         }
05325 
05326         if (val & (BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_CORE_RST_REQ |
05327                BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_CORE_RST_BSY)) {
05328             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "Chip reset did not complete\n");
05329             return -EBUSY;
05330         }
05331     }
05332 
05333     /* Make sure byte swapping is properly configured. */
05334     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCI_SWAP_DIAG0);
05335     if (val != 0x01020304) {
05336         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "Chip not in correct endian mode\n");
05337         return -ENODEV;
05338     }
05339 
05340     /* Wait for the firmware to finish its initialization. */
05341     rc = bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA_WAIT1 | reset_code, 1, 0);
05342     if (rc)
05343         return rc;
05344 
05345     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
05346     old_port = bp->phy_port;
05347     bnx2_init_fw_cap(bp);
05348     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP) &&
05349         old_port != bp->phy_port)
05350         bnx2_set_default_remote_link(bp);
05351     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
05352 
05353     if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) {
05354         /* Adjust the voltage regular to two steps lower.  The default
05355          * of this register is 0x0000000e. */
05356         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_VREG_CONTROL, 0x000000fa);
05357 
05358         /* Remove bad rbuf memory from the free pool. */
05359         rc = bnx2_alloc_bad_rbuf(bp);
05360     }
05361 
05362     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)
05363         bnx2_setup_msix_tbl(bp);
05364 
05365     return rc;
05366 }
05367 
05368 static int
05369 bnx2_init_chip(struct bnx2 *bp)
05370 {
05371     u32 val, mtu;
05372     int rc, i;
05373 
05374     /* Make sure the interrupt is not active. */
05375     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD_MASK_INT);
05376 
05377     val = BNX2_DMA_CONFIG_DATA_BYTE_SWAP |
05378           BNX2_DMA_CONFIG_DATA_WORD_SWAP |
05379 #ifdef __BIG_ENDIAN
05380           BNX2_DMA_CONFIG_CNTL_BYTE_SWAP |
05381 #endif
05382           BNX2_DMA_CONFIG_CNTL_WORD_SWAP |
05383           DMA_READ_CHANS << 12 |
05384           DMA_WRITE_CHANS << 16;
05385 
05386     val |= (0x2 << 20) | (1 << 11);
05387 
05388     if ((bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIX) && (bp->bus_speed_mhz == 133))
05389         val |= (1 << 23);
05390 
05391     if ((CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706) &&
05392         (CHIP_ID(bp) != CHIP_ID_5706_A0) && !(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIX))
05393         val |= BNX2_DMA_CONFIG_CNTL_PING_PONG_DMA;
05394 
05395     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_DMA_CONFIG, val);
05396 
05397     if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) {
05398         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_TDMA_CONFIG);
05399         val |= BNX2_TDMA_CONFIG_ONE_DMA;
05400         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_TDMA_CONFIG, val);
05401     }
05402 
05403     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIX) {
05404         u16 val16;
05405 
05406         pci_read_config_word(bp->pdev, bp->pcix_cap + PCI_X_CMD,
05407                      &val16);
05408         pci_write_config_word(bp->pdev, bp->pcix_cap + PCI_X_CMD,
05409                       val16 & ~PCI_X_CMD_ERO);
05410     }
05411 
05412     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS,
05413            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS_HOST_COALESCE_ENABLE |
05414            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_STATUS_BITS_RX_V2P_ENABLE |
05415            BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_STATUS_BITS_CONTEXT_ENABLE);
05416 
05417     /* Initialize context mapping and zero out the quick contexts.  The
05418      * context block must have already been enabled. */
05419     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05420         rc = bnx2_init_5709_context(bp);
05421         if (rc)
05422             return rc;
05423     } else
05424         bnx2_init_context(bp);
05425 
05426     if ((rc = bnx2_init_cpus(bp)) != 0)
05427         return rc;
05428 
05429     bnx2_init_nvram(bp);
05430 
05431     bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, bp->dev->dev_addr, 0);
05432 
05433     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MQ_CONFIG);
05434     val &= ~BNX2_MQ_CONFIG_KNL_BYP_BLK_SIZE;
05435     val |= BNX2_MQ_CONFIG_KNL_BYP_BLK_SIZE_256;
05436     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05437         val |= BNX2_MQ_CONFIG_BIN_MQ_MODE;
05438         if (CHIP_REV(bp) == CHIP_REV_Ax)
05439             val |= BNX2_MQ_CONFIG_HALT_DIS;
05440     }
05441 
05442     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_CONFIG, val);
05443 
05444     val = 0x10000 + (MAX_CID_CNT * MB_KERNEL_CTX_SIZE);
05445     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_BYP_WIND_START, val);
05446     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_WIND_END, val);
05447 
05448     val = (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8) << 24;
05449     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RV2P_CONFIG, val);
05450 
05451     /* Configure page size. */
05452     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_TBDR_CONFIG);
05453     val &= ~BNX2_TBDR_CONFIG_PAGE_SIZE;
05454     val |= (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8) << 24 | 0x40;
05455     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_TBDR_CONFIG, val);
05456 
05457     val = bp->mac_addr[0] +
05458           (bp->mac_addr[1] << 8) +
05459           (bp->mac_addr[2] << 16) +
05460           bp->mac_addr[3] +
05461           (bp->mac_addr[4] << 8) +
05462           (bp->mac_addr[5] << 16);
05463     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_BACKOFF_SEED, val);
05464 
05465     /* Program the MTU.  Also include 4 bytes for CRC32. */
05466     mtu = bp->dev->mtu;
05467     val = mtu + ETH_HLEN + ETH_FCS_LEN;
05468     if (val > (MAX_ETHERNET_PACKET_SIZE + 4))
05469         val |= BNX2_EMAC_RX_MTU_SIZE_JUMBO_ENA;
05470     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_RX_MTU_SIZE, val);
05471 
05472     if (mtu < 1500)
05473         mtu = 1500;
05474 
05475     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG_VAL(mtu));
05476     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG2, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG2_VAL(mtu));
05477     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG3, BNX2_RBUF_CONFIG3_VAL(mtu));
05478 
05479     memset(bp->bnx2_napi[0].status_blk.msi, 0, bp->status_stats_size);
05480     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++)
05481         bp->bnx2_napi[i].last_status_idx = 0;
05482 
05483     bp->idle_chk_status_idx = 0xffff;
05484 
05485     bp->rx_mode = BNX2_EMAC_RX_MODE_SORT_MODE;
05486 
05487     /* Set up how to generate a link change interrupt. */
05488     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_ATTENTION_ENA, BNX2_EMAC_ATTENTION_ENA_LINK);
05489 
05490     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATUS_ADDR_L,
05491            (u64) bp->status_blk_mapping & 0xffffffff);
05492     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATUS_ADDR_H, (u64) bp->status_blk_mapping >> 32);
05493 
05494     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATISTICS_ADDR_L,
05495            (u64) bp->stats_blk_mapping & 0xffffffff);
05496     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATISTICS_ADDR_H,
05497            (u64) bp->stats_blk_mapping >> 32);
05498 
05499     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_TX_QUICK_CONS_TRIP,
05500            (bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int << 16) | bp->tx_quick_cons_trip);
05501 
05502     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_RX_QUICK_CONS_TRIP,
05503            (bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int << 16) | bp->rx_quick_cons_trip);
05504 
05505     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMP_PROD_TRIP,
05506            (bp->comp_prod_trip_int << 16) | bp->comp_prod_trip);
05507 
05508     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_TX_TICKS, (bp->tx_ticks_int << 16) | bp->tx_ticks);
05509 
05510     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_RX_TICKS, (bp->rx_ticks_int << 16) | bp->rx_ticks);
05511 
05512     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COM_TICKS,
05513            (bp->com_ticks_int << 16) | bp->com_ticks);
05514 
05515     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_CMD_TICKS,
05516            (bp->cmd_ticks_int << 16) | bp->cmd_ticks);
05517 
05518     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_BROKEN_STATS)
05519         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS, 0);
05520     else
05521         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS, bp->stats_ticks);
05522     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_STAT_COLLECT_TICKS, 0xbb8);  /* 3ms */
05523 
05524     if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A1)
05525         val = BNX2_HC_CONFIG_COLLECT_STATS;
05526     else {
05527         val = BNX2_HC_CONFIG_RX_TMR_MODE | BNX2_HC_CONFIG_TX_TMR_MODE |
05528               BNX2_HC_CONFIG_COLLECT_STATS;
05529     }
05530 
05531     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX) {
05532         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_MSIX_BIT_VECTOR,
05533                BNX2_HC_MSIX_BIT_VECTOR_VAL);
05534 
05535         val |= BNX2_HC_CONFIG_SB_ADDR_INC_128B;
05536     }
05537 
05538     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_ONE_SHOT_MSI)
05539         val |= BNX2_HC_CONFIG_ONE_SHOT | BNX2_HC_CONFIG_USE_INT_PARAM;
05540 
05541     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_CONFIG, val);
05542 
05543     for (i = 1; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
05544         u32 base = ((i - 1) * BNX2_HC_SB_CONFIG_SIZE) +
05545                BNX2_HC_SB_CONFIG_1;
05546 
05547         REG_WR(bp, base,
05548             BNX2_HC_SB_CONFIG_1_TX_TMR_MODE |
05549             BNX2_HC_SB_CONFIG_1_RX_TMR_MODE |
05550             BNX2_HC_SB_CONFIG_1_ONE_SHOT);
05551 
05552         REG_WR(bp, base + BNX2_HC_TX_QUICK_CONS_TRIP_OFF,
05553             (bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int << 16) |
05554              bp->tx_quick_cons_trip);
05555 
05556         REG_WR(bp, base + BNX2_HC_TX_TICKS_OFF,
05557             (bp->tx_ticks_int << 16) | bp->tx_ticks);
05558 
05559         REG_WR(bp, base + BNX2_HC_RX_QUICK_CONS_TRIP_OFF,
05560                (bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int << 16) |
05561             bp->rx_quick_cons_trip);
05562 
05563         REG_WR(bp, base + BNX2_HC_RX_TICKS_OFF,
05564             (bp->rx_ticks_int << 16) | bp->rx_ticks);
05565     }
05566 
05567     /* Clear internal stats counters. */
05568     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND, BNX2_HC_COMMAND_CLR_STAT_NOW);
05569 
05570     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_ATTN_BITS_ENABLE, STATUS_ATTN_EVENTS);
05571 
05572     /* Initialize the receive filter. */
05573     bnx2_set_rx_mode(bp->dev);
05574 
05575     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05576         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_NEW_CORE_CTL);
05577         val |= BNX2_MISC_NEW_CORE_CTL_DMA_ENABLE;
05578         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_NEW_CORE_CTL, val);
05579     }
05580     rc = bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_DATA_WAIT2 | BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET,
05581               1, 0);
05582 
05583     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_DEFAULT);
05584     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_ENABLE_SET_BITS);
05585 
05586     udelay(20);
05587 
05588     bp->hc_cmd = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
05589 
05590     return rc;
05591 }
05592 
05593 static void
05594 bnx2_clear_ring_states(struct bnx2 *bp)
05595 {
05596     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
05597     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr;
05598     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr;
05599     int i;
05600 
05601     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++) {
05602         bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
05603         txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
05604         rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
05605 
05606         txr->tx_cons = 0;
05607         txr->hw_tx_cons = 0;
05608         rxr->rx_prod_bseq = 0;
05609         rxr->rx_prod = 0;
05610         rxr->rx_cons = 0;
05611         rxr->rx_pg_prod = 0;
05612         rxr->rx_pg_cons = 0;
05613     }
05614 }
05615 
05616 static void
05617 bnx2_init_tx_context(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 cid, struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr)
05618 {
05619     u32 val, offset0, offset1, offset2, offset3;
05620     u32 cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(cid);
05621 
05622     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05623         offset0 = BNX2_L2CTX_TYPE_XI;
05624         offset1 = BNX2_L2CTX_CMD_TYPE_XI;
05625         offset2 = BNX2_L2CTX_TBDR_BHADDR_HI_XI;
05626         offset3 = BNX2_L2CTX_TBDR_BHADDR_LO_XI;
05627     } else {
05628         offset0 = BNX2_L2CTX_TYPE;
05629         offset1 = BNX2_L2CTX_CMD_TYPE;
05630         offset2 = BNX2_L2CTX_TBDR_BHADDR_HI;
05631         offset3 = BNX2_L2CTX_TBDR_BHADDR_LO;
05632     }
05633     val = BNX2_L2CTX_TYPE_TYPE_L2 | BNX2_L2CTX_TYPE_SIZE_L2;
05634     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, cid_addr, offset0, val);
05635 
05636     val = BNX2_L2CTX_CMD_TYPE_TYPE_L2 | (8 << 16);
05637     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, cid_addr, offset1, val);
05638 
05639     val = (u64) txr->tx_desc_mapping >> 32;
05640     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, cid_addr, offset2, val);
05641 
05642     val = (u64) txr->tx_desc_mapping & 0xffffffff;
05643     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, cid_addr, offset3, val);
05644 }
05645 
05646 static void
05647 bnx2_init_tx_ring(struct bnx2 *bp, int ring_num)
05648 {
05649     struct tx_bd *txbd;
05650     u32 cid = TX_CID;
05651     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
05652     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr;
05653 
05654     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[ring_num];
05655     txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
05656 
05657     if (ring_num == 0)
05658         cid = TX_CID;
05659     else
05660         cid = TX_TSS_CID + ring_num - 1;
05661 
05662     bp->tx_wake_thresh = bp->tx_ring_size / 2;
05663 
05664     txbd = &txr->tx_desc_ring[MAX_TX_DESC_CNT];
05665 
05666     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) txr->tx_desc_mapping >> 32;
05667     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) txr->tx_desc_mapping & 0xffffffff;
05668 
05669     txr->tx_prod = 0;
05670     txr->tx_prod_bseq = 0;
05671 
05672     txr->tx_bidx_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(cid) + BNX2_L2CTX_TX_HOST_BIDX;
05673     txr->tx_bseq_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(cid) + BNX2_L2CTX_TX_HOST_BSEQ;
05674 
05675     bnx2_init_tx_context(bp, cid, txr);
05676 }
05677 
05678 static void
05679 bnx2_init_rxbd_rings(struct rx_bd *rx_ring[], dma_addr_t dma[], u32 buf_size,
05680              int num_rings)
05681 {
05682     int i;
05683     struct rx_bd *rxbd;
05684 
05685     for (i = 0; i < num_rings; i++) {
05686         int j;
05687 
05688         rxbd = &rx_ring[i][0];
05689         for (j = 0; j < MAX_RX_DESC_CNT; j++, rxbd++) {
05690             rxbd->rx_bd_len = buf_size;
05691             rxbd->rx_bd_flags = RX_BD_FLAGS_START | RX_BD_FLAGS_END;
05692         }
05693         if (i == (num_rings - 1))
05694             j = 0;
05695         else
05696             j = i + 1;
05697         rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) dma[j] >> 32;
05698         rxbd->rx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) dma[j] & 0xffffffff;
05699     }
05700 }
05701 
05702 static void
05703 bnx2_init_rx_ring(struct bnx2 *bp, int ring_num)
05704 {
05705     int i;
05706     u16 prod, ring_prod;
05707     u32 cid, rx_cid_addr, val;
05708     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[ring_num];
05709     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
05710 
05711     if (ring_num == 0)
05712         cid = RX_CID;
05713     else
05714         cid = RX_RSS_CID + ring_num - 1;
05715 
05716     rx_cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(cid);
05717 
05718     bnx2_init_rxbd_rings(rxr->rx_desc_ring, rxr->rx_desc_mapping,
05719                  bp->rx_buf_use_size, bp->rx_max_ring);
05720 
05721     bnx2_init_rx_context(bp, cid);
05722 
05723     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
05724         val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MQ_MAP_L2_5);
05725         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_MAP_L2_5, val | BNX2_MQ_MAP_L2_5_ARM);
05726 
05727 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
05728         /*  Set in the RX context the proper CID location
05729          *  for the completion
05730          */
05731         if(BNX2_NETQUEUE_ENABLED(bp))
05732             bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, 0x04, 1 << 16);
05733 #endif
05734     }
05735 
05736     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_PG_BUF_SIZE, 0);
05737     if (bp->rx_pg_ring_size) {
05738         bnx2_init_rxbd_rings(rxr->rx_pg_desc_ring,
05739                      rxr->rx_pg_desc_mapping,
05740                      PAGE_SIZE, bp->rx_max_pg_ring);
05741         val = (bp->rx_buf_use_size << 16) | PAGE_SIZE;
05742         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_PG_BUF_SIZE, val);
05743         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_RBDC_KEY,
05744                BNX2_L2CTX_RBDC_JUMBO_KEY - ring_num);
05745 
05746         val = (u64) rxr->rx_pg_desc_mapping[0] >> 32;
05747         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_NX_PG_BDHADDR_HI, val);
05748 
05749         val = (u64) rxr->rx_pg_desc_mapping[0] & 0xffffffff;
05750         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_NX_PG_BDHADDR_LO, val);
05751 
05752         if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
05753             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_MAP_L2_3, BNX2_MQ_MAP_L2_3_DEFAULT);
05754     }
05755 
05756     val = (u64) rxr->rx_desc_mapping[0] >> 32;
05757     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_NX_BDHADDR_HI, val);
05758 
05759     val = (u64) rxr->rx_desc_mapping[0] & 0xffffffff;
05760     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, rx_cid_addr, BNX2_L2CTX_NX_BDHADDR_LO, val);
05761 
05762     ring_prod = prod = rxr->rx_pg_prod;
05763     for (i = 0; i < bp->rx_pg_ring_size; i++) {
05764         if (bnx2_alloc_rx_page(bp, rxr, ring_prod) < 0) {
05765             printk(KERN_WARNING PFX "%s: init'ed rx page ring %d "
05766                         "with %d/%d pages only\n",
05767                    bp->dev->name, ring_num, i, bp->rx_pg_ring_size);
05768             break;
05769         }
05770         prod = NEXT_RX_BD(prod);
05771         ring_prod = RX_PG_RING_IDX(prod);
05772     }
05773     rxr->rx_pg_prod = prod;
05774 
05775     ring_prod = prod = rxr->rx_prod;
05776     for (i = 0; i < bp->rx_ring_size; i++) {
05777         if (bnx2_alloc_rx_skb(bp, rxr, ring_prod) < 0) {
05778             printk(KERN_WARNING PFX "%s: init'ed rx ring %d with "
05779                         "%d/%d skbs only\n",
05780                    bp->dev->name, ring_num, i, bp->rx_ring_size);
05781             break;
05782         }
05783         prod = NEXT_RX_BD(prod);
05784         ring_prod = RX_RING_IDX(prod);
05785     }
05786     rxr->rx_prod = prod;
05787 
05788     rxr->rx_bidx_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(cid) + BNX2_L2CTX_HOST_BDIDX;
05789     rxr->rx_bseq_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(cid) + BNX2_L2CTX_HOST_BSEQ;
05790     rxr->rx_pg_bidx_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(cid) + BNX2_L2CTX_HOST_PG_BDIDX;
05791 
05792     REG_WR16(bp, rxr->rx_pg_bidx_addr, rxr->rx_pg_prod);
05793     REG_WR16(bp, rxr->rx_bidx_addr, prod);
05794 
05795     REG_WR(bp, rxr->rx_bseq_addr, rxr->rx_prod_bseq);
05796 }
05797 
05798 static void
05799 bnx2_init_all_rings(struct bnx2 *bp)
05800 {
05801     int i;
05802     u32 val;
05803 
05804     bnx2_clear_ring_states(bp);
05805 
05806     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_TSCH_TSS_CFG, 0);
05807     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_tx_rings; i++)
05808         bnx2_init_tx_ring(bp, i);
05809 
05810     if (bp->num_tx_rings > 1)
05811         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_TSCH_TSS_CFG, ((bp->num_tx_rings - 1) << 24) |
05812                (TX_TSS_CID << 7));
05813 
05814     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RLUP_RSS_CONFIG, 0);
05815     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH_RSS_TBL_SZ, 0);
05816 
05817     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_rx_rings; i++)
05818         bnx2_init_rx_ring(bp, i);
05819 
05820     if (bp->num_rx_rings > 1) {
05821         u32 tbl_32;
05822         u8 *tbl = (u8 *) &tbl_32;
05823 
05824         bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH_RSS_TBL_SZ,
05825                 BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH_RSS_TBL_MAX_ENTRIES);
05826 
05827         for (i = 0; i < BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH_RSS_TBL_MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {
05828             tbl[i % 4] = i % (bp->num_rx_rings - 1);
05829             if ((i % 4) == 3)
05830                 bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp,
05831                         BNX2_RXP_SCRATCH_RSS_TBL + i,
05832                         cpu_to_be32(tbl_32));
05833         }
05834 
05835         val = BNX2_RLUP_RSS_CONFIG_IPV4_RSS_TYPE_ALL_XI |
05836               BNX2_RLUP_RSS_CONFIG_IPV6_RSS_TYPE_ALL_XI;
05837 
05838         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_RLUP_RSS_CONFIG, val);
05839 
05840     }
05841 }
05842 
05843 static u32 bnx2_find_max_ring(u32 ring_size, u32 max_size)
05844 {
05845     u32 max, num_rings = 1;
05846 
05847     while (ring_size > MAX_RX_DESC_CNT) {
05848         ring_size -= MAX_RX_DESC_CNT;
05849         num_rings++;
05850     }
05851     /* round to next power of 2 */
05852     max = max_size;
05853     while ((max & num_rings) == 0)
05854         max >>= 1;
05855 
05856     if (num_rings != max)
05857         max <<= 1;
05858 
05859     return max;
05860 }
05861 
05862 static void
05863 bnx2_set_rx_ring_size(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 size)
05864 {
05865     u32 rx_size, rx_space;
05866 
05867     /* 8 for CRC and VLAN */
05868     rx_size = bp->dev->mtu + ETH_HLEN + BNX2_RX_OFFSET + 8;
05869 
05870     rx_space = SKB_DATA_ALIGN(rx_size + BNX2_RX_ALIGN) + NET_SKB_PAD +
05871         sizeof(struct skb_shared_info);
05872 
05873     bp->rx_copy_thresh = BNX2_RX_COPY_THRESH;
05874     bp->rx_pg_ring_size = 0;
05875     bp->rx_max_pg_ring = 0;
05876     bp->rx_max_pg_ring_idx = 0;
05877 #if !defined(__VMKLNX__)
05878     if ((rx_space > PAGE_SIZE) && !(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_JUMBO_BROKEN)) {
05879         int pages = PAGE_ALIGN(bp->dev->mtu - 40) >> PAGE_SHIFT;
05880 
05881         u32 jumbo_size = size * pages;
05882         if (jumbo_size > MAX_TOTAL_RX_PG_DESC_CNT)
05883             jumbo_size = MAX_TOTAL_RX_PG_DESC_CNT;
05884 
05885         bp->rx_pg_ring_size = jumbo_size;
05886         bp->rx_max_pg_ring = bnx2_find_max_ring(jumbo_size,
05887                             MAX_RX_PG_RINGS);
05888         bp->rx_max_pg_ring_idx = (bp->rx_max_pg_ring * RX_DESC_CNT) - 1;
05889         rx_size = BNX2_RX_COPY_THRESH + BNX2_RX_OFFSET;
05890         bp->rx_copy_thresh = 0;
05891     }
05892 #endif
05893 
05894     bp->rx_buf_use_size = rx_size;
05895     /* hw alignment */
05896     bp->rx_buf_size = bp->rx_buf_use_size + BNX2_RX_ALIGN;
05897     bp->rx_jumbo_thresh = rx_size - BNX2_RX_OFFSET;
05898     bp->rx_ring_size = size;
05899     bp->rx_max_ring = bnx2_find_max_ring(size, MAX_RX_RINGS);
05900     bp->rx_max_ring_idx = (bp->rx_max_ring * RX_DESC_CNT) - 1;
05901 }
05902 
05903 static void
05904 bnx2_free_tx_skbs(struct bnx2 *bp)
05905 {
05906     int i;
05907 
05908     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_tx_rings; i++) {
05909         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
05910         struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
05911         int j;
05912 
05913         if (txr->tx_buf_ring == NULL)
05914             continue;
05915 
05916         for (j = 0; j < TX_DESC_CNT; ) {
05917             struct sw_tx_bd *tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[j];
05918             struct sk_buff *skb = tx_buf->skb;
05919             int k, last;
05920 
05921             if (skb == NULL) {
05922                 j++;
05923                 continue;
05924             }
05925 
05926             pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev,
05927                      pci_unmap_addr(tx_buf, mapping),
05928                      skb_headlen(skb),
05929                      PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
05930 
05931             tx_buf->skb = NULL;
05932 
05933             last = tx_buf->nr_frags;
05934             j++;
05935             for (k = 0; k < last; k++, j++) {
05936                 tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[TX_RING_IDX(j)];
05937                 pci_unmap_page(bp->pdev,
05938                     pci_unmap_addr(tx_buf, mapping),
05939                     skb_shinfo(skb)->frags[k].size,
05940                     PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
05941             }
05942             dev_kfree_skb(skb);
05943         }
05944     }
05945 }
05946 
05947 static void
05948 bnx2_free_rx_skbs(struct bnx2 *bp)
05949 {
05950     int i;
05951 
05952     for (i = 0; i < bp->num_rx_rings; i++) {
05953         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
05954         struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
05955         int j;
05956 
05957         if (rxr->rx_buf_ring == NULL)
05958             return;
05959 
05960         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_ring_idx; j++) {
05961             struct sw_bd *rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[j];
05962             struct sk_buff *skb = rx_buf->skb;
05963 
05964             if (skb == NULL)
05965                 continue;
05966 
05967             pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev,
05968                      pci_unmap_addr(rx_buf, mapping),
05969                      bp->rx_buf_use_size,
05970                      PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
05971 
05972             rx_buf->skb = NULL;
05973 
05974             dev_kfree_skb(skb);
05975         }
05976         for (j = 0; j < bp->rx_max_pg_ring_idx; j++)
05977             bnx2_free_rx_page(bp, rxr, j);
05978     }
05979 }
05980 
05981 static void
05982 bnx2_free_skbs(struct bnx2 *bp)
05983 {
05984     bnx2_free_tx_skbs(bp);
05985     bnx2_free_rx_skbs(bp);
05986 }
05987 
05988 static int
05989 bnx2_reset_nic(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 reset_code)
05990 {
05991     int rc;
05992 
05993     rc = bnx2_reset_chip(bp, reset_code);
05994     bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
05995     if (rc)
05996         return rc;
05997 
05998     if ((rc = bnx2_init_chip(bp)) != 0)
05999         return rc;
06000 
06001     bnx2_init_all_rings(bp);
06002     return 0;
06003 }
06004 
06005 static int
06006 bnx2_init_nic(struct bnx2 *bp, int reset_phy)
06007 {
06008     int rc;
06009 
06010     if ((rc = bnx2_reset_nic(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET)) != 0)
06011         return rc;
06012 
06013     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06014     bnx2_init_phy(bp, reset_phy);
06015     bnx2_set_link(bp);
06016     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
06017         bnx2_remote_phy_event(bp);
06018     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06019     return 0;
06020 }
06021 
06022 static int
06023 bnx2_shutdown_chip(struct bnx2 *bp)
06024 {
06025     u32 reset_code;
06026 
06027     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL)
06028         reset_code = BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_UNLOAD_LNK_DN;
06029     else if (bp->wol)
06030         reset_code = BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_SUSPEND_WOL;
06031     else
06032         reset_code = BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_SUSPEND_NO_WOL;
06033 
06034     return bnx2_reset_chip(bp, reset_code);
06035 }
06036

06071         { 0x0c04, BNX2_FL_NOT_5709, 0x00000000, 0x03ff0001 },
06072         { 0x0c08, BNX2_FL_NOT_5709,  0x0f0ff073, 0x00000000 },
06073 
06074         { 0x1000, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00000001 },
06075         { 0x1004, BNX2_FL_NOT_5709, 0x00000000, 0x000f0001 },
06076 
06077         { 0x1408, 0, 0x01c00800, 0x00000000 },
06078         { 0x149c, 0, 0x8000ffff, 0x00000000 },
06079         { 0x14a8, 0, 0x00000000, 0x000001ff },

06094         { 0x2810, 0, 0xffff0000, 0x00000000 },
06095         { 0x2814, 0, 0xffff0000, 0x00000000 },
06096         { 0x2818, 0, 0xffff0000, 0x00000000 },
06097         { 0x281c, 0, 0xffff0000, 0x00000000 },
06098         { 0x2834, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06099         { 0x2840, 0, 0x00000000, 0xffffffff },
06100         { 0x2844, 0, 0x00000000, 0xffffffff },
06101         { 0x2848, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06102         { 0x284c, 0, 0xf800f800, 0x07ff07ff },
06103 
06104         { 0x2c00, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00000011 },
06105         { 0x2c04, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00030007 },
06106 
06107         { 0x3c00, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00000001 },
06108         { 0x3c04, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00070000 },
06109         { 0x3c08, 0, 0x00007f71, 0x07f00000 },
06110         { 0x3c0c, 0, 0x1f3ffffc, 0x00000000 },
06111         { 0x3c10, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06112         { 0x3c14, 0, 0x00000000, 0xffffffff },
06113         { 0x3c18, 0, 0x00000000, 0xffffffff },
06114         { 0x3c1c, 0, 0xfffff000, 0x00000000 },
06115         { 0x3c20, 0, 0xffffff00, 0x00000000 },
06116 
06117         { 0x5004, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0000007f },
06118         { 0x5008, 0, 0x0f0007ff, 0x00000000 },
06119 
06120         { 0x5c00, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00000001 },
06121         { 0x5c04, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0003000f },
06122         { 0x5c08, 0, 0x00000003, 0x00000000 },
06123         { 0x5c0c, 0, 0x0000fff8, 0x00000000 },
06124         { 0x5c10, 0, 0x00000000, 0xffffffff },
06125         { 0x5c80, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0f7113f1 },
06126         { 0x5c84, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0000f333 },
06127         { 0x5c88, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00077373 },
06128         { 0x5c8c, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0007f737 },
06129 
06130         { 0x6808, 0, 0x0000ff7f, 0x00000000 },
06131         { 0x680c, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06132         { 0x6810, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06133         { 0x6814, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06134         { 0x6818, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06135         { 0x681c, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06136         { 0x6820, 0, 0x00ff00ff, 0x00000000 },
06137         { 0x6824, 0, 0x00ff00ff, 0x00000000 },
06138         { 0x6828, 0, 0x00ff00ff, 0x00000000 },
06139         { 0x682c, 0, 0x03ff03ff, 0x00000000 },
06140         { 0x6830, 0, 0x03ff03ff, 0x00000000 },
06141         { 0x6834, 0, 0x03ff03ff, 0x00000000 },
06142         { 0x6838, 0, 0x03ff03ff, 0x00000000 },
06143         { 0x683c, 0, 0x0000ffff, 0x00000000 },
06144         { 0x6840, 0, 0x00000ff0, 0x00000000 },
06145         { 0x6844, 0, 0x00ffff00, 0x00000000 },
06146         { 0x684c, 0, 0xffffffff, 0x00000000 },
06147         { 0x6850, 0, 0x7f7f7f7f, 0x00000000 },
06148         { 0x6854, 0, 0x7f7f7f7f, 0x00000000 },
06149         { 0x6858, 0, 0x7f7f7f7f, 0x00000000 },
06150         { 0x685c, 0, 0x7f7f7f7f, 0x00000000 },
06151         { 0x6908, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0001ff0f },
06152         { 0x690c, 0, 0x00000000, 0x0ffe00f0 },
06153 
06154         { 0xffff, 0, 0x00000000, 0x00000000 },
06155     };
06156 
06157     ret = 0;
06158     is_5709 = 0;
06159     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
06160         is_5709 = 1;
06161 
06162     for (i = 0; reg_tbl[i].offset != 0xffff; i++) {
06163         u32 offset, rw_mask, ro_mask, save_val, val;
06164         u16 flags = reg_tbl[i].flags;
06165 
06166         if (is_5709 && (flags & BNX2_FL_NOT_5709))
06167             continue;
06168 
06169         offset = (u32) reg_tbl[i].offset;
06170         rw_mask = reg_tbl[i].rw_mask;
06171         ro_mask = reg_tbl[i].ro_mask;
06172 
06173         save_val = readl(bp->regview + offset);
06174 
06175         writel(0, bp->regview + offset);
06176 
06177         val = readl(bp->regview + offset);
06178         if ((val & rw_mask) != 0) {
06179             goto reg_test_err;
06180         }
06181 
06182         if ((val & ro_mask) != (save_val & ro_mask)) {
06183             goto reg_test_err;
06184         }
06185 
06186         writel(0xffffffff, bp->regview + offset);
06187 
06188         val = readl(bp->regview + offset);
06189         if ((val & rw_mask) != rw_mask) {
06190             goto reg_test_err;
06191         }
06192 
06193         if ((val & ro_mask) != (save_val & ro_mask)) {
06194             goto reg_test_err;
06195         }
06196 
06197         writel(save_val, bp->regview + offset);
06198         continue;
06199 
06200 reg_test_err:
06201         writel(save_val, bp->regview + offset);
06202         ret = -ENODEV;
06203         break;
06204     }
06205     return ret;
06206 }
06207 
06208 static int
06209 bnx2_do_mem_test(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 start, u32 size)
06210 {
06211     static const u32 test_pattern[] = { 0x00000000, 0xffffffff, 0x55555555,
06212         0xaaaaaaaa , 0xaa55aa55, 0x55aa55aa };
06213     int i;
06214 
06215     for (i = 0; i < sizeof(test_pattern) / 4; i++) {
06216         u32 offset;
06217 
06218         for (offset = 0; offset < size; offset += 4) {
06219 
06220             bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, start + offset, test_pattern[i]);
06221 
06222             if (bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, start + offset) !=
06223                 test_pattern[i]) {
06224                 return -ENODEV;
06225             }
06226         }
06227     }
06228     return 0;
06229 }
06230 
06231 static int
06232 bnx2_test_memory(struct bnx2 *bp)
06233 {
06234     int ret = 0;
06235     int i;
06236     static struct mem_entry {
06237         u32   offset;
06238         u32   len;
06239     } mem_tbl_5706[] = {
06240         { 0x60000,  0x4000 },
06241         { 0xa0000,  0x3000 },
06242         { 0xe0000,  0x4000 },
06243         { 0x120000, 0x4000 },
06244         { 0x1a0000, 0x4000 },
06245         { 0x160000, 0x4000 },
06246         { 0xffffffff, 0    },
06247     },
06248     mem_tbl_5709[] = {
06249         { 0x60000,  0x4000 },
06250         { 0xa0000,  0x3000 },
06251         { 0xe0000,  0x4000 },
06252         { 0x120000, 0x4000 },
06253         { 0x1a0000, 0x4000 },
06254         { 0xffffffff, 0    },
06255     };
06256     struct mem_entry *mem_tbl;
06257 
06258     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
06259         mem_tbl = mem_tbl_5709;
06260     else
06261         mem_tbl = mem_tbl_5706;
06262 
06263     for (i = 0; mem_tbl[i].offset != 0xffffffff; i++) {
06264         if ((ret = bnx2_do_mem_test(bp, mem_tbl[i].offset,
06265             mem_tbl[i].len)) != 0) {
06266             return ret;
06267         }
06268     }
06269 
06270     return ret;
06271 }
06272 
06273 #define BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK   0
06274 #define BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK   1
06275 
06276 static int
06277 bnx2_run_loopback(struct bnx2 *bp, int loopback_mode)
06278 {
06279     unsigned int pkt_size, num_pkts, i;
06280     struct sk_buff *skb, *rx_skb;
06281     unsigned char *packet;
06282     u16 rx_start_idx, rx_idx;
06283     dma_addr_t map;
06284     struct tx_bd *txbd;
06285     struct sw_bd *rx_buf;
06286     struct l2_fhdr *rx_hdr;
06287     int ret = -ENODEV;
06288     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0], *tx_napi;
06289     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
06290     struct bnx2_rx_ring_info *rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
06291 
06292     tx_napi = bnapi;
06293 
06294     txr = &tx_napi->tx_ring;
06295     rxr = &bnapi->rx_ring;
06296     if (loopback_mode == BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK) {
06297         bp->loopback = MAC_LOOPBACK;
06298         bnx2_set_mac_loopback(bp);
06299     }
06300     else if (loopback_mode == BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK) {
06301         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
06302             return 0;
06303 
06304         bp->loopback = PHY_LOOPBACK;
06305         bnx2_set_phy_loopback(bp);
06306     }
06307     else
06308         return -EINVAL;
06309 
06310     pkt_size = min(bp->dev->mtu + ETH_HLEN, bp->rx_jumbo_thresh - 4);
06311     skb = netdev_alloc_skb(bp->dev, pkt_size);
06312     if (!skb)
06313         return -ENOMEM;
06314     packet = skb_put(skb, pkt_size);
06315     memcpy(packet, bp->dev->dev_addr, 6);
06316     memset(packet + 6, 0x0, 8);
06317     for (i = 14; i < pkt_size; i++)
06318         packet[i] = (unsigned char) (i & 0xff);
06319 
06320     map = pci_map_single(bp->pdev, skb->data, pkt_size,
06321         PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
06322 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x02061b)
06323     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(bp->pdev, map)) {
06324 #else
06325     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(map)) {
06326 #endif
06327         dev_kfree_skb(skb);
06328         return -EIO;
06329     }
06330 
06331     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND,
06332            bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW_WO_INT);
06333 
06334     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
06335 
06336     udelay(5);
06337     rx_start_idx = bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi);
06338 
06339     num_pkts = 0;
06340 
06341     txbd = &txr->tx_desc_ring[TX_RING_IDX(txr->tx_prod)];
06342 
06343     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) map >> 32;
06344     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) map & 0xffffffff;
06345     txbd->tx_bd_mss_nbytes = pkt_size;
06346     txbd->tx_bd_vlan_tag_flags = TX_BD_FLAGS_START | TX_BD_FLAGS_END;
06347 
06348     num_pkts++;
06349     txr->tx_prod = NEXT_TX_BD(txr->tx_prod);
06350     txr->tx_prod_bseq += pkt_size;
06351 
06352     REG_WR16(bp, txr->tx_bidx_addr, txr->tx_prod);
06353     REG_WR(bp, txr->tx_bseq_addr, txr->tx_prod_bseq);
06354 
06355     udelay(100);
06356 
06357     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND,
06358            bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW_WO_INT);
06359 
06360     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
06361 
06362     udelay(5);
06363 
06364     pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev, map, pkt_size, PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
06365     dev_kfree_skb(skb);
06366 
06367     if (bnx2_get_hw_tx_cons(tx_napi) != txr->tx_prod)
06368         goto loopback_test_done;
06369 
06370     rx_idx = bnx2_get_hw_rx_cons(bnapi);
06371     if (rx_idx != rx_start_idx + num_pkts) {
06372         goto loopback_test_done;
06373     }
06374 
06375     rx_buf = &rxr->rx_buf_ring[rx_start_idx];
06376     rx_skb = rx_buf->skb;
06377 
06378     rx_hdr = (struct l2_fhdr *) rx_skb->data;
06379     skb_reserve(rx_skb, BNX2_RX_OFFSET);
06380 
06381     pci_dma_sync_single_for_cpu(bp->pdev,
06382         pci_unmap_addr(rx_buf, mapping),
06383         bp->rx_buf_size, PCI_DMA_FROMDEVICE);
06384 
06385     if (rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_status &
06386         (L2_FHDR_ERRORS_BAD_CRC |
06387         L2_FHDR_ERRORS_PHY_DECODE |
06388         L2_FHDR_ERRORS_ALIGNMENT |
06389         L2_FHDR_ERRORS_TOO_SHORT |
06390         L2_FHDR_ERRORS_GIANT_FRAME)) {
06391 
06392         goto loopback_test_done;
06393     }
06394 
06395     if ((rx_hdr->l2_fhdr_pkt_len - 4) != pkt_size) {
06396         goto loopback_test_done;
06397     }
06398 
06399     for (i = 14; i < pkt_size; i++) {
06400         if (*(rx_skb->data + i) != (unsigned char) (i & 0xff)) {
06401             goto loopback_test_done;
06402         }
06403     }
06404 
06405     ret = 0;
06406 
06407 loopback_test_done:
06408     bp->loopback = 0;
06409     return ret;
06410 }
06411 
06412 #define BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK_FAILED    1
06413 #define BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK_FAILED    2
06414 #define BNX2_LOOPBACK_FAILED        (BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK_FAILED | \
06415                      BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK_FAILED)
06416 
06417 static int
06418 bnx2_test_loopback(struct bnx2 *bp)
06419 {
06420     int rc = 0;
06421 
06422     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
06423         return BNX2_LOOPBACK_FAILED;
06424 
06425     bnx2_reset_nic(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET);
06426     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06427     bnx2_init_phy(bp, 1);
06428     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06429     if (bnx2_run_loopback(bp, BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK))
06430         rc |= BNX2_MAC_LOOPBACK_FAILED;
06431     if (bnx2_run_loopback(bp, BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK))
06432         rc |= BNX2_PHY_LOOPBACK_FAILED;
06433     return rc;
06434 }
06435 
06436 #define NVRAM_SIZE 0x200
06437 #define CRC32_RESIDUAL 0xdebb20e3
06438 
06439 static int
06440 bnx2_test_nvram(struct bnx2 *bp)
06441 {
06442     __be32 buf[NVRAM_SIZE / 4];
06443     u8 *data = (u8 *) buf;
06444     int rc = 0;
06445     u32 magic, csum;
06446 
06447     if ((rc = bnx2_nvram_read(bp, 0, data, 4)) != 0)
06448         goto test_nvram_done;
06449 
06450         magic = be32_to_cpu(buf[0]);
06451     if (magic != 0x669955aa) {
06452         rc = -ENODEV;
06453         goto test_nvram_done;
06454     }
06455 
06456     if ((rc = bnx2_nvram_read(bp, 0x100, data, NVRAM_SIZE)) != 0)
06457         goto test_nvram_done;
06458 
06459     csum = ether_crc_le(0x100, data);
06460     if (csum != CRC32_RESIDUAL) {
06461         rc = -ENODEV;
06462         goto test_nvram_done;
06463     }
06464 
06465     csum = ether_crc_le(0x100, data + 0x100);
06466     if (csum != CRC32_RESIDUAL) {
06467         rc = -ENODEV;
06468     }
06469 
06470 test_nvram_done:
06471     return rc;
06472 }
06473 
06474 static int
06475 bnx2_test_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
06476 {
06477     u32 bmsr;
06478 
06479     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
06480         return -ENODEV;
06481 
06482     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP) {
06483         int i;
06484 
06485         for (i = 0; i < 6 && !bp->link_up; i++) {
06486             if (bnx2_msleep_interruptible(500))
06487                 break;
06488         }
06489         if (bp->link_up)
06490             return 0;
06491         return -ENODEV;
06492     }
06493     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06494     bnx2_enable_bmsr1(bp);
06495     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr1, &bmsr);
06496     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmsr1, &bmsr);
06497     bnx2_disable_bmsr1(bp);
06498     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
06499 
06500     if (bmsr & BMSR_LSTATUS) {
06501         return 0;
06502     }
06503     return -ENODEV;
06504 }
06505 
06506 static int
06507 bnx2_test_intr(struct bnx2 *bp)
06508 {
06509     int i;
06510     u16 status_idx;
06511 
06512     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
06513         return -ENODEV;
06514 
06515     status_idx = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD) & 0xffff;
06516 
06517     /* This register is not touched during run-time. */
06518     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND, bp->hc_cmd | BNX2_HC_COMMAND_COAL_NOW);
06519     REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND);
06520 
06521     for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
06522         if ((REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_INT_ACK_CMD) & 0xffff) !=
06523             status_idx) {
06524 
06525             break;
06526         }
06527 
06528         bnx2_msleep_interruptible(10);
06529     }
06530     if (i < 10)
06531         return 0;
06532 
06533     return -ENODEV;
06534 }
06535 
06536 /* Determining link for parallel detection. */
06537 static int
06538 bnx2_5706_serdes_has_link(struct bnx2 *bp)
06539 {
06540     u32 mode_ctl, an_dbg, exp;
06541 
06542     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_NO_PARALLEL)
06543         return 0;
06544 
06545     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, MISC_SHDW_MODE_CTL);
06546     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &mode_ctl);
06547 
06548     if (!(mode_ctl & MISC_SHDW_MODE_CTL_SIG_DET))
06549         return 0;
06550 
06551     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG);
06552     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &an_dbg);
06553     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &an_dbg);
06554 
06555     if (an_dbg & (MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG_NOSYNC | MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG_RUDI_INVALID))
06556         return 0;
06557 
06558     bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_ADDRESS, MII_EXPAND_REG1);
06559     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, &exp);
06560     bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_DSP_RW_PORT, &exp);
06561 
06562     if (exp & MII_EXPAND_REG1_RUDI_C)   /* receiving CONFIG */
06563         return 0;
06564 
06565     return 1;
06566 }
06567 
06568 static void
06569 bnx2_5706_serdes_timer(struct bnx2 *bp)
06570 {
06571     int check_link = 1;
06572 
06573     spin_lock(&bp->phy_lock);
06574     if (bp->serdes_an_pending) {
06575         bp->serdes_an_pending--;
06576         check_link = 0;
06577     } else if ((bp->link_up == 0) && (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)) {
06578         u32 bmcr;
06579 
06580         bp->current_interval = BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL;
06581 
06582         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
06583 
06584         if (bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE) {
06585             if (bnx2_5706_serdes_has_link(bp)) {
06586                 bmcr &= ~BMCR_ANENABLE;
06587                 bmcr |= BMCR_SPEED1000 | BMCR_FULLDPLX;
06588                 bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr);
06589                 bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT;
06590             }
06591         }
06592     }
06593     else if ((bp->link_up) && (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) &&
06594          (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT)) {
06595         u32 phy2;
06596 
06597         bnx2_write_phy(bp, 0x17, 0x0f01);
06598         bnx2_read_phy(bp, 0x15, &phy2);
06599         if (phy2 & 0x20) {
06600             u32 bmcr;
06601 
06602             bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
06603             bmcr |= BMCR_ANENABLE;
06604             bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr);
06605 
06606             bp->phy_flags &= ~BNX2_PHY_FLAG_PARALLEL_DETECT;
06607         }
06608     } else
06609         bp->current_interval = BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL;
06610 
06611     if (check_link) {
06612         u32 val;
06613 
06614         bnx2_write_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG);
06615         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &val);
06616         bnx2_read_phy(bp, MII_BNX2_MISC_SHADOW, &val);
06617 
06618         if (bp->link_up && (val & MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG_NOSYNC)) {
06619             if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_FORCED_DOWN)) {
06620                 bnx2_5706s_force_link_dn(bp, 1);
06621                 bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_FORCED_DOWN;
06622             } else
06623                 bnx2_set_link(bp);
06624         } else if (!bp->link_up && !(val & MISC_SHDW_AN_DBG_NOSYNC))
06625             bnx2_set_link(bp);
06626     }
06627     spin_unlock(&bp->phy_lock);
06628 }
06629 
06630 static void
06631 bnx2_5708_serdes_timer(struct bnx2 *bp)
06632 {
06633     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
06634         return;
06635 
06636     if ((bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE) == 0) {
06637         bp->serdes_an_pending = 0;
06638         return;
06639     }
06640 
06641     spin_lock(&bp->phy_lock);
06642     if (bp->serdes_an_pending)
06643         bp->serdes_an_pending--;
06644     else if ((bp->link_up == 0) && (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)) {
06645         u32 bmcr;
06646 
06647         bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
06648         if (bmcr & BMCR_ANENABLE) {
06649             bnx2_enable_forced_2g5(bp);
06650             bp->current_interval = BNX2_SERDES_FORCED_TIMEOUT;
06651         } else {
06652             bnx2_disable_forced_2g5(bp);
06653             bp->serdes_an_pending = 2;
06654             bp->current_interval = BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL;
06655         }
06656 
06657     } else
06658         bp->current_interval = BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL;
06659 
06660     spin_unlock(&bp->phy_lock);
06661 }
06662 
06663 static void
06664 bnx2_timer(unsigned long data)
06665 {
06666     struct bnx2 *bp = (struct bnx2 *) data;
06667 
06668     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
06669         return;
06670 
06671     if (atomic_read(&bp->intr_sem) != 0)
06672         goto bnx2_restart_timer;
06673 
06674 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06675     if ((bp->flags & (BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI | BNX2_FLAG_ONE_SHOT_MSI)) ==
06676          BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI)
06677         bnx2_chk_missed_msi(bp);
06678 #endif
06679 
06680     bnx2_send_heart_beat(bp);
06681 
06682     bp->stats_blk->stat_FwRxDrop =
06683         bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_FW_RX_DROP_COUNT);
06684 
06685     /* workaround occasional corrupted counters */
06686     if ((bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_BROKEN_STATS) && bp->stats_ticks)
06687         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMMAND, bp->hc_cmd |
06688                         BNX2_HC_COMMAND_STATS_NOW);
06689 
06690     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
06691         if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706)
06692             bnx2_5706_serdes_timer(bp);
06693         else
06694             bnx2_5708_serdes_timer(bp);
06695     }
06696 
06697 bnx2_restart_timer:
06698     mod_timer(&bp->timer, jiffies + bp->current_interval);
06699 }
06700 
06701 static int
06702 bnx2_request_irq(struct bnx2 *bp)
06703 {
06704     unsigned long flags;
06705     struct bnx2_irq *irq;
06706     int rc = 0, i;
06707 
06708     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI_OR_MSIX)
06709         flags = 0;
06710     else
06711         flags = IRQF_SHARED;
06712 
06713     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
06714         irq = &bp->irq_tbl[i];
06715         rc = request_irq(irq->vector, irq->handler, flags, irq->name,
06716                  &bp->bnx2_napi[i]);
06717         if (rc)
06718             break;
06719         irq->requested = 1;
06720     }
06721     return rc;
06722 }
06723 
06724 static void
06725 bnx2_free_irq(struct bnx2 *bp)
06726 {
06727     struct bnx2_irq *irq;
06728     int i;
06729 
06730     for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
06731         irq = &bp->irq_tbl[i];
06732         if (irq->requested)
06733             free_irq(irq->vector, &bp->bnx2_napi[i]);
06734         irq->requested = 0;
06735     }
06736 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06737     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI)
06738         pci_disable_msi(bp->pdev);
06739     else if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)
06740         pci_disable_msix(bp->pdev);
06741 
06742     bp->flags &= ~(BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI_OR_MSIX | BNX2_FLAG_ONE_SHOT_MSI);
06743 #endif
06744 }
06745 
06746 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06747 static void
06748 bnx2_enable_msix(struct bnx2 *bp, int msix_vecs)
06749 {
06750 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
06751     int i, rc;
06752     struct msix_entry msix_ent[BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC];
06753     struct net_device *dev = bp->dev;
06754     const int len = sizeof(bp->irq_tbl[0].name);
06755 
06756     bnx2_setup_msix_tbl(bp);
06757     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_MSIX_CONTROL, BNX2_MAX_MSIX_HW_VEC - 1);
06758     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_MSIX_TBL_OFF_BIR, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW2_BASE);
06759     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_PCI_MSIX_PBA_OFF_BIT, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW3_BASE);
06760 
06761     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++) {
06762         msix_ent[i].entry = i;
06763         msix_ent[i].vector = 0;
06764     }
06765 
06766     rc = pci_enable_msix(bp->pdev, msix_ent, BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC);
06767     if (rc != 0)
06768         return;
06769 
06770     bp->irq_nvecs = msix_vecs;
06771     bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX | BNX2_FLAG_ONE_SHOT_MSI;
06772     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++) {
06773         bp->irq_tbl[i].vector = msix_ent[i].vector;
06774         snprintf(bp->irq_tbl[i].name, len, "%s-%d", dev->name, i);
06775         bp->irq_tbl[i].handler = bnx2_msi_1shot;
06776     }
06777 #endif
06778 }
06779 #endif
06780 
06781 static void
06782 bnx2_setup_int_mode(struct bnx2 *bp, int dis_msi)
06783 {
06784 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06785     int cpus = num_online_cpus();
06786 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
06787     int msix_vecs = min(cpus, 4);
06788     if(force_netq_param[bp->index] != BNX2_OPTION_UNSET)
06789         msix_vecs = min(force_netq_param[bp->index], RX_MAX_RSS_RINGS);
06790 
06791     /* Once is for the default queuue */
06792     msix_vecs += 1;
06793 #else
06794     int msix_vecs = min(cpus + 1, RX_MAX_RINGS);
06795 #endif
06796 #endif
06797 
06798     bp->irq_tbl[0].handler = bnx2_interrupt;
06799     strcpy(bp->irq_tbl[0].name, bp->dev->name);
06800     bp->irq_nvecs = 1;
06801     bp->irq_tbl[0].vector = bp->pdev->irq;
06802 
06803 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06804     if ((bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_MSIX_CAP) && !dis_msi && cpus > 1)
06805         bnx2_enable_msix(bp, msix_vecs);
06806 
06807     if ((bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_MSI_CAP) && !dis_msi &&
06808         !(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)) {
06809         if (pci_enable_msi(bp->pdev) == 0) {
06810             bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI;
06811             if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
06812                 bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_ONE_SHOT_MSI;
06813                 bp->irq_tbl[0].handler = bnx2_msi_1shot;
06814             } else
06815                 bp->irq_tbl[0].handler = bnx2_msi;
06816 
06817             bp->irq_tbl[0].vector = bp->pdev->irq;
06818         }
06819     }
06820 #endif
06821 
06822 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
06823     bp->num_tx_rings = 1;
06824 #else
06825 #if defined(__VMKLNX__)
06826 #if defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
06827     bp->num_tx_rings = bp->irq_nvecs;
06828     bp->dev->real_num_tx_queues = bp->num_tx_rings;
06829 #else
06830     bp->num_tx_rings = 1;
06831 #endif
06832 #else
06833     bp->num_tx_rings = rounddown_pow_of_two(bp->irq_nvecs);
06834 #endif
06835     bp->dev->real_num_tx_queues = bp->num_tx_rings;
06836 #endif
06837     bp->num_rx_rings = bp->irq_nvecs;
06838 }
06839 
06840 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
06841 static int
06842 bnx2_open(struct net_device *dev)
06843 {
06844     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
06845     int rc;
06846 
06847     netif_carrier_off(dev);
06848 
06849     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
06850     bnx2_disable_int(bp);
06851 
06852     bnx2_setup_int_mode(bp, disable_msi);
06853 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
06854     bnx2_napi_enable(bp);
06855 #endif
06856     rc = bnx2_alloc_mem(bp);
06857     if (rc)
06858         goto open_err;
06859 
06860     rc = bnx2_request_irq(bp);
06861     if (rc)
06862         goto open_err;
06863 
06864     rc = bnx2_init_nic(bp, 1);
06865     if (rc)
06866         goto open_err;
06867 
06868     mod_timer(&bp->timer, jiffies + bp->current_interval);
06869 
06870     atomic_set(&bp->intr_sem, 0);
06871 
06872     bnx2_enable_int(bp);
06873 
06874 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
06875     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI) {
06876         /* Test MSI to make sure it is working
06877          * If MSI test fails, go back to INTx mode
06878          */
06879         if (bnx2_test_intr(bp) != 0) {
06880             printk(KERN_WARNING PFX "%s: No interrupt was generated"
06881                    " using MSI, switching to INTx mode. Please"
06882                    " report this failure to the PCI maintainer"
06883                    " and include system chipset information.\n",
06884                    bp->dev->name);
06885 
06886             bnx2_disable_int(bp);
06887             bnx2_free_irq(bp);
06888 
06889             bnx2_setup_int_mode(bp, 1);
06890 
06891             rc = bnx2_init_nic(bp, 0);
06892 
06893             if (!rc)
06894                 rc = bnx2_request_irq(bp);
06895 
06896             if (rc) {
06897                 del_timer_sync(&bp->timer);
06898                 goto open_err;
06899             }
06900             bnx2_enable_int(bp);
06901         }
06902     }
06903     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSI)
06904         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: using MSI\n", dev->name);
06905     else if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)
06906         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: using MSIX\n", dev->name);
06907 #endif
06908 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
06909     if (bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp))
06910         bnx2_open_netqueue_hw(bp);
06911 #endif
06912 
06913     netif_tx_start_all_queues(dev);
06914 
06915     return 0;
06916 
06917 open_err:
06918 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
06919     bnx2_napi_disable(bp);
06920 #endif
06921     bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
06922     bnx2_free_irq(bp);
06923     bnx2_free_mem(bp);
06924     return rc;
06925 }
06926 
06927 static void
06928 #if defined(INIT_DELAYED_WORK_DEFERRABLE) || defined(INIT_WORK_NAR)
06929 bnx2_reset_task(struct work_struct *work)
06930 #else
06931 bnx2_reset_task(void *data)
06932 #endif
06933 {
06934 #if defined(INIT_DELAYED_WORK_DEFERRABLE) || defined(INIT_WORK_NAR)
06935     struct bnx2 *bp = container_of(work, struct bnx2, reset_task);
06936 #else
06937     struct bnx2 *bp = data;
06938 #endif
06939 
06940     rtnl_lock();
06941     if (!netif_running(bp->dev)) {
06942         rtnl_unlock();
06943         return;
06944     }
06945 
06946     bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
06947 
06948     bnx2_init_nic(bp, 1);
06949 
06950     atomic_set(&bp->intr_sem, 1);
06951     bnx2_netif_start(bp);
06952     rtnl_unlock();
06953 }
06954 
06955 static void bnx2_dump_ftq(struct bnx2 *bp)
06956 {
06957     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "<--- start FTQ dump on %s --->\n", bp->dev->name);
