06959            REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RV2P_PFTQ_CTL));
06960     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_RV2P_TFTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06961            REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RV2P_TFTQ_CTL));
06962     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_RV2P_MFTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06963            REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RV2P_MFTQ_CTL));
06964     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_TBDR_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06965            REG_RD(bp, BNX2_TBDR_FTQ_CTL));
06966     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_TDMA_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06967            REG_RD(bp, BNX2_TDMA_FTQ_CTL));
06968     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_TXP_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06969            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_FTQ_CTL));
06970     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_TPAT_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06971            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_FTQ_CTL));
06972     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_RXP_CFTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06973            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CFTQ_CTL));
06974     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_RXP_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06975            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_FTQ_CTL));
06976     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_COM_COMXQ_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06977            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_COMXQ_FTQ_CTL));
06978     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_COM_COMTQ_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06979            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_COMTQ_FTQ_CTL));
06980     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_COM_COMQ_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06981            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_COMQ_FTQ_CTL));
06982     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BNX2_CP_CPQ_FTQ_CTL %x\n", bp->dev->name,
06983            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPQ_FTQ_CTL));
06984     printk(KERN_ERR PFX
06985            "%s: TXP mode %x state %x evt_mask %x pc %x pc %x instr %x\n",
06986            bp->dev->name,
06987            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_MODE),
06988            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_STATE),
06989            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_EVENT_MASK),
06990            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
06991            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
06992            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TXP_CPU_INSTRUCTION));
06993     printk(KERN_ERR PFX
06994            "%s: TPAT mode %x state %x evt_mask %x pc %x pc %x instr %x\n",
06995            bp->dev->name,
06996            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_MODE),
06997            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_STATE),
06998            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_EVENT_MASK),
06999            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07000            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07001            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_TPAT_CPU_INSTRUCTION));
07002     printk(KERN_ERR PFX
07003            "%s: RXP mode %x state %x evt_mask %x pc %x pc %x instr %x\n",
07004            bp->dev->name,
07005            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_MODE),
07006            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_STATE),
07007            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_EVENT_MASK),
07008            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07009            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07010            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_RXP_CPU_INSTRUCTION));
07011     printk(KERN_ERR PFX
07012            "%s: COM mode %x state %x evt_mask %x pc %x pc %x instr %x\n",
07013            bp->dev->name,
07014            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_MODE),
07015            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_STATE),
07016            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_EVENT_MASK),
07017            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07018            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07019            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_CPU_INSTRUCTION));
07020     printk(KERN_ERR PFX
07021            "%s: CP mode %x state %x evt_mask %x pc %x pc %x instr %x\n",
07022            bp->dev->name,
07023            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_MODE),
07024            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_STATE),
07025            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_EVENT_MASK),
07026            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07027            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_PROGRAM_COUNTER),
07028            bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_CPU_INSTRUCTION));
07029     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "<--- end FTQ dump on %s --->\n", bp->dev->name);
07030 }
07031 
07032 static void
07033 bnx2_dump_state(struct bnx2 *bp)
07034 {
07035     struct net_device *dev = bp->dev;
07036 
07037     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s DEBUG: intr_sem[%x]\n", dev->name,
07038         atomic_read(&bp->intr_sem));
07039     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s DEBUG: EMAC_TX_STATUS[%08x] "
07040                 "RPM_MGMT_PKT_CTRL[%08x]\n", dev->name,
07041         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_EMAC_TX_STATUS),
07042         REG_RD(bp, BNX2_RPM_MGMT_PKT_CTRL));
07043     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s DEBUG: MCP_STATE_P0[%08x] MCP_STATE_P1[%08x]\n",
07044         dev->name, bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_MCP_STATE_P0),
07045         bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_MCP_STATE_P1));
07046     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s DEBUG: HC_STATS_INTERRUPT_STATUS[%08x]\n",
07047         dev->name, REG_RD(bp, BNX2_HC_STATS_INTERRUPT_STATUS));
07048     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX)
07049         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s DEBUG: PBA[%08x]\n", dev->name,
07050             REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCI_GRC_WINDOW3_BASE));
07051 }
07052 
07053 static void
07054 bnx2_tx_timeout(struct net_device *dev)
07055 {
07056     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07057 
07058     bnx2_dump_ftq(bp);
07059     bnx2_dump_state(bp);
07060 
07061     if (stop_on_tx_timeout) {
07062         printk(KERN_WARNING PFX
07063                "%s: prevent chip reset during tx timeout\n",
07064             bp->dev->name);
07065         return;
07066     }
07067 
07068     /* This allows the netif to be shutdown gracefully before resetting */
07069 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20600)
07070     schedule_work(&bp->reset_task);
07071 #else
07072     schedule_task(&bp->reset_task);
07073 #endif
07074 }
07075 
07076 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
07077 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
07078 static void
07079 bnx2_vlan_rx_register(struct net_device *dev, struct vlan_group *vlgrp)
07080 {
07081     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07082 
07083     if (netif_running(dev))
07084         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
07085 
07086     bp->vlgrp = vlgrp;
07087 
07088     if (!netif_running(dev))
07089         return;
07090 
07091     bnx2_set_rx_mode(dev);
07092     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN)
07093         bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_KEEP_VLAN_UPDATE, 0, 1);
07094 
07095     bnx2_netif_start(bp);
07096 }
07097 
07098 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x20616)
07099 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
07100 static void
07101 bnx2_vlan_rx_kill_vid(struct net_device *dev, uint16_t vid)
07102 {
07103     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07104 
07105     if (netif_running(dev))
07106         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
07107 
07108     vlan_group_set_device(bp->vlgrp, vid, NULL);
07109 
07110     if (!netif_running(dev))
07111         return;
07112 
07113     bnx2_set_rx_mode(dev);
07114     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_CAN_KEEP_VLAN)
07115         bnx2_fw_sync(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_KEEP_VLAN_UPDATE, 0, 1);
07116 
07117     bnx2_netif_start(bp);
07118 }
07119 #endif
07120 #endif
07121 
07122 /* Called with netif_tx_lock.
07123  * bnx2_tx_int() runs without netif_tx_lock unless it needs to call
07124  * netif_wake_queue().
07125  */
07126 static netdev_tx_t
07127 bnx2_start_xmit(struct sk_buff *skb, struct net_device *dev)
07128 {
07129     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07130     dma_addr_t mapping;
07131     struct tx_bd *txbd;
07132     struct sw_tx_bd *tx_buf;
07133     u32 len, vlan_tag_flags, last_frag, mss;
07134     u16 prod, ring_prod;
07135     int i;
07136 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
07137     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0];
07138     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
07139 #else
07140     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
07141     struct bnx2_tx_ring_info *txr;
07142     struct netdev_queue *txq;
07143 
07144     /*  Determine which tx ring we will be placed on */
07145     i = skb_get_queue_mapping(skb);
07146     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
07147     txr = &bnapi->tx_ring;
07148     txq = netdev_get_tx_queue(dev, i);
07149 #endif
07150 
07151     if (unlikely(bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) <
07152         (skb_shinfo(skb)->nr_frags + 1))) {
07153 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
07154         netif_stop_queue(dev);
07155 #else
07156         netif_tx_stop_queue(txq);
07157 #endif
07158         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: BUG! Tx ring full when queue awake!\n",
07159             dev->name);
07160 
07161         return NETDEV_TX_BUSY;
07162     }
07163     len = skb_headlen(skb);
07164     prod = txr->tx_prod;
07165     ring_prod = TX_RING_IDX(prod);
07166 
07167     vlan_tag_flags = 0;
07168     if (skb->ip_summed == CHECKSUM_PARTIAL) {
07169         vlan_tag_flags |= TX_BD_FLAGS_TCP_UDP_CKSUM;
07170     }
07171 
07172 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
07173     if (bp->vlgrp && vlan_tx_tag_present(skb)) {
07174         vlan_tag_flags |=
07175             (TX_BD_FLAGS_VLAN_TAG | (vlan_tx_tag_get(skb) << 16));
07176     }
07177 #endif
07178 #ifdef BCM_TSO 
07179     if ((mss = skb_shinfo(skb)->gso_size)) {
07180         u32 tcp_opt_len;
07181         struct iphdr *iph;
07182 
07183         tcp_opt_len = tcp_optlen(skb);
07184 
07185         if (skb_transport_offset(skb) + tcp_opt_len +
07186             sizeof(struct tcphdr) + mss >= skb->len)
07187             goto abort_tso;
07188 
07189         vlan_tag_flags |= TX_BD_FLAGS_SW_LSO;
07190 
07191 #ifndef BCM_NO_TSO6
07192         if (skb_shinfo(skb)->gso_type & SKB_GSO_TCPV6) {
07193             u32 tcp_off = skb_transport_offset(skb) -
07194                       sizeof(struct ipv6hdr) - ETH_HLEN;
07195 
07196             vlan_tag_flags |= ((tcp_opt_len >> 2) << 8) |
07197                       TX_BD_FLAGS_SW_FLAGS;
07198             if (likely(tcp_off == 0))
07199                 vlan_tag_flags &= ~TX_BD_FLAGS_TCP6_OFF0_MSK;
07200             else {
07201                 tcp_off >>= 3;
07202                 vlan_tag_flags |= ((tcp_off & 0x3) <<
07203                            TX_BD_FLAGS_TCP6_OFF0_SHL) |
07204                           ((tcp_off & 0x10) <<
07205                            TX_BD_FLAGS_TCP6_OFF4_SHL);
07206                 mss |= (tcp_off & 0xc) << TX_BD_TCP6_OFF2_SHL;
07207             }
07208         } else
07209 #endif
07210         {
07211             iph = ip_hdr(skb);
07212             if (tcp_opt_len || (iph->ihl > 5)) {
07213                 vlan_tag_flags |= ((iph->ihl - 5) +
07214                            (tcp_opt_len >> 2)) << 8;
07215             }
07216         }
07217     }
07218     else
07219 abort_tso:
07220 #endif
07221     {
07222         mss = 0;
07223     }
07224 
07225     mapping = pci_map_single(bp->pdev, skb->data, len, PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
07226 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x02061b)
07227     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(bp->pdev, mapping)) {
07228 #else
07229     if (pci_dma_mapping_error(mapping)) {
07230 #endif
07231         dev_kfree_skb(skb);
07232         return NETDEV_TX_OK;
07233     }
07234 
07235     tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[ring_prod];
07236     tx_buf->skb = skb;
07237     pci_unmap_addr_set(tx_buf, mapping, mapping);
07238 
07239     txbd = &txr->tx_desc_ring[ring_prod];
07240 
07241     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) mapping >> 32;
07242     txbd->tx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) mapping & 0xffffffff;
07243     txbd->tx_bd_mss_nbytes = len | (mss << 16);
07244     txbd->tx_bd_vlan_tag_flags = vlan_tag_flags | TX_BD_FLAGS_START;
07245 
07246     last_frag = skb_shinfo(skb)->nr_frags;
07247     tx_buf->nr_frags = last_frag;
07248     tx_buf->is_gso = skb_is_gso(skb);
07249 
07250     for (i = 0; i < last_frag; i++) {
07251         skb_frag_t *frag = &skb_shinfo(skb)->frags[i];
07252 
07253         prod = NEXT_TX_BD(prod);
07254         ring_prod = TX_RING_IDX(prod);
07255         txbd = &txr->tx_desc_ring[ring_prod];
07256 
07257         len = frag->size;
07258         mapping = pci_map_page(bp->pdev, frag->page, frag->page_offset,
07259             len, PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
07260 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x02061b)
07261         if (pci_dma_mapping_error(bp->pdev, mapping))
07262 #else
07263         if (pci_dma_mapping_error(mapping))
07264 #endif
07265             goto dma_error;
07266         pci_unmap_addr_set(&txr->tx_buf_ring[ring_prod], mapping,
07267                    mapping);
07268 
07269         txbd->tx_bd_haddr_hi = (u64) mapping >> 32;
07270         txbd->tx_bd_haddr_lo = (u64) mapping & 0xffffffff;
07271         txbd->tx_bd_mss_nbytes = len | (mss << 16);
07272         txbd->tx_bd_vlan_tag_flags = vlan_tag_flags;
07273 
07274     }
07275     txbd->tx_bd_vlan_tag_flags |= TX_BD_FLAGS_END;
07276 
07277     prod = NEXT_TX_BD(prod);
07278     txr->tx_prod_bseq += skb->len;
07279 
07280     REG_WR16(bp, txr->tx_bidx_addr, prod);
07281     REG_WR(bp, txr->tx_bseq_addr, txr->tx_prod_bseq);
07282 
07283     mmiowb();
07284 
07285     txr->tx_prod = prod;
07286 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE <= 0x2061e)
07287     dev->trans_start = jiffies;
07288 #endif
07289 
07290 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
07291     bnapi->tx_packets_sent++;
07292     wmb();
07293 #endif
07294 
07295     if (unlikely(bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) <= MAX_SKB_FRAGS)) {
07296 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
07297         netif_stop_queue(dev);
07298 #else
07299         netif_tx_stop_queue(txq);
07300 #endif
07301         if (bnx2_tx_avail(bp, txr) > bp->tx_wake_thresh)
07302 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
07303             netif_wake_queue(dev);
07304 #else
07305             netif_tx_wake_queue(txq);
07306 #endif
07307     }
07308 
07309     return NETDEV_TX_OK;
07310 dma_error:
07311     /* save value of frag that failed */
07312     last_frag = i;
07313 
07314     /* start back at beginning and unmap skb */
07315     prod = txr->tx_prod;
07316     ring_prod = TX_RING_IDX(prod);
07317     tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[ring_prod];
07318     tx_buf->skb = NULL;
07319     pci_unmap_single(bp->pdev, pci_unmap_addr(tx_buf, mapping),
07320              skb_headlen(skb), PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
07321 
07322     /* unmap remaining mapped pages */
07323     for (i = 0; i < last_frag; i++) {
07324         prod = NEXT_TX_BD(prod);
07325         ring_prod = TX_RING_IDX(prod);
07326         tx_buf = &txr->tx_buf_ring[ring_prod];
07327         pci_unmap_page(bp->pdev, pci_unmap_addr(tx_buf, mapping),
07328                    skb_shinfo(skb)->frags[i].size,
07329                    PCI_DMA_TODEVICE);
07330     }
07331 
07332     dev_kfree_skb(skb);
07333     return NETDEV_TX_OK;
07334 }
07335 
07336 
07337 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
07338 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
07339 static int
07340 bnx2_close(struct net_device *dev)
07341 {
07342     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07343 
07344 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20616)
07345     cancel_work_sync(&bp->reset_task);
07346 #endif
07347 
07348     netif_tx_disable(bp->dev);
07349     bp->dev->trans_start = jiffies; /* prevent tx timeout */
07350 
07351     if (bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp) &&
07352         (bp->netq_state == BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED))
07353         bnx2_netqueue_flush_all(bp);
07354     bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
07355 
07356     if (bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp))
07357         bnx2_close_netqueue_hw(bp);
07358 
07359     del_timer_sync(&bp->timer);
07360     if (bp->reset_failed == 0)
07361         bnx2_shutdown_chip(bp);
07362     bnx2_free_irq(bp);
07363     bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
07364     bnx2_free_mem(bp);
07365     bp->link_up = 0;
07366     netif_carrier_off(bp->dev);
07367     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D3hot);
07368 
07369     return 0;
07370 }
07371 #else
07372 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
07373 static int
07374 bnx2_close(struct net_device *dev)
07375 {
07376     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07377 
07378 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20616)
07379     cancel_work_sync(&bp->reset_task);
07380 #endif
07381 
07382     bnx2_disable_int_sync(bp);
07383 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
07384     bnx2_napi_disable(bp);
07385 #endif
07386     del_timer_sync(&bp->timer);
07387     bnx2_shutdown_chip(bp);
07388     bnx2_free_irq(bp);
07389     bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
07390     bnx2_free_mem(bp);
07391     bp->link_up = 0;
07392     netif_carrier_off(bp->dev);
07393     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D3hot);
07394     return 0;
07395 }
07396 #endif /* defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__) */
07397 
07398 #define GET_NET_STATS64(ctr)                    \
07399     (unsigned long) ((unsigned long) (ctr##_hi) << 32) +    \
07400     (unsigned long) (ctr##_lo)
07401 
07402 #define GET_NET_STATS32(ctr)        \
07403     (ctr##_lo)
07404 
07405 #if (BITS_PER_LONG == 64)
07406 #define GET_NET_STATS   GET_NET_STATS64
07407 #else
07408 #define GET_NET_STATS   GET_NET_STATS32
07409 #endif
07410 
07411 static struct net_device_stats *
07412 bnx2_get_stats(struct net_device *dev)
07413 {
07414     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07415     struct statistics_block *stats_blk = bp->stats_blk;
07416     struct net_device_stats *net_stats = &bp->net_stats;
07417 
07418     if (bp->stats_blk == NULL) {
07419         return net_stats;
07420     }
07421     net_stats->rx_packets =
07422         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCInUcastPkts) +
07423         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCInMulticastPkts) +
07424         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCInBroadcastPkts);
07425 
07426     net_stats->tx_packets =
07427         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCOutUcastPkts) +
07428         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCOutMulticastPkts) +
07429         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCOutBroadcastPkts);
07430 
07431     net_stats->rx_bytes =
07432         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCInOctets);
07433 
07434     net_stats->tx_bytes =
07435         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCOutOctets);
07436 
07437     net_stats->multicast =
07438         GET_NET_STATS(stats_blk->stat_IfHCOutMulticastPkts);
07439 
07440     net_stats->collisions =
07441         (unsigned long) stats_blk->stat_EtherStatsCollisions;
07442 
07443     net_stats->rx_length_errors =
07444         (unsigned long) (stats_blk->stat_EtherStatsUndersizePkts +
07445         stats_blk->stat_EtherStatsOverrsizePkts);
07446 
07447     net_stats->rx_over_errors =
07448         (unsigned long) (stats_blk->stat_IfInFTQDiscards +
07449         stats_blk->stat_IfInMBUFDiscards);
07450 
07451     net_stats->rx_frame_errors =
07452         (unsigned long) stats_blk->stat_Dot3StatsAlignmentErrors;
07453 
07454     net_stats->rx_crc_errors =
07455         (unsigned long) stats_blk->stat_Dot3StatsFCSErrors;
07456 
07457     net_stats->rx_errors = net_stats->rx_length_errors +
07458         net_stats->rx_over_errors + net_stats->rx_frame_errors +
07459         net_stats->rx_crc_errors;
07460 
07461     net_stats->tx_aborted_errors =
07462             (unsigned long) (stats_blk->stat_Dot3StatsExcessiveCollisions +
07463         stats_blk->stat_Dot3StatsLateCollisions);
07464 
07465     if ((CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706) ||
07466         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_A0))
07467         net_stats->tx_carrier_errors = 0;
07468     else {
07469         net_stats->tx_carrier_errors =
07470             (unsigned long)
07471             stats_blk->stat_Dot3StatsCarrierSenseErrors;
07472     }
07473 
07474     net_stats->tx_errors =
07475             (unsigned long)
07476         stats_blk->stat_emac_tx_stat_dot3statsinternalmactransmiterrors
07477         +
07478         net_stats->tx_aborted_errors +
07479         net_stats->tx_carrier_errors;
07480 
07481     net_stats->rx_missed_errors =
07482         (unsigned long) (stats_blk->stat_IfInFTQDiscards +
07483         stats_blk->stat_IfInMBUFDiscards + stats_blk->stat_FwRxDrop);
07484 
07485     return net_stats;
07486 }
07487 
07488 /* All ethtool functions called with rtnl_lock */
07489 
07490 static int
07491 bnx2_get_settings(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_cmd *cmd)
07492 {
07493     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07494     int support_serdes = 0, support_copper = 0;
07495 
07496     cmd->supported = SUPPORTED_Autoneg;
07497     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP) {
07498         support_serdes = 1;
07499         support_copper = 1;
07500     } else if (bp->phy_port == PORT_FIBRE)
07501         support_serdes = 1;
07502     else
07503         support_copper = 1;
07504 
07505     if (support_serdes) {
07506         cmd->supported |= SUPPORTED_1000baseT_Full |
07507             SUPPORTED_FIBRE;
07508         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE)
07509             cmd->supported |= SUPPORTED_2500baseX_Full;
07510 
07511     }
07512     if (support_copper) {
07513         cmd->supported |= SUPPORTED_10baseT_Half |
07514             SUPPORTED_10baseT_Full |
07515             SUPPORTED_100baseT_Half |
07516             SUPPORTED_100baseT_Full |
07517             SUPPORTED_1000baseT_Full |
07518             SUPPORTED_TP;
07519 
07520     }
07521 
07522     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07523     cmd->port = bp->phy_port;
07524     cmd->advertising = bp->advertising;
07525 
07526     if (bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED) {
07527         cmd->autoneg = AUTONEG_ENABLE;
07528     }
07529     else {
07530         cmd->autoneg = AUTONEG_DISABLE;
07531     }
07532 
07533     if (netif_carrier_ok(dev)) {
07534         cmd->speed = bp->line_speed;
07535         cmd->duplex = bp->duplex;
07536     }
07537     else {
07538         cmd->speed = -1;
07539         cmd->duplex = -1;
07540     }
07541     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07542 
07543     cmd->transceiver = XCVR_INTERNAL;
07544     cmd->phy_address = bp->phy_addr;
07545 
07546     return 0;
07547 }
07548 
07549 static int
07550 bnx2_set_settings(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_cmd *cmd)
07551 {
07552     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07553     u8 autoneg = bp->autoneg;
07554     u8 req_duplex = bp->req_duplex;
07555     u16 req_line_speed = bp->req_line_speed;
07556     u32 advertising = bp->advertising;
07557     int err = -EINVAL;
07558 
07559     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07560 
07561     if (cmd->port != PORT_TP && cmd->port != PORT_FIBRE)
07562         goto err_out_unlock;
07563 
07564     if (cmd->port != bp->phy_port &&
07565         !(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP))
07566         goto err_out_unlock;
07567 
07568     /* If device is down, we can store the settings only if the user
07569      * is setting the currently active port.
07570      */
07571     if (!netif_running(dev) && cmd->port != bp->phy_port)
07572         goto err_out_unlock;
07573 
07574     if (cmd->autoneg == AUTONEG_ENABLE) {
07575         autoneg |= AUTONEG_SPEED;
07576 
07577         cmd->advertising &= ETHTOOL_ALL_COPPER_SPEED;
07578 
07579         /* allow advertising 1 speed */
07580         if ((cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_10baseT_Half) ||
07581             (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_10baseT_Full) ||
07582             (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_100baseT_Half) ||
07583             (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_100baseT_Full)) {
07584 
07585             if (cmd->port == PORT_FIBRE)
07586                 goto err_out_unlock;
07587 
07588             advertising = cmd->advertising;
07589 
07590         } else if (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_2500baseX_Full) {
07591             if (!(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE) ||
07592                 (cmd->port == PORT_TP))
07593                 goto err_out_unlock;
07594         } else if (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Full)
07595             advertising = cmd->advertising;
07596         else if (cmd->advertising == ADVERTISED_1000baseT_Half)
07597             goto err_out_unlock;
07598         else {
07599             if (cmd->port == PORT_FIBRE)
07600                 advertising = ETHTOOL_ALL_FIBRE_SPEED;
07601             else
07602                 advertising = ETHTOOL_ALL_COPPER_SPEED;
07603         }
07604         advertising |= ADVERTISED_Autoneg;
07605     }
07606     else {
07607         if (cmd->port == PORT_FIBRE) {
07608             if ((cmd->speed != SPEED_1000 &&
07609                  cmd->speed != SPEED_2500) ||
07610                 (cmd->duplex != DUPLEX_FULL))
07611                 goto err_out_unlock;
07612 
07613             if (cmd->speed == SPEED_2500 &&
07614                 !(bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE))
07615                 goto err_out_unlock;
07616         }
07617         else if (cmd->speed == SPEED_1000 || cmd->speed == SPEED_2500)
07618             goto err_out_unlock;
07619 
07620         autoneg &= ~AUTONEG_SPEED;
07621         req_line_speed = cmd->speed;
07622         req_duplex = cmd->duplex;
07623         advertising = 0;
07624     }
07625 
07626     bp->autoneg = autoneg;
07627     bp->advertising = advertising;
07628     bp->req_line_speed = req_line_speed;
07629     bp->req_duplex = req_duplex;
07630 
07631     err = 0;
07632     /* If device is down, the new settings will be picked up when it is
07633      * brought up.
07634      */
07635     if (netif_running(dev))
07636         err = bnx2_setup_phy(bp, cmd->port);
07637 
07638 err_out_unlock:
07639     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07640 
07641     return err;
07642 }
07643 
07644 static void
07645 bnx2_get_drvinfo(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_drvinfo *info)
07646 {
07647     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07648 
07649     strcpy(info->driver, DRV_MODULE_NAME);
07650     strcpy(info->version, DRV_MODULE_VERSION);
07651     strcpy(info->bus_info, pci_name(bp->pdev));
07652     strcpy(info->fw_version, bp->fw_version);
07653 
07654 #if defined(VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION) && \
07655     (VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION >= 35000) && (VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION < 40000)
07656     info->eedump_len = bnx2_get_eeprom_len(dev);
07657 #endif
07658 }
07659 
07660 #define BNX2_REGDUMP_LEN        (32 * 1024)
07661 
07662 static int
07663 bnx2_get_regs_len(struct net_device *dev)
07664 {
07665     return BNX2_REGDUMP_LEN;
07666 }
07667 
07668 static void
07669 bnx2_get_regs(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_regs *regs, void *_p)
07670 {
07671     u32 *p = _p, i, offset;
07672     u8 *orig_p = _p;
07673     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07674     u32 reg_boundaries[] = { 0x0000, 0x0098, 0x0400, 0x045c,
07675                  0x0800, 0x0880, 0x0c00, 0x0c10,
07676                  0x0c30, 0x0d08, 0x1000, 0x101c,
07677                  0x1040, 0x1048, 0x1080, 0x10a4,
07678                  0x1400, 0x1490, 0x1498, 0x14f0,
07679                  0x1500, 0x155c, 0x1580, 0x15dc,
07680                  0x1600, 0x1658, 0x1680, 0x16d8,
07681                  0x1800, 0x1820, 0x1840, 0x1854,
07682                  0x1880, 0x1894, 0x1900, 0x1984,
07683                  0x1c00, 0x1c0c, 0x1c40, 0x1c54,
07684                  0x1c80, 0x1c94, 0x1d00, 0x1d84,
07685                  0x2000, 0x2030, 0x23c0, 0x2400,
07686                  0x2800, 0x2820, 0x2830, 0x2850,
07687                  0x2b40, 0x2c10, 0x2fc0, 0x3058,
07688                  0x3c00, 0x3c94, 0x4000, 0x4010,
07689                  0x4080, 0x4090, 0x43c0, 0x4458,
07690                  0x4c00, 0x4c18, 0x4c40, 0x4c54,
07691                  0x4fc0, 0x5010, 0x53c0, 0x5444,
07692                  0x5c00, 0x5c18, 0x5c80, 0x5c90,
07693                  0x5fc0, 0x6000, 0x6400, 0x6428,
07694                  0x6800, 0x6848, 0x684c, 0x6860,
07695                  0x6888, 0x6910, 0x8000 };
07696 
07697     regs->version = 0;
07698 
07699     memset(p, 0, BNX2_REGDUMP_LEN);
07700 
07701     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
07702         return;
07703 
07704     i = 0;
07705     offset = reg_boundaries[0];
07706     p += offset;
07707     while (offset < BNX2_REGDUMP_LEN) {
07708         *p++ = REG_RD(bp, offset);
07709         offset += 4;
07710         if (offset == reg_boundaries[i + 1]) {
07711             offset = reg_boundaries[i + 2];
07712             p = (u32 *) (orig_p + offset);
07713             i += 2;
07714         }
07715     }
07716 }
07717 
07718 static void
07719 bnx2_get_wol(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_wolinfo *wol)
07720 {
07721     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07722 
07723     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL) {
07724         wol->supported = 0;
07725         wol->wolopts = 0;
07726     }
07727     else {
07728         wol->supported = WAKE_MAGIC;
07729         if (bp->wol)
07730             wol->wolopts = WAKE_MAGIC;
07731         else
07732             wol->wolopts = 0;
07733     }
07734     memset(&wol->sopass, 0, sizeof(wol->sopass));
07735 }
07736 
07737 static int
07738 bnx2_set_wol(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_wolinfo *wol)
07739 {
07740     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07741 
07742     if (wol->wolopts & ~WAKE_MAGIC)
07743         return -EINVAL;
07744 
07745     if (wol->wolopts & WAKE_MAGIC) {
07746         if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL)
07747             return -EINVAL;
07748 
07749         bp->wol = 1;
07750     }
07751     else {
07752         bp->wol = 0;
07753     }
07754     return 0;
07755 }
07756 
07757 static int
07758 bnx2_nway_reset(struct net_device *dev)
07759 {
07760     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07761     u32 bmcr;
07762 
07763     if (!netif_running(dev))
07764         return -EAGAIN;
07765 
07766     if (!(bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_SPEED)) {
07767         return -EINVAL;
07768     }
07769 
07770     spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07771 
07772     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP) {
07773         int rc;
07774 
07775         rc = bnx2_setup_remote_phy(bp, bp->phy_port);
07776         spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07777         return rc;
07778     }
07779 
07780     /* Force a link down visible on the other side */
07781     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
07782         bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, BMCR_LOOPBACK);
07783         spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07784 
07785         bnx2_msleep(20);
07786 
07787         spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07788 
07789         bp->current_interval = BNX2_SERDES_AN_TIMEOUT;
07790         bp->serdes_an_pending = 1;
07791         mod_timer(&bp->timer, jiffies + bp->current_interval);
07792     }
07793 
07794     bnx2_read_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, &bmcr);
07795     bmcr &= ~BMCR_LOOPBACK;
07796     bnx2_write_phy(bp, bp->mii_bmcr, bmcr | BMCR_ANRESTART | BMCR_ANENABLE);
07797 
07798     spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
07799 
07800     return 0;
07801 }
07802 
07803 static u32
07804 bnx2_get_link(struct net_device *dev)
07805 {
07806     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07807 
07808     return bp->link_up;
07809 }
07810 
07811 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20418) || \
07812     (defined(VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION) && \
07813     ((VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION >= 35000) && (VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION < 40000)))
07814 static int
07815 bnx2_get_eeprom_len(struct net_device *dev)
07816 {
07817     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07818 
07819     if (bp->flash_info == NULL)
07820         return 0;
07821 
07822     return (int) bp->flash_size;
07823 }
07824 #endif

07864 static int
07865 bnx2_get_coalesce(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_coalesce *coal)
07866 {
07867     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07868 
07869     memset(coal, 0, sizeof(struct ethtool_coalesce));
07870 
07871     coal->rx_coalesce_usecs = bp->rx_ticks;
07872     coal->rx_max_coalesced_frames = bp->rx_quick_cons_trip;
07873     coal->rx_coalesce_usecs_irq = bp->rx_ticks_int;
07874     coal->rx_max_coalesced_frames_irq = bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int;
07875 
07876     coal->tx_coalesce_usecs = bp->tx_ticks;
07877     coal->tx_max_coalesced_frames = bp->tx_quick_cons_trip;
07878     coal->tx_coalesce_usecs_irq = bp->tx_ticks_int;
07879     coal->tx_max_coalesced_frames_irq = bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int;
07880 
07881     coal->stats_block_coalesce_usecs = bp->stats_ticks;
07882 
07883     return 0;
07884 }
07885 
07886 static int
07887 bnx2_set_coalesce(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_coalesce *coal)
07888 {
07889     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07890 
07891     bp->rx_ticks = (u16) coal->rx_coalesce_usecs;
07892     if (bp->rx_ticks > 0x3ff) bp->rx_ticks = 0x3ff;
07893 
07894     bp->rx_quick_cons_trip = (u16) coal->rx_max_coalesced_frames;
07895     if (bp->rx_quick_cons_trip > 0xff) bp->rx_quick_cons_trip = 0xff;
07896 
07897     bp->rx_ticks_int = (u16) coal->rx_coalesce_usecs_irq;
07898     if (bp->rx_ticks_int > 0x3ff) bp->rx_ticks_int = 0x3ff;
07899 
07900     bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int = (u16) coal->rx_max_coalesced_frames_irq;
07901     if (bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int > 0xff)
07902         bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int = 0xff;
07903 
07904     bp->tx_ticks = (u16) coal->tx_coalesce_usecs;
07905     if (bp->tx_ticks > 0x3ff) bp->tx_ticks = 0x3ff;
07906 
07907     bp->tx_quick_cons_trip = (u16) coal->tx_max_coalesced_frames;
07908     if (bp->tx_quick_cons_trip > 0xff) bp->tx_quick_cons_trip = 0xff;
07909 
07910     bp->tx_ticks_int = (u16) coal->tx_coalesce_usecs_irq;
07911     if (bp->tx_ticks_int > 0x3ff) bp->tx_ticks_int = 0x3ff;
07912 
07913     bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int = (u16) coal->tx_max_coalesced_frames_irq;
07914     if (bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int > 0xff) bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int =
07915         0xff;
07916 
07917     bp->stats_ticks = coal->stats_block_coalesce_usecs;
07918     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_BROKEN_STATS) {
07919         if (bp->stats_ticks != 0 && bp->stats_ticks != USEC_PER_SEC)
07920             bp->stats_ticks = USEC_PER_SEC;
07921     }
07922     if (bp->stats_ticks > BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS_HC_STAT_TICKS)
07923         bp->stats_ticks = BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS_HC_STAT_TICKS;
07924     bp->stats_ticks &= BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS_HC_STAT_TICKS;
07925 
07926     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
07927         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
07928         bnx2_init_nic(bp, 0);
07929         bnx2_netif_start(bp);
07930     }
07931 
07932     return 0;
07933 }
07934 
07935 static void
07936 bnx2_get_ringparam(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_ringparam *ering)
07937 {
07938     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
07939 
07940     ering->rx_max_pending = MAX_TOTAL_RX_DESC_CNT;
07941     ering->rx_mini_max_pending = 0;
07942     ering->rx_jumbo_max_pending = MAX_TOTAL_RX_PG_DESC_CNT;
07943 
07944     ering->rx_pending = bp->rx_ring_size;
07945     ering->rx_mini_pending = 0;
07946     ering->rx_jumbo_pending = bp->rx_pg_ring_size;
07947 
07948     ering->tx_max_pending = MAX_TX_DESC_CNT;
07949     ering->tx_pending = bp->tx_ring_size;
07950 }
07951 
07952 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
07953 static int
07954 bnx2_change_ring_size(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 rx, u32 tx)
07955 {
07956     int rc;
07957 
07958     if(bp->reset_failed) {
07959         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Previous error detected preventing MTU "
07960                 "change\n", bp->dev->name);
07961         return -EIO;
07962     }
07963 
07964     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
07965         netif_tx_disable(bp->dev);
07966         bp->dev->trans_start = jiffies; /* prevent tx timeout */
07967 
07968         if (bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp) &&
07969             (bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED)) {
07970             bnx2_netqueue_flush_all(bp);
07971         }
07972         bnx2_stop_netqueue_hw(bp);
07973 
07974         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
07975 
07976 #if (VMWARE_ESX_DDK_VERSION >= 41000)
07977         vmknetddi_queueops_invalidate_state(bp->dev);
07978 #endif
07979 
07980         bnx2_free_irq(bp);
07981 
07982         rc = bnx2_reset_chip(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET);
07983 
07984         bnx2_setup_int_mode(bp, disable_msi);
07985 
07986 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
07987         if ((bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_MSIX_CAP))
07988             bnx2_setup_msix_tbl(bp);
07989 #endif
07990 
07991         bnx2_request_irq(bp);
07992 
07993         /*  Did the chip reset fail ? */
07994         if (rc != 0) {
07995             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: chip reset failed during MTU "
07996                         "change\n",
07997                 bp->dev->name);
07998 
07999             bp->reset_failed = 1;
08000 
08001             goto error;
08002         }
08003         bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
08004         bnx2_free_mem(bp);
08005     }
08006 
08007     bnx2_set_rx_ring_size(bp, rx);
08008     bp->tx_ring_size = tx;
08009 
08010     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
08011         rc = bnx2_alloc_mem(bp);
08012         if (rc) {
08013             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: failed alloc mem during MTU "
08014                         "change\n",
08015                 bp->dev->name);
08016             goto error;
08017         }
08018         rc = bnx2_init_nic(bp, 0);
08019         if (rc) {
08020             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: failed init nic during MTU "
08021                         "change\n",
08022                 bp->dev->name);
08023             goto error;
08024         }
08025 
08026         bnx2_init_netqueue_hw(bp);
08027         bnx2_start_netqueue_hw(bp);
08028 
08029         bnx2_netif_start(bp);
08030     }
08031 
08032     return 0;
08033 
08034 error:
08035     netif_carrier_off(bp->dev);        
08036 
08037     return rc;
08038 }
08039 #else
08040 static int
08041 bnx2_change_ring_size(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 rx, u32 tx)
08042 {
08043     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
08044         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
08045         bnx2_reset_chip(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET);
08046         bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
08047         bnx2_free_mem(bp);
08048     }
08049 
08050     bnx2_set_rx_ring_size(bp, rx);
08051     bp->tx_ring_size = tx;
08052 
08053     if (netif_running(bp->dev)) {
08054         int rc;
08055 
08056         rc = bnx2_alloc_mem(bp);
08057         if (!rc)
08058             rc = bnx2_init_nic(bp, 0);
08059 
08060         if (rc) {
08061             bnx2_napi_enable(bp);
08062             dev_close(bp->dev);
08063             return rc;
08064         }
08065         bnx2_netif_start(bp);
08066     }
08067     return 0;
08068 }
08069 #endif
08070 
08071 static int
08072 bnx2_set_ringparam(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_ringparam *ering)
08073 {
08074     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08075     int rc;
08076 
08077     if ((ering->rx_pending > MAX_TOTAL_RX_DESC_CNT) ||
08078         (ering->tx_pending > MAX_TX_DESC_CNT) ||
08079         (ering->tx_pending <= MAX_SKB_FRAGS)) {
08080 
08081         return -EINVAL;
08082     }
08083     rc = bnx2_change_ring_size(bp, ering->rx_pending, ering->tx_pending);
08084     return rc;
08085 }
08086 
08087 static void
08088 bnx2_get_pauseparam(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_pauseparam *epause)
08089 {
08090     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08091 
08092     epause->autoneg = ((bp->autoneg & AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL) != 0);
08093     epause->rx_pause = ((bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_RX) != 0);
08094     epause->tx_pause = ((bp->flow_ctrl & FLOW_CTRL_TX) != 0);
08095 }
08096 
08097 static int
08098 bnx2_set_pauseparam(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_pauseparam *epause)
08099 {
08100     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08101 
08102     bp->req_flow_ctrl = 0;
08103     if (epause->rx_pause)
08104         bp->req_flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_RX;
08105     if (epause->tx_pause)
08106         bp->req_flow_ctrl |= FLOW_CTRL_TX;
08107 
08108     if (epause->autoneg) {
08109         bp->autoneg |= AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL;
08110     }
08111     else {
08112         bp->autoneg &= ~AUTONEG_FLOW_CTRL;
08113     }
08114 
08115     if (netif_running(dev)) {
08116         spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08117         bnx2_setup_phy(bp, bp->phy_port);
08118         spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08119     }
08120 
08121     return 0;
08122 }

08138     return 0;
08139 }

08312     STATS_OFFSET32(stat_IfInMBUFDiscards),
08313     STATS_OFFSET32(stat_FwRxDrop),
08314 };
08315 
08316 /* stat_IfHCInBadOctets and stat_Dot3StatsCarrierSenseErrors are
08317  * skipped because of errata.
08318  */
08319 static u8 bnx2_5706_stats_len_arr[BNX2_NUM_STATS] = {
08320     8,0,8,8,8,8,8,8,8,8,
08321     4,0,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08322     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08323     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08324     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08325 };
08326 
08327 static u8 bnx2_5708_stats_len_arr[BNX2_NUM_STATS] = {
08328     8,0,8,8,8,8,8,8,8,8,
08329     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08330     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08331     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08332     4,4,4,4,4,4,4,
08333 };

08335 #define BNX2_NUM_TESTS 6
08336 
08337 static struct {
08338     char string[ETH_GSTRING_LEN];
08339 } bnx2_tests_str_arr[BNX2_NUM_TESTS] = {
08340     { "register_test (offline)" },
08341     { "memory_test (offline)" },
08342     { "loopback_test (offline)" },
08343     { "nvram_test (online)" },
08344     { "interrupt_test (online)" },
08345     { "link_test (online)" },
08346 };

08350 bnx2_get_sset_count(struct net_device *dev, int sset)
08351 {
08352     switch (sset) {
08353     case ETH_SS_TEST:
08354         return BNX2_NUM_TESTS;
08355     case ETH_SS_STATS:
08356         return BNX2_NUM_STATS;
08357     default:
08358         return -EOPNOTSUPP;
08359     }
08360 }

08366 }

08368 
08369 static void
08370 bnx2_self_test(struct net_device *dev, struct ethtool_test *etest, u64 *buf)
08371 {
08372     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08373 
08374     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
08375 
08376     memset(buf, 0, sizeof(u64) * BNX2_NUM_TESTS);
08377     if (etest->flags & ETH_TEST_FL_OFFLINE) {
08378         int i;
08379 
08380         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
08381         bnx2_reset_chip(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_DIAG);
08382         bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
08383 
08384         if (bnx2_test_registers(bp) != 0) {
08385             buf[0] = 1;
08386             etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08387         }
08388         if (bnx2_test_memory(bp) != 0) {
08389             buf[1] = 1;
08390             etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08391         }
08392         if ((buf[2] = bnx2_test_loopback(bp)) != 0)
08393             etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08394 
08395         if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
08396             bnx2_shutdown_chip(bp);
08397         else {
08398             bnx2_init_nic(bp, 1);
08399             bnx2_netif_start(bp);
08400         }
08401 
08402         /* wait for link up */
08403         for (i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
08404             if (bp->link_up)
08405                 break;
08406             bnx2_msleep_interruptible(1000);
08407         }
08408     }
08409 
08410     if (bnx2_test_nvram(bp) != 0) {
08411         buf[3] = 1;
08412         etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08413     }
08414     if (bnx2_test_intr(bp) != 0) {
08415         buf[4] = 1;
08416         etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08417     }
08418 
08419     if (bnx2_test_link(bp) != 0) {
08420         buf[5] = 1;
08421         etest->flags |= ETH_TEST_FL_FAILED;
08422 
08423     }
08424     if (!netif_running(bp->dev))
08425         bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D3hot);
08426 }

08428 static void
08429 bnx2_get_strings(struct net_device *dev, u32 stringset, u8 *buf)
08430 {
08431     switch (stringset) {
08432     case ETH_SS_STATS:
08433         memcpy(buf, bnx2_stats_str_arr,
08434             sizeof(bnx2_stats_str_arr));
08435         break;
08436     case ETH_SS_TEST:
08437         memcpy(buf, bnx2_tests_str_arr,
08438             sizeof(bnx2_tests_str_arr));
08439         break;
08440     }
08441 }

08450 
08451 static void
08452 bnx2_get_ethtool_stats(struct net_device *dev,
08453         struct ethtool_stats *stats, u64 *buf)
08454 {
08455     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08456     int i;
08457     u32 *hw_stats = (u32 *) bp->stats_blk;
08458     u8 *stats_len_arr = NULL;
08459 
08460     if (hw_stats == NULL) {
08461         memset(buf, 0, sizeof(u64) * BNX2_NUM_STATS);
08462         return;
08463     }
08464 
08465     if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) ||
08466         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A1) ||
08467         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A2) ||
08468         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_A0))
08469         stats_len_arr = bnx2_5706_stats_len_arr;
08470     else
08471         stats_len_arr = bnx2_5708_stats_len_arr;
08472 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
08473     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_NUM_STATS - BNX2_NUM_NETQ_STATS; i++) {
08474 #else
08475     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_NUM_STATS; i++) {
08476 #endif
08477         if (stats_len_arr[i] == 0) {
08478             /* skip this counter */
08479             buf[i] = 0;
08480             continue;
08481         }
08482         if (stats_len_arr[i] == 4) {
08483             /* 4-byte counter */
08484             buf[i] = (u64)
08485                 *(hw_stats + bnx2_stats_offset_arr[i]);
08486             continue;
08487         }
08488         /* 8-byte counter */
08489         buf[i] = (((u64) *(hw_stats +
08490                     bnx2_stats_offset_arr[i])) << 32) +
08491                 *(hw_stats + bnx2_stats_offset_arr[i] + 1);
08492     }
08493 
08494 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
08495     /*  Copy over the NetQ specific statistics */
08496     {
08497         int j;
08498 
08499         for (j = 0; j < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; j++) {
08500             struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[j];
08501 
08502             buf[i + (j*5) + 0] = (u64) (bnapi->stats.rx_packets);
08503             buf[i + (j*5) + 1] = (u64) (bnapi->stats.rx_bytes);
08504             buf[i + (j*5) + 2] = (u64) (bnapi->stats.rx_errors);
08505             buf[i + (j*5) + 3] = (u64) (bnapi->stats.tx_packets);
08506             buf[i + (j*5) + 4] = (u64) (bnapi->stats.tx_bytes);
08507         }
08508     }
08509 #endif
08510 }
08511 
08512 static int
08513 bnx2_phys_id(struct net_device *dev, u32 data)
08514 {
08515     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08516     int i;
08517     u32 save;
08518 
08519     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
08520 
08521     if (data == 0)
08522         data = 2;
08523 
08524     save = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG);
08525     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG, BNX2_MISC_CFG_LEDMODE_MAC);
08526 
08527     for (i = 0; i < (data * 2); i++) {
08528         if ((i % 2) == 0) {
08529             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_LED, BNX2_EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE);
08530         }
08531         else {
08532             REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_LED, BNX2_EMAC_LED_OVERRIDE |
08533                 BNX2_EMAC_LED_1000MB_OVERRIDE |
08534                 BNX2_EMAC_LED_100MB_OVERRIDE |
08535                 BNX2_EMAC_LED_10MB_OVERRIDE |
08536                 BNX2_EMAC_LED_TRAFFIC_OVERRIDE |
08537                 BNX2_EMAC_LED_TRAFFIC);
08538         }
08539         bnx2_msleep_interruptible(500);
08540         if (signal_pending(current))
08541             break;
08542     }
08543     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_EMAC_LED, 0);
08544     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MISC_CFG, save);
08545 
08546     if (!netif_running(dev))
08547         bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D3hot);
08548 
08549     return 0;
08550 }

08628 #if defined(BNX2_VMWARE_BMAPILNX)
08629 static int
08630 bnx2_ioctl_cim(struct net_device *dev, struct ifreq *ifr)
08631 {
08632     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08633     void __user *useraddr = ifr->ifr_data;
08634     struct bnx2_ioctl_req req;
08635     int rc = 0;
08636     u32 val;
08637 
08638     if (copy_from_user(&req, useraddr, sizeof(req))) {
08639         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() could not copy from user"
08640                     "bnx2_ioctl_req\n", bp->dev->name);
08641         return -EFAULT;
08642     }
08643 
08644     switch(req.cmd) {
08645     case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_ENABLE_NIC:
08646         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() enable NIC\n",
08647                      bp->dev->name);
08648 
08649         rc = bnx2_open(bp->dev);
08650         break;
08651     case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_DISABLE_NIC:
08652         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() disable NIC\n",
08653                      bp->dev->name);
08654 
08655         rc = bnx2_close(bp->dev);
08656         break;
08657     case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_REG_READ: {
08658         u32 mem_len;
08659 
08660 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
08661         mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID + 2);
08662 #else
08663         mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(TX_TSS_CID + TX_MAX_TSS_RINGS + 1);
08664 #endif
08665         if(mem_len < req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_offset) {
08666             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() reg read: "
08667                         "out of range: max reg: 0x%x "
08668                         "req reg: 0x%x\n",
08669                 bp->dev->name,
08670                 mem_len, req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_offset);
08671             rc = -EINVAL;
08672             break;
08673         }
08674 
08675         val = REG_RD(bp, req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_offset);
08676 
08677         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() reg read: "
08678                      "reg: 0x%x value:0x%x",
08679                      bp->dev->name, 
08680                      req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_offset,
08681                      req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_value);
08682         req.cmd_req.reg_read.reg_value = val;
08683 
08684         break;
08685     } case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_REG_WRITE: {
08686         u32 mem_len;
08687 
08688 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
08689         mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID + 2);
08690 #else
08691         mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(TX_TSS_CID + TX_MAX_TSS_RINGS + 1);
08692 #endif
08693         if(mem_len < req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_offset) {
08694             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() reg write: "
08695                         "out of range: max reg: 0x%x "
08696                         "req reg: 0x%x\n",
08697                 bp->dev->name,
08698                 mem_len, req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_offset);
08699             rc = -EINVAL;
08700             break;
08701         }
08702 
08703         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() reg write: "
08704                      "reg: 0x%x value:0x%x",
08705                      bp->dev->name, 
08706                      req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_offset,
08707                      req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_value);
08708 
08709         REG_WR(bp, req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_offset,
08710                req.cmd_req.reg_write.reg_value);
08711 
08712         break;
08713     } case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_GET_NIC_PARAM:
08714         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() get NIC param\n",
08715                      bp->dev->name);
08716 
08717         req.cmd_req.get_nic_param.mtu = dev->mtu;
08718         memcpy(req.cmd_req.get_nic_param.current_mac_addr,
08719                dev->dev_addr,
08720                sizeof(req.cmd_req.get_nic_param.current_mac_addr));
08721         break;
08722     case BNX2_VMWARE_CIM_CMD_GET_NIC_STATUS:
08723         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() get NIC status\n",
08724                      bp->dev->name);
08725 
08726         req.cmd_req.get_nic_status.nic_status = netif_running(dev);
08727         break;
08728     default:
08729         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() unknown req.cmd: 0x%x\n",
08730                     bp->dev->name, req.cmd);
08731         rc = -EINVAL;
08732     }
08733 
08734         if (rc == 0 &&
08735         copy_to_user(useraddr, &req, sizeof(req))) {
08736         printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: bnx2_ioctl() couldn't copy to user "
08737                     "bnx2_ioctl_req\n", bp->dev->name);
08738                 return -EFAULT;
08739     }
08740 
08741     return rc;
08742 }
08743 #endif  /* BNX2_VMWARE_BMAPILNX */
08744 
08745 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
08746 static int
08747 bnx2_ioctl(struct net_device *dev, struct ifreq *ifr, int cmd)
08748 {
08749 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x020607)
08750     struct mii_ioctl_data *data = if_mii(ifr);
08751 #else
08752     struct mii_ioctl_data *data = (struct mii_ioctl_data *) &ifr->ifr_ifru;
08753 #endif
08754     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08755     int err;
08756 
08757     switch(cmd) {
08758     case SIOCGMIIPHY:
08759         data->phy_id = bp->phy_addr;
08760 
08761         /* fallthru */
08762     case SIOCGMIIREG: {
08763         u32 mii_regval;
08764 
08765         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
08766             return -EOPNOTSUPP;
08767 
08768         if (!netif_running(dev))
08769             return -EAGAIN;
08770 
08771         spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08772         err = bnx2_read_phy(bp, data->reg_num & 0x1f, &mii_regval);
08773         spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08774 
08775         data->val_out = mii_regval;
08776 
08777         return err;
08778     }
08779 
08780     case SIOCSMIIREG:
08781         if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_REMOTE_PHY_CAP)
08782             return -EOPNOTSUPP;
08783 
08784         if (!netif_running(dev))
08785             return -EAGAIN;
08786 
08787         spin_lock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08788         err = bnx2_write_phy(bp, data->reg_num & 0x1f, data->val_in);
08789         spin_unlock_bh(&bp->phy_lock);
08790 
08791         return err;
08792 
08793 #if defined(BNX2_VMWARE_BMAPILNX)
08794 #define SIOBNX2CIM  0x89F0
08795     case SIOBNX2CIM:
08796         return bnx2_ioctl_cim(dev, ifr);
08797 #endif  /* BNX2_VMWARE_BMAPILNX */
08798     default:
08799         /* do nothing */
08800         break;
08801     }
08802     return -EOPNOTSUPP;
08803 }
08804 
08805 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
08806 static int
08807 bnx2_change_mac_addr(struct net_device *dev, void *p)
08808 {
08809     struct sockaddr *addr = p;
08810     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08811 
08812     if (!is_valid_ether_addr(addr->sa_data))
08813         return -EINVAL;
08814 
08815     memcpy(dev->dev_addr, addr->sa_data, dev->addr_len);
08816     if (netif_running(dev))
08817         bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, bp->dev->dev_addr, 0);
08818 
08819     return 0;
08820 }
08821 
08822 /* Called with rtnl_lock */
08823 static int
08824 bnx2_change_mtu(struct net_device *dev, int new_mtu)
08825 {
08826     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08827 
08828     if (((new_mtu + ETH_HLEN) > MAX_ETHERNET_JUMBO_PACKET_SIZE) ||
08829         ((new_mtu + ETH_HLEN) < MIN_ETHERNET_PACKET_SIZE))
08830         return -EINVAL;
08831 
08832     dev->mtu = new_mtu;
08833     return (bnx2_change_ring_size(bp, bp->rx_ring_size, bp->tx_ring_size));
08834 }
08835 
08836 #if defined(HAVE_POLL_CONTROLLER) || defined(CONFIG_NET_POLL_CONTROLLER)
08837 static void
08838 poll_bnx2(struct net_device *dev)
08839 {
08840     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
08841 
08842 #if defined(RED_HAT_LINUX_KERNEL) && (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x020600)
08843     if (netdump_mode) {
08844         bnx2_interrupt(bp->pdev->irq, &bp->bnx2_napi[0], NULL);
08845         if (dev->poll_list.prev) {
08846             int budget = 64;
08847 
08848             bnx2_poll(dev, &budget);
08849         }
08850     }
08851     else
08852 #endif
08853     {
08854         int i;
08855 
08856         for (i = 0; i < bp->irq_nvecs; i++) {
08857             unsigned int irq = bp->irq_tbl[i].vector;
08858 
08859             disable_irq(irq);
08860 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20613)
08861             bnx2_interrupt(irq, &bp->bnx2_napi[i]);
08862 #else
08863             bnx2_interrupt(irq, &bp->bnx2_napi[i], NULL);
08864 #endif
08865             enable_irq(irq);
08866         }
08867     }
08868 }
08869 #endif
08870 
08871 static void __devinit
08872 bnx2_get_5709_media(struct bnx2 *bp)
08873 {
08874     u32 val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL);
08875     u32 bond_id = val & BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_BOND_ID;
08876     u32 strap;
08877 
08878     if (bond_id == BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_BOND_ID_C)
08879         return;
08880     else if (bond_id == BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_BOND_ID_S) {
08881         bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES;
08882         return;
08883     }
08884 
08885     if (val & BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_STRAP_OVERRIDE)
08886         strap = (val & BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_PHY_CTRL) >> 21;
08887     else
08888         strap = (val & BNX2_MISC_DUAL_MEDIA_CTRL_PHY_CTRL_STRAP) >> 8;
08889 
08890     if (PCI_FUNC(bp->pdev->devfn) == 0) {
08891         switch (strap) {
08892         case 0x4:
08893         case 0x5:
08894         case 0x6:
08895             bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES;
08896             return;
08897         }
08898     } else {
08899         switch (strap) {
08900         case 0x1:
08901         case 0x2:
08902         case 0x4:
08903             bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES;
08904             return;
08905         }
08906     }
08907 }
08908 
08909 static void __devinit
08910 bnx2_get_pci_speed(struct bnx2 *bp)
08911 {
08912     u32 reg;
08913 
08914     reg = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS);
08915     if (reg & BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS_PCIX_DET) {
08916         u32 clkreg;
08917 
08918         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_PCIX;
08919 
08920         clkreg = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS);
08921 
08922         clkreg &= BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET;
08923         switch (clkreg) {
08924         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_133MHZ:
08925             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 133;
08926             break;
08927 
08928         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_95MHZ:
08929             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 100;
08930             break;
08931 
08932         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_66MHZ:
08933         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_80MHZ:
08934             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 66;
08935             break;
08936 
08937         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_48MHZ:
08938         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_55MHZ:
08939             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 50;
08940             break;
08941 
08942         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_LOW:
08943         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_32MHZ:
08944         case BNX2_PCICFG_PCI_CLOCK_CONTROL_BITS_PCI_CLK_SPD_DET_38MHZ:
08945             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 33;
08946             break;
08947         }
08948     }
08949     else {
08950         if (reg & BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS_M66EN)
08951             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 66;
08952         else
08953             bp->bus_speed_mhz = 33;
08954     }
08955 
08956     if (reg & BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_STATUS_32BIT_DET)
08957         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_PCI_32BIT;
08958 
08959 }
08960 
08961 static void __devinit
08962 bnx2_read_vpd_fw_ver(struct bnx2 *bp)
08963 {
08964     int rc, i, v0_len = 0;
08965     u8 *data;
08966     u8 *v0_str = NULL;
08967     bool mn_match = false;
08968 
08969 #define BNX2_VPD_NVRAM_OFFSET   0x300
08970 #define BNX2_VPD_LEN        128
08971 #define BNX2_MAX_VER_SLEN   30
08972 
08973     data = kmalloc(256, GFP_KERNEL);
08974     if (!data)
08975         return;
08976 
08977     rc = bnx2_nvram_read(bp, BNX2_VPD_NVRAM_OFFSET, data + BNX2_VPD_LEN,
08978                  BNX2_VPD_LEN);
08979     if (rc)
08980         goto vpd_done;
08981 
08982     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_VPD_LEN; i += 4) {
08983         data[i] = data[i + BNX2_VPD_LEN + 3];
08984         data[i + 1] = data[i + BNX2_VPD_LEN + 2];
08985         data[i + 2] = data[i + BNX2_VPD_LEN + 1];
08986         data[i + 3] = data[i + BNX2_VPD_LEN];
08987     }
08988 
08989     for (i = 0; i <= BNX2_VPD_LEN - 3; ) {
08990         unsigned char val = data[i];
08991         unsigned int block_end;
08992 
08993         if (val == 0x82 || val == 0x91) {
08994             i = (i + 3 + (data[i + 1] + (data[i + 2] << 8)));
08995             continue;
08996         }
08997 
08998         if (val != 0x90)
08999             goto vpd_done;
09000 
09001         block_end = (i + 3 + (data[i + 1] + (data[i + 2] << 8)));
09002         i += 3;
09003 
09004         if (block_end > BNX2_VPD_LEN)
09005             goto vpd_done;
09006 
09007         while (i < (block_end - 2)) {
09008             int len = data[i + 2];
09009 
09010             if (i + 3 + len > block_end)
09011                 goto vpd_done;
09012 
09013             if (data[i] == 'M' && data[i + 1] == 'N') {
09014                 if (len != 4 ||
09015                     memcmp(&data[i + 3], "1028", 4))
09016                     goto vpd_done;
09017                 mn_match = true;
09018 
09019             } else if (data[i] == 'V' && data[i + 1] == '0') {
09020                 if (len > BNX2_MAX_VER_SLEN)
09021                     goto vpd_done;
09022 
09023                 v0_len = len;
09024                 v0_str = &data[i + 3];
09025             }
09026             i += 3 + len;
09027 
09028             if (mn_match && v0_str) {
09029                 memcpy(bp->fw_version, v0_str, v0_len);
09030                 bp->fw_version[v0_len] = ' ';
09031                 goto vpd_done;
09032             }
09033         }
09034         goto vpd_done;
09035     }
09036 
09037 vpd_done:
09038     kfree(data);
09039 }
09040 
09041 static int __devinit
09042 bnx2_init_board(struct pci_dev *pdev, struct net_device *dev)
09043 {
09044     struct bnx2 *bp;
09045     unsigned long mem_len;
09046     int rc, i, j;
09047     u32 reg;
09048     u64 dma_mask, persist_dma_mask;
09049 
09050 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x20610)
09051     SET_MODULE_OWNER(dev);
09052 #endif
09053 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20419)
09054     SET_NETDEV_DEV(dev, &pdev->dev);
09055 #endif
09056     bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09057 
09058     bp->flags = 0;
09059     bp->phy_flags = 0;
09060 
09061     /* enable device (incl. PCI PM wakeup), and bus-mastering */
09062     rc = pci_enable_device(pdev);
09063     if (rc) {
09064         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "Cannot enable PCI device, aborting.\n");
09065         goto err_out;
09066     }
09067 
09068     if (!(pci_resource_flags(pdev, 0) & IORESOURCE_MEM)) {
09069         dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09070             "Cannot find PCI device base address, aborting.\n");
09071         rc = -ENODEV;
09072         goto err_out_disable;
09073     }
09074 
09075     rc = pci_request_regions(pdev, DRV_MODULE_NAME);
09076     if (rc) {
09077         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "Cannot obtain PCI resources, aborting.\n");
09078         goto err_out_disable;
09079     }
09080 
09081     pci_set_master(pdev);
09082 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x020611)
09083     pci_save_state(pdev);
09084 #endif
09085 
09086     bp->pm_cap = pci_find_capability(pdev, PCI_CAP_ID_PM);
09087     if (bp->pm_cap == 0) {
09088         dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09089             "Cannot find power management capability, aborting.\n");
09090         rc = -EIO;
09091         goto err_out_release;
09092     }
09093 
09094     bp->dev = dev;
09095     bp->pdev = pdev;
09096 
09097     spin_lock_init(&bp->phy_lock);
09098     spin_lock_init(&bp->indirect_lock);
09099 #ifdef BCM_CNIC
09100     mutex_init(&bp->cnic_lock);
09101 #endif
09102 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20600)
09103 #if defined(INIT_DELAYED_WORK_DEFERRABLE) || defined(INIT_WORK_NAR)
09104     INIT_WORK(&bp->reset_task, bnx2_reset_task);
09105 #else
09106     INIT_WORK(&bp->reset_task, bnx2_reset_task, bp);
09107 #endif
09108 #else
09109     INIT_TQUEUE(&bp->reset_task, bnx2_reset_task, bp);
09110 #endif
09111 
09112     dev->base_addr = dev->mem_start = pci_resource_start(pdev, 0);
09113 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09114     mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID + 2);
09115 #else
09116     mem_len = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(TX_TSS_CID + TX_MAX_TSS_RINGS + 1);
09117 #endif
09118     dev->mem_end = dev->mem_start + mem_len;
09119     dev->irq = pdev->irq;
09120 
09121     bp->regview = ioremap_nocache(dev->base_addr, mem_len);
09122 
09123     if (!bp->regview) {
09124         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "Cannot map register space, aborting.\n");
09125         rc = -ENOMEM;
09126         goto err_out_release;
09127     }
09128 
09129     /* Configure byte swap and enable write to the reg_window registers.
09130      * Rely on CPU to do target byte swapping on big endian systems
09131      * The chip's target access swapping will not swap all accesses
09132      */
09133     pci_write_config_dword(bp->pdev, BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG,
09134                    BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_REG_WINDOW_ENA |
09135                    BNX2_PCICFG_MISC_CONFIG_TARGET_MB_WORD_SWAP);
09136 
09137     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
09138 
09139     bp->chip_id = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MISC_ID);
09140 
09141     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09142         if (pci_find_capability(pdev, PCI_CAP_ID_EXP) == 0) {
09143             dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09144                 "Cannot find PCIE capability, aborting.\n");
09145             rc = -EIO;
09146             goto err_out_unmap;
09147         }
09148         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_PCIE;
09149         if (CHIP_REV(bp) == CHIP_REV_Ax)
09150             bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_JUMBO_BROKEN;
09151     } else {
09152         bp->pcix_cap = pci_find_capability(pdev, PCI_CAP_ID_PCIX);
09153         if (bp->pcix_cap == 0) {
09154             dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09155                 "Cannot find PCIX capability, aborting.\n");
09156             rc = -EIO;
09157             goto err_out_unmap;
09158         }
09159         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_BROKEN_STATS;
09160     }
09161 
09162 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
09163     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709 && CHIP_REV(bp) != CHIP_REV_Ax) {
09164         if (pci_find_capability(pdev, PCI_CAP_ID_MSIX))
09165             bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_MSIX_CAP;
09166     }
09167 #endif
09168 
09169     if (CHIP_ID(bp) != CHIP_ID_5706_A0 && CHIP_ID(bp) != CHIP_ID_5706_A1) {
09170         if (pci_find_capability(pdev, PCI_CAP_ID_MSI))
09171             bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_MSI_CAP;
09172     }
09173 
09174     /* 5708 cannot support DMA addresses > 40-bit.  */
09175     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708)
09176         persist_dma_mask = dma_mask = DMA_BIT_MASK(40);
09177     else
09178         persist_dma_mask = dma_mask = DMA_BIT_MASK(64);
09179 
09180     /* Configure DMA attributes. */
09181     if (pci_set_dma_mask(pdev, dma_mask) == 0) {
09182         dev->features |= NETIF_F_HIGHDMA;
09183         rc = pci_set_consistent_dma_mask(pdev, persist_dma_mask);
09184         if (rc) {
09185             dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09186                 "pci_set_consistent_dma_mask failed, aborting.\n");
09187             goto err_out_unmap;
09188         }
09189     } else if ((rc = pci_set_dma_mask(pdev, DMA_BIT_MASK(32))) != 0) {
09190         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "System does not support DMA, aborting.\n");
09191         goto err_out_unmap;
09192     }
09193 
09194     if (!(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIE))
09195         bnx2_get_pci_speed(bp);
09196 
09197     /* 5706A0 may falsely detect SERR and PERR. */
09198     if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) {
09199         reg = REG_RD(bp, PCI_COMMAND);
09200         reg &= ~(PCI_COMMAND_SERR | PCI_COMMAND_PARITY);
09201         REG_WR(bp, PCI_COMMAND, reg);
09202     }
09203     else if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A1) &&
09204         !(bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIX)) {
09205 
09206         dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09207             "5706 A1 can only be used in a PCIX bus, aborting.\n");
09208         goto err_out_unmap;
09209     }
09210 
09211     bnx2_init_nvram(bp);
09212 
09213     reg = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_SHM_HDR_SIGNATURE);
09214 
09215     if ((reg & BNX2_SHM_HDR_SIGNATURE_SIG_MASK) ==
09216         BNX2_SHM_HDR_SIGNATURE_SIG) {
09217         u32 off = PCI_FUNC(pdev->devfn) << 2;
09218 
09219         bp->shmem_base = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_SHM_HDR_ADDR_0 + off);
09220     } else
09221         bp->shmem_base = HOST_VIEW_SHMEM_BASE;
09222 
09223     /* Get the permanent MAC address.  First we need to make sure the
09224      * firmware is actually running.
09225      */
09226     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_DEV_INFO_SIGNATURE);
09227 
09228     if ((reg & BNX2_DEV_INFO_SIGNATURE_MAGIC_MASK) !=
09229         BNX2_DEV_INFO_SIGNATURE_MAGIC) {
09230         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "Firmware not running, aborting.\n");
09231         rc = -ENODEV;
09232         goto err_out_unmap;
09233     }
09234 
09235     bnx2_read_vpd_fw_ver(bp);
09236 
09237     j = strlen(bp->fw_version);
09238     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_DEV_INFO_BC_REV);
09239     for (i = 0; i < 3 && j < 24; i++) {
09240         u8 num, k, skip0;
09241 
09242         if (i == 0) {
09243             bp->fw_version[j++] = 'b';
09244             bp->fw_version[j++] = 'c';
09245             bp->fw_version[j++] = ' ';
09246         }
09247         num = (u8) (reg >> (24 - (i * 8)));
09248         for (k = 100, skip0 = 1; k >= 1; num %= k, k /= 10) {
09249             if (num >= k || !skip0 || k == 1) {
09250                 bp->fw_version[j++] = (num / k) + '0';
09251                 skip0 = 0;
09252             }
09253         }
09254         if (i != 2)
09255             bp->fw_version[j++] = '.';
09256     }
09257     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_PORT_FEATURE);
09258     if (reg & BNX2_PORT_FEATURE_WOL_ENABLED)
09259         bp->wol = 1;
09260 
09261     if (reg & BNX2_PORT_FEATURE_ASF_ENABLED) {
09262         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_ASF_ENABLE;
09263 
09264         for (i = 0; i < 30; i++) {
09265             reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_BC_STATE_CONDITION);
09266             if (reg & BNX2_CONDITION_MFW_RUN_MASK)
09267                 break;
09268             bnx2_msleep(10);
09269         }
09270     }
09271     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_BC_STATE_CONDITION);
09272     reg &= BNX2_CONDITION_MFW_RUN_MASK;
09273     if (reg != BNX2_CONDITION_MFW_RUN_UNKNOWN &&
09274         reg != BNX2_CONDITION_MFW_RUN_NONE) {
09275         u32 addr = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_MFW_VER_PTR);
09276 
09277         if (j < 32)
09278             bp->fw_version[j++] = ' ';
09279         for (i = 0; i < 3 && j < 28; i++) {
09280             reg = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, addr + i * 4);
09281             reg = swab32(reg);
09282             memcpy(&bp->fw_version[j], &reg, 4);
09283             j += 4;
09284         }
09285     }
09286 
09287     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_MAC_UPPER);
09288     bp->mac_addr[0] = (u8) (reg >> 8);
09289     bp->mac_addr[1] = (u8) reg;
09290 
09291     reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_PORT_HW_CFG_MAC_LOWER);
09292     bp->mac_addr[2] = (u8) (reg >> 24);
09293     bp->mac_addr[3] = (u8) (reg >> 16);
09294     bp->mac_addr[4] = (u8) (reg >> 8);
09295     bp->mac_addr[5] = (u8) reg;
09296 
09297     bp->tx_ring_size = MAX_TX_DESC_CNT;
09298     bnx2_set_rx_ring_size(bp, 255);
09299 
09300     bp->rx_csum = 1;
09301 
09302     bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int = 2;
09303     bp->tx_quick_cons_trip = 20;
09304     bp->tx_ticks_int = 18;
09305     bp->tx_ticks = 80;
09306 
09307     bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int = 2;
09308     bp->rx_quick_cons_trip = 12;
09309     bp->rx_ticks_int = 18;
09310     bp->rx_ticks = 18;
09311 
09312     bp->stats_ticks = USEC_PER_SEC & BNX2_HC_STATS_TICKS_HC_STAT_TICKS;
09313 
09314     bp->current_interval = BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL;
09315 
09316     bp->phy_addr = 1;
09317 
09318     /* Disable WOL support if we are running on a SERDES chip. */
09319     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
09320         bnx2_get_5709_media(bp);
09321     else if (CHIP_BOND_ID(bp) & CHIP_BOND_ID_SERDES_BIT)
09322         bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES;
09323 
09324     bp->phy_port = PORT_TP;
09325     if (bp->phy_flags & BNX2_PHY_FLAG_SERDES) {
09326         bp->phy_port = PORT_FIBRE;
09327         reg = bnx2_shmem_rd(bp, BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_CONFIG);
09328         if (!(reg & BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_GIG_LINK_ON_VAUX)) {
09329             bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL;
09330             bp->wol = 0;
09331         }
09332         if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706) {
09333             /* Don't do parallel detect on this board because of
09334              * some board problems.  The link will not go down
09335              * if we do parallel detect.
09336              */
09337             if (pdev->subsystem_vendor == PCI_VENDOR_ID_HP &&
09338                 pdev->subsystem_device == 0x310c)
09339                 bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_NO_PARALLEL;
09340         } else {
09341             bp->phy_addr = 2;
09342             if (reg & BNX2_SHARED_HW_CFG_PHY_2_5G)
09343                 bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_2_5G_CAPABLE;
09344         }
09345     } else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706 ||
09346            CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5708)
09347         bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_CRC_FIX;
09348     else if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709 &&
09349          (CHIP_REV(bp) == CHIP_REV_Ax ||
09350           CHIP_REV(bp) == CHIP_REV_Bx))
09351         bp->phy_flags |= BNX2_PHY_FLAG_DIS_EARLY_DAC;
09352 
09353     bnx2_init_fw_cap(bp);
09354 
09355     if ((CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_A0) ||
09356         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_B0) ||
09357         (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5708_B1) ||
09358         !(REG_RD(bp, BNX2_PCI_CONFIG_3) & BNX2_PCI_CONFIG_3_VAUX_PRESET)) {
09359         bp->flags |= BNX2_FLAG_NO_WOL;
09360         bp->wol = 0;
09361     }
09362 
09363     if (CHIP_ID(bp) == CHIP_ID_5706_A0) {
09364         bp->tx_quick_cons_trip_int =
09365             bp->tx_quick_cons_trip;
09366         bp->tx_ticks_int = bp->tx_ticks;
09367         bp->rx_quick_cons_trip_int =
09368             bp->rx_quick_cons_trip;
09369         bp->rx_ticks_int = bp->rx_ticks;
09370         bp->comp_prod_trip_int = bp->comp_prod_trip;
09371         bp->com_ticks_int = bp->com_ticks;
09372         bp->cmd_ticks_int = bp->cmd_ticks;
09373     }
09374 
09375 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
09376     /* Disable MSI on 5706 if AMD 8132 bridge is found.
09377      *
09378      * MSI is defined to be 32-bit write.  The 5706 does 64-bit MSI writes
09379      * with byte enables disabled on the unused 32-bit word.  This is legal
09380      * but causes problems on the AMD 8132 which will eventually stop
09381      * responding after a while.
09382      *
09383      * AMD believes this incompatibility is unique to the 5706, and
09384      * prefers to locally disable MSI rather than globally disabling it.
09385      */
09386     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5706 && disable_msi == 0) {
09387         struct pci_dev *amd_8132 = NULL;
09388 
09389         while ((amd_8132 = pci_get_device(PCI_VENDOR_ID_AMD,
09390                           PCI_DEVICE_ID_AMD_8132_BRIDGE,
09391                           amd_8132))) {
09392             u8 rev;
09393 
09394             pci_read_config_byte(amd_8132, PCI_REVISION_ID, &rev);
09395             if (rev >= 0x10 && rev <= 0x13) {
09396                 disable_msi = 1;
09397                 pci_dev_put(amd_8132);
09398                 break;
09399             }
09400         }
09401     }
09402 #endif
09403     bnx2_set_default_link(bp);
09404     bp->req_flow_ctrl = FLOW_CTRL_RX | FLOW_CTRL_TX;
09405 
09406     init_timer(&bp->timer);
09407     bp->timer.expires = RUN_AT(BNX2_TIMER_INTERVAL);
09408     bp->timer.data = (unsigned long) bp;
09409     bp->timer.function = bnx2_timer;
09410 
09411     return 0;
09412 
09413 err_out_unmap:
09414     if (bp->regview) {
09415         iounmap(bp->regview);
09416         bp->regview = NULL;
09417     }
09418 
09419 err_out_release:
09420     pci_release_regions(pdev);
09421 
09422 err_out_disable:
09423     pci_disable_device(pdev);
09424     pci_set_drvdata(pdev, NULL);
09425 
09426 err_out:
09427     return rc;
09428 }
09429 
09430 static char * __devinit
09431 bnx2_bus_string(struct bnx2 *bp, char *str)
09432 {
09433     char *s = str;
09434 
09435     if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIE) {
09436         s += sprintf(s, "PCI Express");
09437     } else {
09438         s += sprintf(s, "PCI");
09439         if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCIX)
09440             s += sprintf(s, "-X");
09441         if (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_PCI_32BIT)
09442             s += sprintf(s, " 32-bit");
09443         else
09444             s += sprintf(s, " 64-bit");
09445         s += sprintf(s, " %dMHz", bp->bus_speed_mhz);
09446     }
09447     return str;
09448 }
09449 
09450 static void __devinit
09451 bnx2_init_napi(struct bnx2 *bp)
09452 {
09453     int i;
09454 
09455     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_MSIX_VEC; i++) {
09456         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
09457 #ifdef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
09458         int (*poll)(struct napi_struct *, int);
09459 
09460         if (i == 0)
09461             poll = bnx2_poll;
09462         else
09463             poll = bnx2_poll_msix;
09464 
09465         netif_napi_add(bp->dev, &bp->bnx2_napi[i].napi, poll, 64);
09466 #endif
09467 
09468         bnapi->bp = bp;
09469     }
09470 #ifndef BNX2_NEW_NAPI
09471     bp->dev->poll = bnx2_poll;
09472     bp->dev->weight = 64;
09473 #endif
09474 }

09476 #ifdef HAVE_NET_DEVICE_OPS

09478     .ndo_open       = bnx2_open,
09479     .ndo_start_xmit     = bnx2_start_xmit,
09480     .ndo_stop       = bnx2_close,
09481     .ndo_get_stats      = bnx2_get_stats,
09482     .ndo_set_rx_mode    = bnx2_set_rx_mode,
09483     .ndo_do_ioctl       = bnx2_ioctl,
09484     .ndo_validate_addr  = eth_validate_addr,
09485     .ndo_set_mac_address    = bnx2_change_mac_addr,
09486     .ndo_change_mtu     = bnx2_change_mtu,
09487     .ndo_tx_timeout     = bnx2_tx_timeout,
09488 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
09489     .ndo_vlan_rx_register   = bnx2_vlan_rx_register,
09490 #endif
09491 #if defined(HAVE_POLL_CONTROLLER) || defined(CONFIG_NET_POLL_CONTROLLER)
09492     .ndo_poll_controller    = poll_bnx2,
09493 #endif
09494 };
09495 #endif
