09497 static void inline vlan_features_add(struct net_device *dev, unsigned long flags)
09498 {
09499 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x2061a)
09500 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
09501     dev->vlan_features |= flags;
09502 #endif
09503 #endif
09504 }
09505 
09506 static int __devinit
09507 bnx2_init_one(struct pci_dev *pdev, const struct pci_device_id *ent)
09508 {
09509     static int version_printed = 0;
09510     struct net_device *dev = NULL;
09511     struct bnx2 *bp;
09512     int rc;
09513     char str[40];
09514     DECLARE_MAC_BUF(mac);
09515 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09516     static int index = 0;
09517 #endif
09518 
09519     if (version_printed++ == 0)
09520         printk(KERN_INFO "%s", version);
09521 
09522     /* dev zeroed in init_etherdev */
09523 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20418)
09524 #ifndef BCM_HAVE_MULTI_QUEUE
09525     dev = alloc_etherdev(sizeof(*bp));
09526 #else
09527     dev = alloc_etherdev_mq(sizeof(*bp), TX_MAX_RINGS);
09528 #endif
09529 #else
09530     dev = init_etherdev(NULL, sizeof(*bp));
09531 #endif
09532 
09533     if (!dev)
09534         return -ENOMEM;
09535 
09536     rc = bnx2_init_board(pdev, dev);
09537     if (rc < 0) {
09538 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20418)
09539         free_netdev(dev);
09540 #else
09541         unregister_netdev(dev);
09542         kfree(dev);
09543 #endif
09544         return rc;
09545     }
09546 
09547 #ifndef HAVE_NET_DEVICE_OPS
09548     dev->open = bnx2_open;
09549     dev->hard_start_xmit = bnx2_start_xmit;
09550     dev->stop = bnx2_close;
09551     dev->get_stats = bnx2_get_stats;
09552 #ifdef HAVE_SET_RX_MODE
09553     dev->set_rx_mode = bnx2_set_rx_mode;
09554 #else
09555     dev->set_multicast_list = bnx2_set_rx_mode;
09556 #endif
09557     dev->do_ioctl = bnx2_ioctl;
09558     dev->set_mac_address = bnx2_change_mac_addr;
09559     dev->change_mtu = bnx2_change_mtu;
09560     dev->tx_timeout = bnx2_tx_timeout;
09561 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
09562     dev->vlan_rx_register = bnx2_vlan_rx_register;
09563 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x20616)
09564     dev->vlan_rx_kill_vid = bnx2_vlan_rx_kill_vid;
09565 #endif
09566 #endif
09567 #if defined(HAVE_POLL_CONTROLLER) || defined(CONFIG_NET_POLL_CONTROLLER)
09568     dev->poll_controller = poll_bnx2;
09569 #endif
09570 #else
09571     dev->netdev_ops = &bnx2_netdev_ops;
09572 #endif
09573     dev->watchdog_timeo = TX_TIMEOUT;
09574     dev->ethtool_ops = &bnx2_ethtool_ops;
09575 
09576     bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09577     bnx2_init_napi(bp);
09578 
09579     pci_set_drvdata(pdev, dev);
09580 
09581     memcpy(dev->dev_addr, bp->mac_addr, 6);
09582 #ifdef ETHTOOL_GPERMADDR
09583     memcpy(dev->perm_addr, bp->mac_addr, 6);
09584 #endif
09585 
09586 #ifdef NETIF_F_IPV6_CSUM
09587     dev->features |= NETIF_F_IP_CSUM | NETIF_F_SG;
09588     vlan_features_add(dev, NETIF_F_IP_CSUM | NETIF_F_SG);
09589     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09590         dev->features |= NETIF_F_IPV6_CSUM;
09591         vlan_features_add(dev, NETIF_F_IPV6_CSUM);
09592     }
09593 #else
09594     dev->features |= NETIF_F_SG;
09595     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709)
09596         dev->features |= NETIF_F_HW_CSUM;
09597     else
09598         dev->features |= NETIF_F_IP_CSUM;
09599 #endif
09600 #ifdef BCM_VLAN
09601     dev->features |= NETIF_F_HW_VLAN_TX | NETIF_F_HW_VLAN_RX;
09602 #endif
09603 #ifdef BCM_TSO
09604     dev->features |= NETIF_F_TSO | NETIF_F_TSO_ECN;
09605     vlan_features_add(dev, NETIF_F_TSO | NETIF_F_TSO_ECN);
09606     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09607         dev->features |= NETIF_F_TSO6;
09608         vlan_features_add(dev, NETIF_F_TSO6);
09609     }
09610 #endif
09611 
09612 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09613     /*  If enabled register the NetQueue callbacks */
09614     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09615         bp->index = index;
09616         index++;
09617         if (BNX2_NETQUEUE_ENABLED(bp))
09618             VMKNETDDI_REGISTER_QUEUEOPS(dev, bnx2_netqueue_ops);
09619     }
09620 #endif
09621 
09622 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20418)
09623     if ((rc = register_netdev(dev))) {
09624         dev_err(&pdev->dev, "Cannot register net device\n");
09625         goto error;
09626     }
09627 #endif
09628     printk(KERN_INFO "%s: %s (%c%d) %s found at mem %lx, "
09629         "IRQ %d, node addr %s\n",
09630         dev->name,
09631         board_info[ent->driver_data].name,
09632         ((CHIP_ID(bp) & 0xf000) >> 12) + 'A',
09633         ((CHIP_ID(bp) & 0x0ff0) >> 4),
09634         bnx2_bus_string(bp, str),
09635         dev->base_addr,
09636         bp->pdev->irq, print_mac(mac, dev->dev_addr));
09637 
09638 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09639     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09640         if (BNX2_NETQUEUE_ENABLED(bp)) {
09641             printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue Ops registered [%d]\n",
09642                      dev->name, bp->index);
09643         } else
09644             printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue Ops not registered "
09645                      "[%d]\n",
09646                      dev->name, bp->index);
09647     }
09648 #endif
09649 
09650     return 0;
09651 
09652 error:
09653     if (bp->regview)
09654         iounmap(bp->regview);
09655     pci_release_regions(pdev);
09656     pci_disable_device(pdev);
09657     pci_set_drvdata(pdev, NULL);
09658     free_netdev(dev);
09659     return rc;
09660 }
09661 
09662 static void __devexit
09663 bnx2_remove_one(struct pci_dev *pdev)
09664 {
09665     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09666     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09667 
09668 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20600)
09669     flush_scheduled_work();
09670 #endif
09671 
09672     unregister_netdev(dev);
09673 
09674     if (bp->regview)
09675         iounmap(bp->regview);
09676 
09677 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20418)
09678     free_netdev(dev);
09679 #else
09680     kfree(dev);
09681 #endif
09682     pci_release_regions(pdev);
09683     pci_disable_device(pdev);
09684     pci_set_drvdata(pdev, NULL);
09685 }
09686 
09687 static int
09688 bnx2_suspend(struct pci_dev *pdev, pm_message_t state)
09689 {
09690     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09691     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09692 
09693 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x2060b)
09694     /* PCI register 4 needs to be saved whether netif_running() or not.
09695      * MSI address and data need to be saved if using MSI and
09696      * netif_running().
09697      */
09698     pci_save_state(pdev);
09699 #endif
09700     if (!netif_running(dev))
09701         return 0;
09702 
09703 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x20600)
09704     flush_scheduled_work();
09705 #endif
09706     bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
09707     netif_device_detach(dev);
09708     del_timer_sync(&bp->timer);
09709     bnx2_shutdown_chip(bp);
09710     bnx2_free_skbs(bp);
09711 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x2060b)
09712     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, state);
09713 #else
09714     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, pci_choose_state(pdev, state));
09715 #endif
09716     return 0;
09717 }
09718 
09719 static int
09720 bnx2_resume(struct pci_dev *pdev)
09721 {
09722     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09723     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09724 
09725 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x2060b)
09726     pci_restore_state(pdev);
09727 #endif
09728     if (!netif_running(dev))
09729         return 0;
09730 
09731     bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
09732     netif_device_attach(dev);
09733     bnx2_init_nic(bp, 1);
09734     bnx2_netif_start(bp);
09735     return 0;
09736 }
09737 
09738 #if !defined(__VMKLNX__)
09739 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x020611)
09740 
09748 static pci_ers_result_t bnx2_io_error_detected(struct pci_dev *pdev,
09749                            pci_channel_state_t state)
09750 {
09751     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09752     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09753 
09754     rtnl_lock();
09755     netif_device_detach(dev);
09756 
09757     if (state == pci_channel_io_perm_failure) {
09758         rtnl_unlock();
09759         return PCI_ERS_RESULT_DISCONNECT;
09760     }
09761 
09762     if (netif_running(dev)) {
09763         bnx2_netif_stop(bp);
09764         del_timer_sync(&bp->timer);
09765         bnx2_reset_nic(bp, BNX2_DRV_MSG_CODE_RESET);
09766     }
09767 
09768     pci_disable_device(pdev);
09769     rtnl_unlock();
09770 
09771     /* Request a slot slot reset. */
09772     return PCI_ERS_RESULT_NEED_RESET;
09773 }
09774 
09781 static pci_ers_result_t bnx2_io_slot_reset(struct pci_dev *pdev)
09782 {
09783     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09784     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09785 
09786     rtnl_lock();
09787     if (pci_enable_device(pdev)) {
09788         dev_err(&pdev->dev,
09789             "Cannot re-enable PCI device after reset.\n");
09790         rtnl_unlock();
09791         return PCI_ERS_RESULT_DISCONNECT;
09792     }
09793     pci_set_master(pdev);
09794     pci_restore_state(pdev);
09795     pci_save_state(pdev);
09796 
09797     if (netif_running(dev)) {
09798         bnx2_set_power_state(bp, PCI_D0);
09799         bnx2_init_nic(bp, 1);
09800     }
09801 
09802     rtnl_unlock();
09803     return PCI_ERS_RESULT_RECOVERED;
09804 }
09805 
09813 static void bnx2_io_resume(struct pci_dev *pdev)
09814 {
09815     struct net_device *dev = pci_get_drvdata(pdev);
09816     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(dev);
09817 
09818     rtnl_lock();
09819     if (netif_running(dev))
09820         bnx2_netif_start(bp);
09821 
09822     netif_device_attach(dev);
09823     rtnl_unlock();
09824 }
09825 
09826 static struct pci_error_handlers bnx2_err_handler = {
09827     .error_detected = bnx2_io_error_detected,
09828     .slot_reset = bnx2_io_slot_reset,
09829     .resume     = bnx2_io_resume,
09830 };
09831 
09832 #endif
09833 #endif

09835 static struct pci_driver bnx2_pci_driver = {
09836     .name       = DRV_MODULE_NAME,
09837     .id_table   = bnx2_pci_tbl,
09838     .probe      = bnx2_init_one,
09839     .remove     = __devexit_p(bnx2_remove_one),
09840     .suspend    = bnx2_suspend,
09841     .resume     = bnx2_resume,
09842 #if !defined(__VMKLNX__)
09843 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE >= 0x020611)
09844     .err_handler    = &bnx2_err_handler,
09845 #endif
09846 #endif
09847 };
09848 
09849 static int __init bnx2_init(void)
09850 {
09851     int rc = 0;
09852 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09853     int i;
09854 
09855     /*  sanity check the force_netq parameter */
09856     for (i = 0; i < BNX2_MAX_NIC; i++) {
09857         if((force_netq_param[i] < BNX2_OPTION_UNSET) ||
09858            (force_netq_param[i] > 7)) {
09859             printk(KERN_ERR "bnx2x: please use a 'force_netq' "
09860                     "value between (-1 to 7), "
09861                     "0 to disable NetQueue, "
09862                     "-1 to use the default value "
09863                     "failure at index %d val: %d\n",
09864                     i, force_netq_param[i]);
09865             rc = -EINVAL;
09866         }
09867     }
09868 
09869     if(rc != 0)
09870         return rc;
09871 #endif
09872 
09873 #if (LINUX_VERSION_CODE < 0x020613)
09874     rc = pci_module_init(&bnx2_pci_driver);
09875 #else
09876     rc = pci_register_driver(&bnx2_pci_driver);
09877 #endif
09878     return rc;
09879 }
09880 
09881 static void __exit bnx2_cleanup(void)
09882 {
09883     pci_unregister_driver(&bnx2_pci_driver);
09884 }
09885 
09886 module_init(bnx2_init);
09887 module_exit(bnx2_cleanup);
09888

09890 #if defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__)
09891 
09892 #ifdef BNX2_DEBUG
09893 static u32 bnx2_read_ctx(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 offset)
09894 {
09895     int i;
09896 
09897     if (CHIP_NUM(bp) != CHIP_NUM_5709) {
09898         REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_DATA_ADR, offset);
09899         return REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_DATA);
09900     }
09901 
09902     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL, offset | BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL_READ_REQ);
09903     for (i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
09904         udelay(5);
09905         if (REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL) & BNX2_CTX_CTX_CTRL_READ_REQ)
09906             continue;
09907         break;
09908     }
09909 
09910     return REG_RD(bp, BNX2_CTX_CTX_DATA);
09911 }
09912 
09913 static void dump_ctx(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 cid)
09914 {
09915     u32 addr = cid * 128;
09916     int i;
09917 
09918     for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
09919         u32 val, val1, val2, val3;
09920 
09921         val  = bnx2_read_ctx(bp, addr);
09922         val1 = bnx2_read_ctx(bp, addr+4);
09923         val2 = bnx2_read_ctx(bp, addr+8);
09924         val3 = bnx2_read_ctx(bp, addr+0xc);
09925         printk(KERN_ALERT "ctx  %08x: %08x %08x %08x %08x\n",
09926             addr, val, val1, val2, val3);
09927         addr += 0x10;
09928     }
09929 }
09930 #endif
09931 
09932 #define BNX2_NETQ_WAIT_EVENT_TIMEOUT    msecs_to_jiffies(1000)
09933 
09934 #define L2_KWQ_PAGE_CNT    1
09935 #define L2_KCQ_PAGE_CNT    1
09936 
09937 #define L2_KWQE_CNT (BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kwqe))
09938 #define L2_KCQE_CNT (BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kcqe))
09939 #define MAX_L2_KWQE_CNT (L2_KWQE_CNT - 1)
09940 #define MAX_L2_KCQE_CNT (L2_KCQE_CNT - 1)
09941 
09942 #define MAX_L2_KWQ_IDX     ((L2_KWQ_PAGE_CNT * L2_KWQE_CNT) - 1)
09943 #define MAX_L2_KCQ_IDX     ((L2_KCQ_PAGE_CNT * L2_KCQE_CNT) - 1)
09944 
09945 #define L2_KWQ_PG(x) (((x) & ~MAX_L2_KWQE_CNT) >> (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 5))
09946 #define L2_KWQ_IDX(x) ((x) & MAX_L2_KWQE_CNT)
09947 
09948 #define L2_KCQ_PG(x) (((x) & ~MAX_L2_KCQE_CNT) >> (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 5))
09949 #define L2_KCQ_IDX(x) ((x) & MAX_L2_KCQE_CNT)
09950 
09951 /*
09952  *      krnlq_context definition
09953  */
09954 #define L2_KRNLQ_FLAGS          0x00000000
09955 #define L2_KRNLQ_SIZE           0x00000000
09956 #define L2_KRNLQ_TYPE           0x00000000
09957 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ       (0xf<<0)
09958 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_256       (0<<0)
09959 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_512       (1<<0)
09960 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_1K        (2<<0)
09961 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_2K        (3<<0)
09962 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_4K        (4<<0)
09963 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_8K        (5<<0)

09965 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_32K       (7<<0)
09966 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_64K       (8<<0)
09967 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_128K      (9<<0)
09968 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_256K      (10<<0)
09969 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_512K      (11<<0)
09970 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_1M        (12<<0)
09971 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_PG_SZ_2M        (13<<0)
09972 #define KRNLQ_FLAGS_QE_SELF_SEQ     (1<<15)
09973 #define KRNLQ_SIZE_TYPE_SIZE    ((((0x28 + 0x1f) & ~0x1f) / 0x20) << 16)
09974 #define KRNLQ_TYPE_TYPE         (0xf<<28)
09975 #define KRNLQ_TYPE_TYPE_EMPTY       (0<<28)
09976 #define KRNLQ_TYPE_TYPE_KRNLQ       (6<<28)
09977 
09978 #define L2_KRNLQ_HOST_QIDX              0x00000004
09979 #define L2_KRNLQ_HOST_FW_QIDX           0x00000008
09980 #define L2_KRNLQ_NX_QE_SELF_SEQ         0x0000000c
09981 #define L2_KRNLQ_QE_SELF_SEQ_MAX        0x0000000c
09982 #define L2_KRNLQ_NX_QE_HADDR_HI         0x00000010
09983 #define L2_KRNLQ_NX_QE_HADDR_LO         0x00000014
09984 #define L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_PGIDX            0x00000018

09986 #define L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_NPAGES           0x0000001c
09987 #define L2_KRNLQ_QIDX_INCR              0x0000001c
09988 #define L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_HADDR_HI         0x00000020

09993 static int
09994 bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue_update(struct net_device *netdev,
09995                    int index,
09996                    int update);

09998 static int
09999 bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(struct bnx2 *bp)
10000 {
10001     rmb();
10002 
10003     return ((BNX2_NETQUEUE_ENABLED(bp)) &&
10004         (bp->flags & BNX2_FLAG_USING_MSIX) &&
10005         (CHIP_NUM(bp) == CHIP_NUM_5709));
10006 }
10007 
10008 static inline u32
10009 bnx2_netqueue_kwq_avail(struct bnx2 *bp)
10010 {
10011     return MAX_L2_KWQ_IDX -
10012         ((bp->netq_kwq_prod_idx - bp->netq_kwq_con_idx) &
10013           MAX_L2_KWQ_IDX);
10014 }
10015 
10016 static int
10017 bnx2_netqueue_submit_kwqes(struct bnx2 *bp, struct l2_kwqe *wqes)
10018 {
10019     struct l2_kwqe *prod_qe;
10020     u16 prod, sw_prod;
10021 
10022     if (1 > bnx2_netqueue_kwq_avail(bp)) {
10023         printk(KERN_WARNING "%s: No kwq's available\n", bp->dev->name);
10024         return -EAGAIN;
10025     }
10026 
10027     prod = bp->netq_kwq_prod_idx;
10028     sw_prod = prod & MAX_L2_KWQ_IDX;
10029 
10030     prod_qe = &bp->netq_kwq[L2_KWQ_PG(sw_prod)][L2_KWQ_IDX(sw_prod)];
10031     memcpy(prod_qe, wqes, sizeof(struct l2_kwqe));
10032     prod++;
10033     sw_prod = prod & MAX_L2_KWQ_IDX;
10034 
10035     bp->netq_kwq_prod_idx = prod;
10036 
10037     barrier();
10038     REG_WR16(bp, bp->netq_kwq_io_addr, bp->netq_kwq_prod_idx);
10039     wmb();
10040     mmiowb();
10041 
10042     return 0;
10043 }
10044 
10045 static void
10046 bnx2_netqueue_free_dma(struct bnx2 *bp, struct netq_dma *dma)
10047 {
10048     int i;
10049 
10050     if (dma->pg_arr) {
10051         for (i = 0; i < dma->num_pages; i++) {
10052             if (dma->pg_arr[i]) {
10053                 pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, BCM_PAGE_SIZE,
10054                             dma->pg_arr[i],
10055                             dma->pg_map_arr[i]);
10056                 dma->pg_arr[i] = NULL;
10057             }
10058         }
10059     }
10060     if (dma->pgtbl) {
10061         pci_free_consistent(bp->pdev, dma->pgtbl_size,
10062                     dma->pgtbl, dma->pgtbl_map);
10063         dma->pgtbl = NULL;
10064     }
10065     kfree(dma->pg_arr);
10066     dma->pg_arr = NULL;
10067     dma->num_pages = 0;
10068 }
10069 
10070 static void
10071 bnx2_netqueue_free_resc(struct bnx2 *bp)
10072 {
10073     bnx2_netqueue_free_dma(bp, &bp->netq_kwq_info);
10074     bnx2_netqueue_free_dma(bp, &bp->netq_kcq_info);
10075 }
10076 
10077 static void
10078 bnx2_netqueue_setup_page_tbl(struct bnx2 *bp,
10079                  struct netq_dma *dma)
10080 {
10081     int i;
10082     u32 *page_table = dma->pgtbl;
10083 
10084     for (i = 0; i < dma->num_pages; i++) {
10085         /* Each entry needs to be in big endian format. */
10086         *page_table = (u32) ((u64) dma->pg_map_arr[i] >> 32);
10087         page_table++;
10088         *page_table = (u32) dma->pg_map_arr[i];
10089         page_table++;
10090     }
10091 }
10092 
10093 static int
10094 bnx2_netqueue_alloc_dma(struct bnx2 *bp, struct netq_dma *dma,
10095             int pages)
10096 {
10097     int i, size;
10098 
10099     size = pages * (sizeof(void *) + sizeof(dma_addr_t));
10100     dma->pg_arr = kzalloc(size, GFP_ATOMIC);
10101     if (dma->pg_arr == NULL) {
10102         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't alloc space for dma page array\n",
10103                bp->dev->name);
10104         return -ENOMEM;
10105     }
10106 
10107     dma->pg_map_arr = (dma_addr_t *) (dma->pg_arr + pages);
10108     dma->num_pages = pages;
10109 
10110     for (i = 0; i < pages; i++) {
10111         dma->pg_arr[i] = pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev,
10112                               BCM_PAGE_SIZE,
10113                               &dma->pg_map_arr[i]);
10114         if (dma->pg_arr[i] == NULL) {
10115             printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't alloc dma page\n",
10116                    bp->dev->name);
10117 
10118             goto error;
10119         }
10120     }
10121 
10122     dma->pgtbl_size = ((pages * 8) + BCM_PAGE_SIZE - 1) &
10123               ~(BCM_PAGE_SIZE - 1);
10124     dma->pgtbl = pci_alloc_consistent(bp->pdev, dma->pgtbl_size,
10125                       &dma->pgtbl_map);
10126     if (dma->pgtbl == NULL)
10127         goto error;
10128 
10129     bnx2_netqueue_setup_page_tbl(bp, dma);
10130 
10131     return 0;
10132 
10133 error:
10134     bnx2_netqueue_free_dma(bp, dma);
10135     return -ENOMEM;
10136 }
10137 
10138 static int
10139 bnx2_netqueue_alloc_resc(struct bnx2 *bp)
10140 {
10141     int ret;
10142 
10143     ret = bnx2_netqueue_alloc_dma(bp, &bp->netq_kwq_info,
10144                       L2_KWQ_PAGE_CNT);
10145     if (ret) {
10146         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't alloc space for kwq\n",
10147                bp->dev->name);
10148         goto error;
10149     }
10150     bp->netq_kwq = (struct l2_kwqe **) bp->netq_kwq_info.pg_arr;
10151 
10152     ret = bnx2_netqueue_alloc_dma(bp, &bp->netq_kcq_info,
10153                       L2_KCQ_PAGE_CNT);
10154     if (ret) {
10155         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't alloc space for kwq\n",
10156                bp->dev->name);
10157         goto error;
10158     }
10159     bp->netq_kcq = (struct l2_kcqe **) bp->netq_kcq_info.pg_arr;
10160 
10161     return 0;
10162 
10163 error:
10164     bnx2_netqueue_free_resc(bp);
10165     bp->netq_kwq = NULL;
10166     bp->netq_kcq = NULL;
10167 
10168     return ret;
10169 }
10170 
10171 static void
10172 bnx2_init_netqueue_context(struct bnx2 *bp, u32 cid)
10173 {
10174     u32 cid_addr;
10175     int i;
10176 
10177     cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(cid);
10178 
10179     for (i = 0; i < CTX_SIZE; i += 4)
10180         bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, cid_addr, i, 0);
10181 }
10182 
10183 static int
10184 bnx2_netqueue_get_kcqes(struct bnx2 *bp, u16 hw_prod, u16 *sw_prod)
10185 {
10186     u16 i, ri, last;
10187     struct l2_kcqe *kcqe;
10188     int kcqe_cnt = 0, last_cnt = 0;
10189 
10190     i = ri = last = *sw_prod;
10191     ri &= MAX_L2_KCQ_IDX;
10192 
10193     while ((i != hw_prod) && (kcqe_cnt < BNX2_NETQ_MAX_COMPLETED_KCQE)) {
10194         kcqe = &bp->netq_kcq[L2_KCQ_PG(ri)][L2_KCQ_IDX(ri)];
10195         bp->netq_completed_kcq[kcqe_cnt++] = kcqe;
10196         i = (i + 1);
10197         ri = i & MAX_L2_KCQ_IDX;
10198         if (likely(!(kcqe->flags & L2_KCQE_FLAGS_NEXT))) {
10199             last_cnt = kcqe_cnt;
10200             last = i;
10201         }
10202     }
10203 
10204     *sw_prod = last;
10205     return last_cnt;
10206 }
10207 
10208 
10209 static void
10210 bnx2_service_netq_kcqes(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi, int num_cqes)
10211 {
10212     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
10213     int i, j;
10214 
10215     i = 0;
10216     j = 1;
10217     while (num_cqes) {
10218         u32 kcqe_op_flag = bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->opcode;
10219         u32 kcqe_layer = bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->flags &
10220                  L2_KCQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK;
10221 
10222         printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: kcwe service [reserved: 0x%x, status: 0x%x, qid: 0x%x, qe_self_seq: 0x%x, opcode: 0x%x, flags: 0x%x]\n",
10223             bp->dev->name,
10224             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->reserved,
10225             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->status,
10226             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->qid,
10227             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->qe_self_seq,
10228             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->opcode,
10229             bp->netq_completed_kcq[i]->flags);
10230 
10231         while (j < num_cqes) {
10232             u32 next_op = bp->netq_completed_kcq[i + j]->opcode;
10233 
10234             if ((next_op & L2_KCQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK) != kcqe_layer)
10235                 break;
10236             j++;
10237         }
10238 
10239         if (kcqe_layer != L2_KCQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK_L2) {
10240             printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: Unknown type of KCQE(0x%x)\n",
10241                    bp->dev->name, kcqe_op_flag);
10242             goto end;
10243         }
10244 
10245         bp->netq_flags = kcqe_op_flag;
10246         wake_up(&bp->netq_wait);
10247         wmb();
10248 
10249 end:
10250         num_cqes -= j;
10251         i += j;
10252         j = 1;
10253     }
10254 
10255 
10256     return;
10257 }
10258 
10259 static void
10260 bnx2_netqueue_service_bnx2_msix(struct bnx2_napi *bnapi)
10261 {
10262     struct bnx2 *bp = bnapi->bp;
10263     struct status_block *status_blk = bp->bnx2_napi[0].status_blk.msi;
10264     u32 status_idx = status_blk->status_idx;
10265     u16 hw_prod, sw_prod;
10266     int kcqe_cnt;
10267 
10268     bp->netq_kwq_con_idx = status_blk->status_cmd_consumer_index;
10269 
10270     hw_prod = status_blk->status_completion_producer_index;
10271     sw_prod = bp->netq_kcq_prod_idx;
10272 
10273     /*  Ensure that there is a NetQ kcq avaliable */
10274     if (sw_prod == hw_prod)
10275         return;
10276 
10277     while (sw_prod != hw_prod) {
10278         kcqe_cnt = bnx2_netqueue_get_kcqes(bp, hw_prod, &sw_prod);
10279         if (kcqe_cnt == 0)
10280             goto done;
10281 
10282         bnx2_service_netq_kcqes(bnapi, kcqe_cnt);
10283 
10284         /* Tell compiler that status_blk fields can change. */
10285         barrier();
10286         if (status_idx != status_blk->status_idx) {
10287             status_idx = status_blk->status_idx;
10288             bp->netq_kwq_con_idx = status_blk->status_cmd_consumer_index;
10289             hw_prod = status_blk->status_completion_producer_index;
10290         } else
10291             break;
10292     }
10293 
10294     barrier();
10295 done:
10296     REG_WR16(bp, bp->netq_kcq_io_addr, sw_prod);
10297 
10298     bp->netq_kcq_prod_idx = sw_prod;
10299     bp->netq_last_status_idx = status_idx;
10300 }
10301 
10302 static int
10303 bnx2_netqueue_open_started(struct bnx2 *bp)
10304 {
10305     return (((bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED) ==
10306              BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED)  &&
10307         ((bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_HW_OPENED) ==
10308              BNX2_NETQ_HW_OPENED));
10309 }
10310 
10311 static void
10312 bnx2_stop_netqueue_hw(struct bnx2 *bp)
10313 {
10314     u32 val;
10315 
10316     /* Disable the CP and COM doorbells.  These two processors polls the
10317      * doorbell for a non zero value before running.  This must be done
10318      * after setting up the kernel queue contexts. This is for
10319      * KQW/KCQ #1. */
10320 
10321     val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_SCRATCH + 0x20);
10322     val &= ~KWQ1_READY;
10323     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_SCRATCH + 0x20, val);
10324 
10325     val = bnx2_reg_rd_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_SCRATCH + 0x20);
10326     val &= ~KCQ1_READY;
10327     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_SCRATCH + 0x20, val);
10328 
10329     barrier();
10330 
10331     bp->netq_state &= ~BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED;
10332     wmb();
10333 }
10334 
10335 static void
10336 bnx2_close_netqueue_hw(struct bnx2 *bp)
10337 {
10338     bnx2_stop_netqueue_hw(bp);
10339     bnx2_netqueue_free_resc(bp);
10340 
10341     bp->netq_state &= ~BNX2_NETQ_HW_OPENED;
10342     wmb();
10343 }
10344 
10345 static void
10346 bnx2_start_netqueue_hw(struct bnx2 *bp)
10347 {
10348 
10349     /* Set the CP and COM doorbells.  These two processors polls the
10350      * doorbell for a non zero value before running.  This must be done
10351      * after setting up the kernel queue contexts. This is for
10352      * KQW/KCQ 1. */
10353     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_CP_SCRATCH + 0x20, KWQ1_READY);
10354     bnx2_reg_wr_ind(bp, BNX2_COM_SCRATCH + 0x20, KCQ1_READY);
10355 
10356     bp->netq_state |= BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED;
10357     wmb();
10358 }
10359 
10360 static void
10361 bnx2_init_netqueue_hw(struct bnx2 *bp)
10362 {
10363     u32 val;
10364 
10365     /*  Initialize the bnx2 netqueue structures */
10366     init_waitqueue_head(&bp->netq_wait);
10367 
10368     val = REG_RD(bp, BNX2_MQ_CONFIG);
10369     val &= ~BNX2_MQ_CONFIG_KNL_BYP_BLK_SIZE;
10370     if (BCM_PAGE_BITS > 12)
10371         val |= (12 - 8)  << 4;
10372     else
10373         val |= (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8)  << 4;
10374 
10375     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_CONFIG, val);
10376 
10377     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COMP_PROD_TRIP, (2 << 16) | 8);
10378     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_COM_TICKS, (64 << 16) | 220);
10379     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_HC_CMD_TICKS, (64 << 16) | 220);
10380 
10381     bnx2_init_netqueue_context(bp, NETQUEUE_KWQ_CID);
10382     bnx2_init_netqueue_context(bp, NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID);
10383 
10384     bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KWQ_CID);
10385     bp->netq_kwq_io_addr  = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KWQ_CID) +
10386                 L2_KRNLQ_HOST_QIDX;
10387 
10388     bp->netq_kwq_prod_idx = 0;
10389     bp->netq_kwq_con_idx = 0;
10390 
10391     /* Initialize the kernel work queue context. */
10392     val = KRNLQ_TYPE_TYPE_KRNLQ | KRNLQ_SIZE_TYPE_SIZE |
10393           (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8) | KRNLQ_FLAGS_QE_SELF_SEQ;
10394     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_TYPE, val);
10395 
10396     val = (BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kwqe) - 1) << 16;
10397     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_QE_SELF_SEQ_MAX, val);
10398 
10399     val = ((BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kwqe)) << 16) | L2_KWQ_PAGE_CNT;
10400     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_NPAGES, val);
10401 
10402     val = (u32) ((u64) bp->netq_kwq_info.pgtbl_map >> 32);
10403     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_HADDR_HI, val);
10404 
10405     val = (u32) bp->netq_kwq_info.pgtbl_map;
10406     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kwq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_HADDR_LO, val);
10407 
10408     bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr = GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID);
10409     bp->netq_kcq_io_addr = MB_GET_CID_ADDR(NETQUEUE_KCQ_CID) +
10410                    L2_KRNLQ_HOST_QIDX;
10411     bp->netq_kcq_prod_idx = 0;
10412 
10413     /* Initialize the kernel complete queue context. */
10414     val = KRNLQ_TYPE_TYPE_KRNLQ | KRNLQ_SIZE_TYPE_SIZE |
10415           (BCM_PAGE_BITS - 8) | KRNLQ_FLAGS_QE_SELF_SEQ;
10416     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_TYPE, val);
10417 
10418     val = (BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kcqe) - 1) << 16;
10419     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_QE_SELF_SEQ_MAX, val);
10420 
10421     val = ((BCM_PAGE_SIZE / sizeof(struct l2_kcqe)) << 16)|L2_KCQ_PAGE_CNT;
10422     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_NPAGES, val);
10423 
10424     val = (u32) ((u64) bp->netq_kcq_info.pgtbl_map >> 32);
10425     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_HADDR_HI, val);
10426 
10427     val = (u32) bp->netq_kcq_info.pgtbl_map;
10428     bnx2_ctx_wr(bp, bp->netq_kcq_cid_addr, L2_KRNLQ_PGTBL_HADDR_LO, val);
10429 
10430     /* Enable Commnad Scheduler notification when we write to the
10431      * host producer index of the kernel contexts. */
10432     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_CMD_MASK1, 2);
10433 
10434     /* Enable Command Scheduler notification when we write to either
10435      * the Send Queue or Receive Queue producer indexes of the kernel
10436      * bypass contexts. */
10437     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_BYP_CMD_MASK1, 7);
10438     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_BYP_WRITE_MASK1, 7);
10439 
10440     /* Notify COM when the driver post an application buffer. */
10441     REG_WR(bp, BNX2_MQ_KNL_RX_V2P_MASK2, 0x2000);
10442 
10443     barrier();
10444 }
10445 
10446 static int
10447 bnx2_open_netqueue_hw(struct bnx2 *bp)
10448 {
10449     int err;
10450 
10451     err = bnx2_netqueue_alloc_resc(bp);
10452     if (err != 0) {
10453         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't allocate netq resources\n",
10454                bp->dev->name);
10455         return err;
10456     }
10457 
10458     bnx2_init_netqueue_hw(bp);
10459     bnx2_start_netqueue_hw(bp);
10460 
10461     bp->netq_state |= BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED;
10462     wmb();
10463 
10464     printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware support is enabled\n",
10465         bp->dev->name);
10466 
10467     return 0;
10468 }
10469 
10470 
10471 
10472 static int
10473 bnx2_netq_get_netqueue_features(vmknetddi_queueop_get_features_args_t *args)
10474 {
10475     args->features = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FEATURE_NONE;
10476     args->features |= VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FEATURE_RXQUEUES;
10477     args->features |= VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FEATURE_TXQUEUES;
10478     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10479 }
10480 
10481 static int
10482 bnx2_netq_get_queue_count(vmknetddi_queueop_get_queue_count_args_t *args)
10483 {
10484     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
10485 
10486     /* workaround for packets duplicated */
10487     if (bp->num_tx_rings + bp->num_rx_rings > 1)
10488         bp->netq_enabled = 1;
10489 
10490     if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_RX) {
10491         args->count = max_t(u16, bp->num_rx_rings - 1, 0);
10492 
10493         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Using %d RX NetQ rings\n",
10494                args->netdev->name, args->count);
10495 
10496         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10497     } else if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_TX) {
10498         args->count = max_t(u16, bp->num_tx_rings - 1, 0);
10499 
10500         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Using %d TX NetQ rings\n",
10501                args->netdev->name, args->count);
10502 
10503         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10504     } else {
10505         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Counting queue: invalid queue type\n",
10506                bp->dev->name);
10507         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10508     }
10509 }
10510 
10511 static int
10512 bnx2_netq_get_filter_count(vmknetddi_queueop_get_filter_count_args_t *args)
10513 {
10514     /* Only support 1 Mac filter per queue */
10515     args->count = 1;
10516     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10517 }
10518 
10519 static int
10520 bnx2_netq_alloc_rx_queue(struct bnx2 *bp,
10521              struct bnx2_napi *bnapi,
10522              int queue_id)
10523 {
10524     /* We need to count the default ring as part of the number of RX rings
10525        avaliable */
10526     if (bp->n_rx_queues_allocated >= (bp->num_rx_rings - 1))
10527         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10528 
10529     if((bp->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED) != BNX2_NETQ_HW_STARTED) {
10530         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10531                bp->dev->name);
10532         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10533     }
10534 
10535     if (!bnapi->rx_queue_allocated) {
10536         int rc;
10537         struct l2_kwqe_vm_alloc_rx_queue kwqe_alloc_rx;
10538 
10539         /*  Ensure that the NetQueue is freed */
10540         rc = bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue_update(bp->dev, queue_id, 1);
10541         if(rc == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR) {
10542             printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't clean/free RX "
10543                     "queue during RX alloc\n",
10544                    bp->dev->name);
10545 
10546             return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10547         }
10548 
10549         /*  Prepare the kwqe to be passed to the firmware */
10550         memset(&kwqe_alloc_rx, 0, sizeof(kwqe_alloc_rx));
10551 
10552         kwqe_alloc_rx.kwqe_flags  = KWQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK_L2;
10553         kwqe_alloc_rx.kwqe_opcode = L2_KWQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_ALLOC_RX_QUEUE;
10554         kwqe_alloc_rx.queue_type  = L2_NET_QUEUE;
10555         kwqe_alloc_rx.qid         = queue_id;
10556 
10557         rc = bnx2_netqueue_submit_kwqes(bp,
10558                     (struct l2_kwqe *)&kwqe_alloc_rx);
10559         if (rc != 0) {
10560             printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't submit alloc rx kwqe\n",
10561                    bp->dev->name);
10562             return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10563         }
10564 
10565         bp->netq_flags = 0;
10566         wmb();
10567         rc = wait_event_timeout(bp->netq_wait,
10568                     (bp->netq_flags &
10569                      L2_KCQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_ALLOC_RX_QUEUE),
10570                     BNX2_NETQ_WAIT_EVENT_TIMEOUT);
10571 
10572         if (rc != 0) {
10573             bnapi->rx_queue_allocated = TRUE;
10574 
10575             printk(KERN_INFO "%s: RX NetQ allocated on %d\n",
10576                    bp->dev->name, kwqe_alloc_rx.qid);
10577             return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10578         } else {
10579             printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Timeout RX NetQ allocate on %d\n",
10580                    bp->dev->name, kwqe_alloc_rx.qid);
10581 
10582             return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10583         }
10584     }
10585 
10586     printk(KERN_ERR "%s: No RX NetQueues already allocated!\n",
10587             bp->dev->name);
10588     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10589 }
10590 
10591 static int
10592 bnx2_netq_alloc_rx_queue_vmk(struct net_device *netdev,
10593                  vmknetddi_queueops_queueid_t *p_qid,
10594                  struct napi_struct **napi_p)
10595 {
10596     int i;
10597     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(netdev);
10598 
10599     /* We need to count the default ring as part of the number of RX rings
10600        avaliable */
10601     if (bp->n_rx_queues_allocated >= (bp->num_rx_rings - 1))
10602         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10603 
10604     for_each_nondefault_rx_queue(bp, i) {
10605         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
10606         if (!bnapi->rx_queue_allocated) {
10607             int queue_id = i - 1;
10608             int rc;
10609 
10610             rc = bnx2_netq_alloc_rx_queue(bp, bnapi, queue_id);
10611 
10612             if (rc == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK) {
10613                 bp->n_rx_queues_allocated++;
10614                 *p_qid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_RX_QUEUEID(queue_id);
10615                 *napi_p = &bnapi->napi;
10616 
10617                 return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10618             } else 
10619                 return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10620         }
10621     }
10622 
10623     printk(KERN_ERR "%s: No free RX NetQueues found!\n", bp->dev->name);
10624     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10625 }
10626 
10627 
10628 static int
10629 bnx2_netq_alloc_tx_queue(struct bnx2 *bp,
10630              struct bnx2_napi *bnapi,
10631              int queue_id)
10632 {
10633     if (bp->n_tx_queues_allocated >= (bp->num_tx_rings - 1))
10634         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10635 
10636     if (!bnapi->tx_queue_allocated) {
10637         bnapi->tx_queue_allocated = TRUE;
10638         bp->n_tx_queues_allocated++;
10639 
10640         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: TX NetQ allocated on %d\n",
10641                    bp->dev->name, queue_id);
10642         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10643     }
10644     printk(KERN_ERR "%s: tx queue already allocated!\n",
10645            bp->dev->name);
10646     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10647 }
10648 
10649 static int
10650 bnx2_netq_alloc_tx_queue_vmk(struct net_device *netdev,
10651                  vmknetddi_queueops_queueid_t *p_qid,
10652                  u16 *queue_mapping)
10653 {
10654     int i;
10655     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(netdev);
10656 
10657     if (bp->n_tx_queues_allocated >= (bp->num_tx_rings - 1))
10658         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10659 
10660     for_each_nondefault_tx_queue(bp, i) {
10661         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
10662         if (!bnapi->tx_queue_allocated) {
10663             int rc = bnx2_netq_alloc_tx_queue(bp, bnapi, i);
10664 
10665             *p_qid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_TX_QUEUEID(i);
10666             *queue_mapping = i;
10667 
10668             return rc;
10669         }
10670     }
10671 
10672     printk(KERN_ERR "%s: no free tx queues found!\n",
10673            bp->dev->name);
10674     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10675 }
10676 
10677 static int
10678 bnx2_netq_alloc_queue(vmknetddi_queueop_alloc_queue_args_t *args)
10679 {
10680     struct net_device *netdev = args->netdev;
10681     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(netdev);
10682 
10683     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
10684         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to alloc NetQueue on failed reset "
10685                 "device\n",
10686                netdev->name);
10687         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10688     }
10689 
10690     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
10691         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10692                bp->dev->name);
10693         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10694     }
10695 
10696     if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_TX) {
10697         return bnx2_netq_alloc_tx_queue_vmk(args->netdev,
10698                             &args->queueid,
10699                             &args->queue_mapping);
10700     } else if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_RX) {
10701         return bnx2_netq_alloc_rx_queue_vmk(args->netdev,
10702                             &args->queueid,
10703                             &args->napi);
10704     } else {
10705         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to alloc invalid queue type: %x\n",
10706                bp->dev->name, args->type);
10707         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10708     }
10709 }
10710 
10711 static int
10712 bnx2_netq_free_tx_queue(struct net_device *netdev,
10713                 vmknetddi_queueops_queueid_t qid)
10714 {
10715     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(netdev);
10716     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
10717 
10718     u16 index = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(qid);
10719     if (index > bp->num_tx_rings)
10720         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10721 
10722     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[index];
10723     if (bnapi->tx_queue_allocated != TRUE)
10724         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10725 
10726     bnapi->tx_queue_allocated = FALSE;
10727     bp->n_tx_queues_allocated--;
10728 
10729     printk(KERN_INFO  "%s: Free NetQ TX Queue: %x\n",
10730            bp->dev->name, index);
10731 
10732     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10733 }
10734 
10735 static int
10736 bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue_update(struct net_device *netdev,
10737                    int index,
10738                    int force)
10739 {
10740     int rc;
10741     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(netdev);
10742     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
10743     struct l2_kwqe_vm_free_rx_queue kwqe_free_rx;
10744 
10745     if (index > bp->num_rx_rings) {
10746         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Error Free NetQ RX Queue: "
10747                  "index(%d) > bp->num_rx_rings(%d)\n",
10748                bp->dev->name, index, bp->num_rx_rings);
10749 
10750         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10751     }
10752 
10753     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
10754         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10755                bp->dev->name);
10756         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10757     }
10758 
10759     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[index];
10760     if ((bnapi->rx_queue_allocated != TRUE) && (force == 0)) {
10761         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Error Free NetQ RX Queue %d "
10762                  "already freed\n",
10763                bp->dev->name, index);
10764 
10765         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10766     }
10767 
10768     memset(&kwqe_free_rx, 0, sizeof(kwqe_free_rx));
10769 
10770     kwqe_free_rx.flags  = KWQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK_L2;
10771     kwqe_free_rx.opcode = L2_KWQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_FREE_RX_QUEUE;
10772     kwqe_free_rx.qid    = index;
10773 
10774     rc = bnx2_netqueue_submit_kwqes(bp,
10775                     (struct l2_kwqe *) &kwqe_free_rx);
10776     if (rc != 0) {
10777         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Couldn't submit free rx kwqe\n",
10778                bp->dev->name);
10779 
10780         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10781     }
10782 
10783     bp->netq_flags = 0;
10784     wmb();
10785     rc = wait_event_timeout(bp->netq_wait,
10786                 (bp->netq_flags &
10787                 L2_KCQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_FREE_RX_QUEUE),
10788                 BNX2_NETQ_WAIT_EVENT_TIMEOUT);
10789     if (rc != 0) {
10790         bnapi->rx_queue_allocated = FALSE;
10791 
10792         if(force != 1)
10793             bp->n_rx_queues_allocated--;
10794 
10795         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Free NetQ RX Queue (forced: %d): %x\n",
10796                bp->dev->name, force, index);
10797 
10798         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10799     } else {
10800         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Timeout free NetQ RX Queue "
10801                  "(force: %d): %x\n",
10802                bp->dev->name, force, index);
10803 
10804         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10805     }
10806 }
10807 
10808 static int
10809 bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue(struct net_device *netdev,
10810             vmknetddi_queueops_queueid_t qid)
10811 {
10812     return bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue_update(netdev,
10813                       VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(qid), 0);
10814 }
10815 
10816 static int
10817 bnx2_netq_free_queue(vmknetddi_queueop_free_queue_args_t *args)
10818 {
10819     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
10820 
10821     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
10822         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to free NetQueue on failed reset "
10823                 "device\n",
10824                args->netdev->name);
10825         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10826     }
10827 
10828     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
10829         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10830                bp->dev->name);
10831         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10832     }
10833 
10834     if (VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_IS_TX_QUEUEID(args->queueid)) {
10835         return bnx2_netq_free_tx_queue(args->netdev, args->queueid);
10836     } else if (VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_IS_RX_QUEUEID(args->queueid)) {
10837         return bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue(args->netdev, args->queueid);
10838     } else {
10839         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: free netq: invalid queue type\n",
10840                args->netdev->name);
10841         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10842     }
10843 }
10844 
10845 static int
10846 bnx2_netq_get_queue_vector(vmknetddi_queueop_get_queue_vector_args_t *args)
10847 {
10848     int qid;
10849     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
10850     qid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(args->queueid);
10851     if (qid > bp->num_rx_rings)
10852         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10853 
10854 #ifdef CONFIG_PCI_MSI
10855     args->vector = bp->bnx2_napi[qid].int_num;
10856 #endif
10857     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10858 }
10859 
10860 static int
10861 bnx2_netq_get_default_queue(vmknetddi_queueop_get_default_queue_args_t *args)
10862 {
10863     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
10864 
10865     if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_RX) {
10866         args->queueid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_RX_QUEUEID(0);
10867         args->napi = &bp->bnx2_napi[0].napi;
10868         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10869     } else if (args->type == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUE_TYPE_TX) {
10870         args->queueid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_TX_QUEUEID(0);
10871         args->queue_mapping = 0;
10872         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10873     } else
10874         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10875 }
10876 
10877 static int
10878 bnx2_netq_remove_rx_filter(struct bnx2 *bp, int qid)
10879 {
10880     u16 fw_qid = qid;
10881     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
10882     struct l2_kwqe_vm_remove_rx_filter kwqe_remove_rx_filter;
10883     int rc;
10884 
10885     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
10886         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to remove RX filter NetQueue on "
10887                 "failed reset device\n",
10888                bp->dev->name);
10889         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10890     }
10891 
10892     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
10893         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10894                bp->dev->name);
10895         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10896     }
10897 
10898     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[qid + 1];
10899 
10900     if (qid > bp->num_rx_rings) {
10901         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Free RX Filter NetQ: failed "
10902                  "qid(%d) > bp->num_rx_rings(%d)\n",
10903                bp->dev->name, qid, bp->num_rx_rings);
10904         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10905     }
10906 
10907     memset(&kwqe_remove_rx_filter, 0, sizeof(kwqe_remove_rx_filter));
10908 
10909     kwqe_remove_rx_filter.flags     = KWQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK_L2;
10910     kwqe_remove_rx_filter.opcode        = L2_KWQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_REMOVE_RX_FILTER;
10911     kwqe_remove_rx_filter.filter_type   = L2_VM_FILTER_MAC;
10912     kwqe_remove_rx_filter.qid       = fw_qid;
10913 
10914     rc = bnx2_netqueue_submit_kwqes(bp,
10915                     (struct l2_kwqe *) &kwqe_remove_rx_filter);
10916     if (rc != 0) {
10917         printk(KERN_ERR "Couldn't submit rx filter kwqe\n");
10918         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10919     }
10920 
10921     bp->netq_flags = 0;
10922     wmb();
10923     rc = wait_event_timeout(bp->netq_wait,
10924                 (bp->netq_flags &
10925                  L2_KCQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_REMOVE_RX_FILTER),
10926                 BNX2_NETQ_WAIT_EVENT_TIMEOUT);
10927     if (rc != 0) {
10928         bnapi->rx_queue_active = FALSE;
10929         bnapi->netq_state &= ~BNX2_NETQ_RX_FILTER_APPLIED;
10930 
10931         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQ remove RX filter: %d\n",
10932                bp->dev->name, qid);
10933 
10934         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
10935     } else {
10936         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Timeout NetQ remove RX filter: %d\n",
10937                bp->dev->name, qid);
10938 
10939         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10940     }
10941 }
10942 
10943 static int
10944 bnx2_netq_remove_rx_filter_vmk(vmknetddi_queueop_remove_rx_filter_args_t *args)
10945 {
10946     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
10947     u16 qid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(args->queueid);
10948     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
10949 
10950     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
10951         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to remove RX filter NetQueue on "
10952                 "failed reset device\n",
10953                args->netdev->name);
10954         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10955     }
10956 
10957     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
10958         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
10959                bp->dev->name);
10960         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10961     }
10962 
10963     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[qid + 1];
10964 
10965     if (!VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_IS_RX_QUEUEID(args->queueid)) {
10966         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: !VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_IS_RX_QUEUEID: "
10967                  "qid: %d)\n",
10968                bp->dev->name, qid);
10969         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10970     }
10971 
10972     if (qid > bp->num_rx_rings) {
10973         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: qid(%d) > bp->num_rx_rings(%d)\n",
10974                bp->dev->name, qid, bp->num_rx_rings);
10975         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10976     }
10977 
10978     /* Only support one Mac filter per queue */
10979     if (bnapi->rx_queue_active == 0) {
10980         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: bnapi->rx_queue_active(%d) == 0\n",
10981                bp->dev->name, bnapi->rx_queue_active);
10982         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
10983     }
10984 
10985     return bnx2_netq_remove_rx_filter(bp, qid);
10986 }
10987 
10988 
10989 static int
10990 bnx2_netq_apply_rx_filter(struct bnx2 *bp, struct bnx2_napi *bnapi,
10991               int queueid)
10992 {
10993     u16 fw_queueid = queueid;
10994     struct l2_kwqe_vm_set_rx_filter kwqe_set_rx_filter;
10995     int rc;
10996     DECLARE_MAC_BUF(mac);
10997 
10998     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
10999         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to apply RX filter NetQueue on "
11000                 "failed reset device\n",
11001                bp->dev->name);
11002         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11003     }
11004 
11005     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
11006         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
11007                bp->dev->name);
11008         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11009     }
11010 
11011     if (bnapi->rx_queue_active == TRUE || !bnapi->rx_queue_allocated) {
11012         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: apply filter: RX NetQ %d already active"
11013                 "bnapi->rx_queue_active(%d) || "
11014                 "!bnapi->rx_queue_allocated(%d)\n",
11015                bp->dev->name, queueid, bnapi->rx_queue_active, 
11016                bnapi->rx_queue_allocated);
11017         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11018     }
11019 
11020     bnx2_set_mac_addr(bp, bnapi->mac_filter_addr,
11021               fw_queueid + QID_TO_PM_OFFSET);
11022 
11023 
11024     memset(&kwqe_set_rx_filter, 0, sizeof(&kwqe_set_rx_filter));
11025 
11026     kwqe_set_rx_filter.flags    = KWQE_FLAGS_LAYER_MASK_L2;
11027     kwqe_set_rx_filter.opcode   = L2_KWQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_SET_RX_FILTER;
11028 
11029 #if defined(__LITTLE_ENDIAN)
11030     memcpy(&kwqe_set_rx_filter.mac_addr_hi, bnapi->mac_filter_addr, 2);
11031     memcpy(&kwqe_set_rx_filter.mac_addr_lo, bnapi->mac_filter_addr + 2, 4);
11032 #else
11033     memcpy(&kwqe_set_rx_filter.mac_addr, bnapi->mac_filter_addr, 6);
11034 #endif
11035 
11036     if (bnapi->class == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FILTER_MACADDR) {
11037         kwqe_set_rx_filter.filter_type  = L2_VM_FILTER_MAC;
11038     } else {
11039         kwqe_set_rx_filter.filter_type  = L2_VM_FILTER_MAC_VLAN;
11040         kwqe_set_rx_filter.vlan     = bnapi->vlan_id;
11041     }
11042     kwqe_set_rx_filter.qid      = fw_queueid;
11043 
11044     rc = bnx2_netqueue_submit_kwqes(bp,
11045                     (struct l2_kwqe *) &kwqe_set_rx_filter);
11046     if (rc != 0) {
11047         printk(KERN_ERR "Couldn't submit rx filter kwqe\n");
11048         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11049     }
11050 
11051     bp->netq_flags = 0;
11052     wmb();
11053     rc = wait_event_timeout(bp->netq_wait,
11054                 (bp->netq_flags &
11055                  L2_KCQE_OPCODE_VALUE_VM_SET_RX_FILTER),
11056                 BNX2_NETQ_WAIT_EVENT_TIMEOUT);
11057 
11058     if (rc != 0) {
11059         bnapi->rx_queue_active = TRUE;
11060         bnapi->netq_state |= BNX2_NETQ_RX_FILTER_APPLIED;
11061 
11062         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQ set RX Filter: %d [%s %d]\n",
11063                bp->dev->name,
11064                queueid, print_mac(mac, bnapi->mac_filter_addr),
11065                bnapi->vlan_id);
11066 
11067         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
11068     } else {
11069         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: Timeout submitting NetQ set RX Filter: %d [%s]\n",
11070                bp->dev->name, queueid,
11071                print_mac(mac, bnapi->mac_filter_addr));
11072 
11073         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11074     }
11075 }
11076 
11077 static int
11078 bnx2_netq_apply_rx_filter_vmk(vmknetddi_queueop_apply_rx_filter_args_t *args)
11079 {
11080     u8 *macaddr;
11081     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
11082     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
11083     u16 queueid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(args->queueid);
11084     vmknetddi_queueops_filter_class_t class;
11085     DECLARE_MAC_BUF(mac);
11086 
11087     if(bp->reset_failed == 1) {
11088         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: Trying to apply RX filter NetQueue on "
11089                 "failed reset device\n",
11090                args->netdev->name);
11091         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11092     }
11093 
11094     if(bnx2_netqueue_open_started(bp)) {
11095         printk(KERN_INFO "%s: NetQueue hardware not running yet\n",
11096                bp->dev->name);
11097         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11098     }
11099 
11100     if (!VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_IS_RX_QUEUEID(args->queueid)) {
11101         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: invalid NetQ RX ID: %x\n",
11102                args->netdev->name, args->queueid);
11103         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11104     }
11105 
11106     class = vmknetddi_queueops_get_filter_class(&args->filter);
11107     if ((class != VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FILTER_MACADDR) &&
11108         (class != VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_FILTER_VLANMACADDR)) {
11109         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: recieved invalid RX NetQ filter: %x\n",
11110                args->netdev->name, class);
11111         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11112     }
11113     if (queueid > bp->num_rx_rings) {
11114         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: applying filter with invalid RX NetQ %d ID\n",
11115                args->netdev->name, queueid);
11116         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11117     }
11118 
11119     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[queueid + 1];
11120 
11121     if (bnapi->rx_queue_active || !bnapi->rx_queue_allocated) {
11122         printk(KERN_ERR "%s: RX NetQ %d already active\n",
11123                args->netdev->name, queueid);
11124         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11125     }
11126 
11127     macaddr = (void *)vmknetddi_queueops_get_filter_macaddr(&args->filter);
11128     memcpy(bnapi->mac_filter_addr, macaddr, ETH_ALEN);
11129     bnapi->vlan_id = vmknetddi_queueops_get_filter_vlanid(&args->filter);
11130     bnapi->class = class;
11131 
11132     /*  Apply RX filter code here */
11133     args->filterid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_MK_FILTERID(queueid);
11134 
11135     return bnx2_netq_apply_rx_filter(bp, bnapi, queueid);
11136 }
11137 
11138 static int
11139 bnx2_netq_get_queue_stats(vmknetddi_queueop_get_stats_args_t *args)
11140 {
11141     u16 queueid = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_QUEUEID_VAL(args->queueid);
11142     struct bnx2_napi *bnapi;
11143     struct bnx2 *bp = netdev_priv(args->netdev);
11144 
11145     bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[queueid];
11146 
11147     args->stats = &bnapi->stats;
11148 
11149     return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK;
11150 }

11152 static int
11153 bnx2_netq_get_netqueue_version(vmknetddi_queueop_get_version_args_t *args)
11154 {
11155     return vmknetddi_queueops_version(args);
11156 }
11157 
11158 static void
11159 bnx2_netqueue_flush_all(struct bnx2 *bp)
11160 {
11161     int i;
11162     u16 num_tx = 0, num_rx = 0;
11163 
11164     printk(KERN_INFO PFX "%s: Flushing NetQueues\n", bp->dev->name);
11165 
11166     for_each_nondefault_rx_queue(bp, i) {
11167         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
11168 
11169         if(bnapi->netq_state & BNX2_NETQ_RX_FILTER_APPLIED) {
11170             int rc = bnx2_netq_remove_rx_filter(bp, i);
11171             if (rc == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR) {
11172                 printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: could not remove RX "
11173                             "filter during flush\n",
11174                        bp->dev->name);
11175             }
11176 
11177             if(bnapi->rx_queue_allocated == TRUE) {
11178                 rc = bnx2_netq_free_rx_queue_update(bp->dev,
11179                                     i, 1);
11180                 if (rc == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OK) {
11181                     num_rx++;
11182                 } else {
11183                     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: could "
11184                             "not free RX "
11185                             "queue during flush\n",
11186                             bp->dev->name);
11187                 }
11188             }
11189         }
11190     }
11191 
11192     for_each_nondefault_tx_queue(bp, i) {
11193         struct bnx2_napi *bnapi = &bp->bnx2_napi[i];
11194 
11195         if(bnapi->tx_queue_allocated == TRUE) {
11196             bnx2_netq_free_tx_queue(bp->dev, i);
11197         }
11198 
11199         num_tx++;
11200     }
11201 
11202     printk(KERN_ERR PFX "%s: finished saving NetQueues: rx: %d tx: %d\n",
11203         bp->dev->name, num_rx, num_tx);
11204 }
11205 
11206 
11207 static int
11208 bnx2_netqueue_ops(vmknetddi_queueops_op_t op, void *args)
11209 {
11210     int rc;
11211     struct bnx2 *bp;
11212 
11213     if (op == VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_VERSION)
11214          return bnx2_netq_get_netqueue_version(
11215             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_version_args_t *)args);
11216 
11217     bp = netdev_priv(((vmknetddi_queueop_get_features_args_t *)args)->netdev);
11218 
11219     if (!bnx2_netqueue_is_avail(bp))
11220         return VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11221 
11222 
11223     switch (op) {
11224     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_FEATURES:
11225         rc = bnx2_netq_get_netqueue_features(
11226             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_features_args_t *)args);
11227         break;
11228 
11229     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_QUEUE_COUNT:
11230         rc = bnx2_netq_get_queue_count(
11231             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_queue_count_args_t *)args);
11232         break;
11233 
11234     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_FILTER_COUNT:
11235         rc = bnx2_netq_get_filter_count(
11236             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_filter_count_args_t *)args);
11237         break;
11238 
11239     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_ALLOC_QUEUE:
11240         rc = bnx2_netq_alloc_queue(
11241             (vmknetddi_queueop_alloc_queue_args_t *)args);
11242         break;
11243 
11244     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_FREE_QUEUE:
11245         rc = bnx2_netq_free_queue(
11246             (vmknetddi_queueop_free_queue_args_t *)args);
11247         break;
11248 
11249     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_QUEUE_VECTOR:
11250         rc = bnx2_netq_get_queue_vector(
11251             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_queue_vector_args_t *)args);
11252         break;
11253 
11254     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_DEFAULT_QUEUE:
11255         rc = bnx2_netq_get_default_queue(
11256             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_default_queue_args_t *)args);
11257         break;
11258 
11259     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_APPLY_RX_FILTER:
11260         rc = bnx2_netq_apply_rx_filter_vmk(
11261             (vmknetddi_queueop_apply_rx_filter_args_t *)args);
11262         break;
11263 
11264     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_REMOVE_RX_FILTER:
11265         rc = bnx2_netq_remove_rx_filter_vmk(
11266             (vmknetddi_queueop_remove_rx_filter_args_t *)args);
11267         break;
11268 
11269     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_GET_STATS:
11270         rc = bnx2_netq_get_queue_stats(
11271             (vmknetddi_queueop_get_stats_args_t *)args);
11272         break;
11273 
11274     /*  Unsupported for now */
11275     case VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_OP_SET_TX_PRIORITY:
11276         rc = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11277         break;
11278 
11279     default:
11280         printk(KERN_WARNING "Unhandled NETQUEUE OP %d\n", op);
11281         rc = VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS_ERR;
11282     }
11283 
11284     return rc;
11285 }
11286 #endif /* defined(__VMKLNX__) && defined(__VMKNETDDI_QUEUEOPS__) */
